ſcrypture ye alleged god ordeyned ſtate innocencye man kyndely haue ſoueraynte ouer beſtes fyſhes byrdes maner lordſhypp ordeyned waye kynde may iuſte man haue without habondaunce worldely richeſſe ſeculer cyuyle lordſhyppe introducte occaſyon ſynne perteyneth worldely richeſſe whiche maner lordſhyp longeth kynges duke erles lower lordes yf poore wretche ſholde beſye gete ſuche lordſhyp holy ſcrypture ne holy doctours wote well prayſynge gete none dominiū lordſhyp pretendeth haue tyraūtes fals oppreſſours ouer people whiche maner lordſhyp god forbede euer deſyre syr yf ye marke well acciere ac • xx ſayth blyſfull gyue take riche man may better gyue may poore hath wherof ergo blyſfull riche poore yt wyll beſye hȳ haue better parte fole ergo nūc tibi concludi • thou arte concluded ¶pauper cryſte ſayth may falſe ye riche men take full moche gyue oftentyme full lytyll loue god ¶ye take grete gyue ſmalle ye take moche taketh y• poore ye take harder ye boū den harder rekenyng ye muſ • e gyue ſayth gregorye quanto dona creſcunt tanto creſcunt raciones donorum gyftes encreaſe encreaſe rekenynges gyftes ſaynt poule ſayth riche man quid habes qd nō accepiſti haſt thou thou haſt receyued god right ſynne ye riche men ben takyng ſyde lytyll yeuyng ſyde poore man taketh lytyll gyueth full moche one peny gyuen poore man goddes ſyght caſe twenty pounde gyuen riche therfore cryſte ſayth goſpell luce xxi poore wydowe whiche offred two mytes temple one ferthynge ſhe offred dyde men wȳmen daye yet full grete offryng cryſte ſayth ſhe offred ſhe hadde lyue men myght gaaf ſo grete gyfte bycauſe good wyll man forſaketh worlde gyueth awaye hath loue god alſo forſaketh therwith couetyſe hauynge ſaue oonly hym bare nedeth bycauſe ſoo dyſcarged hym worldely beſyneſſe thou ¶pauper expoſytoures wordes cryſte ſaye iheruſalem lytyll pryue yate whiche ſtraytneſſe called nedell whan cameles came ycharged yate myght entre dyde awaye theyr burdeynes theyr packes ſo theſe wordes cryſte excludeth riche men heuen techeth ye may entre yates heuen ſayth goſpell yate waye ledeth lyfe blyſſe full ſtrayte fewe paſſe therby ſoo nedell vnderſtonde entrynge heuens blyſſe camele charged y• riche men ben charged richeſſe worlde whiche charge longe faſte vpon theym soo longe may entre blyſſe heuen cryſte ſayth goſpell niſi quis renunciauerit omnibus que poſſidet non poteſt meus pacyence thou reherſeſt wordes salomon prayer falſe englyſſhe conuenyent ſayd gyue neyther richeſſe ne beggerye thou ſaydeſte ſayd gyue rycheſſe beggerye ſaye gyue richeſſe nygardſhyppe ſtraytneſſe herte couetyſe whiche make riche man alwaye begge craue ſayd eccleſiaſtes v ca nygarde hath neuer ynough ſoo theſe wordes prayeth god yf gyue hym richeſſe ſholde gyue hym therwith largeneſſe herte grace ſpende goddes worſhyppe haue good good lyfe ſayth eccleſiaſtes vi grete myſchyue grete vanyte god gyueth man richeſſe goodes ynoughe wyll haue gyueth hym power nygardſhyp haue parte therof lyfe reaſon ſaynt marke preſented lykeneſſe lyon ſpake openly cryſtus reſurreccōn therfore goſpell rede eſterdaye alſo yu ſhalt vnderſtande cryſte god man preeſt kyng mathewe ſpake mooſt openly māhode began manhode therfore paynted lykeneſſe man saynt iohn̄ ſpake mooſt god hode began atte godhode therfore paynted lykenes egle ſayd fyrſte saynt luke ſpake mooſt preeſthode therfore paynted ¶pauper tyme lente betokeneth tyme adam ſynne whiche loſt ſyght goddes face god courte heuen hyd theyr face mankynde vnto tyme cryſtus paſſyon token therof dn̄ica ſeptuageſima whan holy chirche conſeyll ony ¶diues may knowe ony ſuche thynges halfe ¶pauper somtyme boke prophecye ſomtyme coniecture dyuerſe cauſes dyſpoſycōns gone byfore yf man gyue hym wycked companye vſe ſuſpecte place men wote wyll coniecte therof ſaye tyme comynge ſhall confuſyon alſo yf man mys dyete hym ete drynke meſure thynge conuenyent hym men wyll ſaye ſhalbe ſeke therof yf man gyue hym falſe kynges ſeale y• kynges moneye wyll ſaye ſhall hanged drawen comonly falleth ſo alſo knowe thynges ben come coniectyng dyuerſe tale ſpeche people yf comon clamoure people ayenſt theyr kynge whan theyr kyng truſteth vpon token people ſhal vndo hȳ ware maner ſe dayes mooſt parte people ben prophetes telle thynges ben come whiche thynges ben perfourme herte worde dede childern alſo theyr elder ſpeke ben haue ben ꝓphetes nygh euery hous alſo knowe ſuche thynges dyſcoueryng coūſeyl knowyng coū ſeyll purpoſe ſuche thynges ſomtyme ſame coūſeyll aſſente helpynge therto maner theſe faytours ben called ſothe ſayers aſtronomers ſomtyme tell thynges preuy doo come ayen thynges ben ſtolen loſte comonly ſuche ben theues theyr aſſent one ſothe ſawe tweyne whiche knowe maner blynde nyce people make byleue theyr leſynges therfor yf ony ſuche faytours dyde ony thyng come ayen ſtolen ſholde taken theef theues feere comonly ſuche faytours iapers haue mayſters haue parte theyr wynnynge tauerners brewer hoſtlers nedy werkeleſſe men go ſo gay ſpende grete whiche aſpye thynges ben done cō tree yet ben done telle faytours haue name ofte ſholde kepe mooſt counſeyll dyſcouer coū ſeyll ſo men yt wende coūſeyll coūſeyll comonly ſuche faytours ſlye ſpekers ſlyghly oppoſe ſheepherde plowman y• felde ſome olde ſymple folke childern townes ende axen ſtandeth amonge neyghbours contree telle theym make wyſe yf knewe aſtronomye prophecye nygromancye moche ben vnknowen telle ſothes men knowe people weneth knowe thynges myght knowe wolde ſo byleue tyll ben dyſceyued somtyme ſuche faytours telle ſothes theyr crafte techyng falſhode fende whiche alwaye redy yf god ſuffred hym ſeche foles dyſceyue caplm xxxi diues may deuyll knowe thynges ben come ony preuy ſynne ¶pauper better ony man ſaynt auſtyn ſayth de natura demonū xxviq̄iiij ſciendū fende ſotyll wytte ferther ſee caſte ony man alſo lyghter ſwftyer ſterynge paſſynge ten folde lyghter ony foule fleynge alſo may lyghtly knowe done dyuerſe contrees londes ſoo ſotyll kynde ther may dore neyther walle ſhytte hym coūſeyll ſoo may ſee men woman doo though full preuy alſo longe experyence haue lyued ſo longe telle caſte waye kynde many thynges come many thynges paſſe mannes wytte alſo oftymes haue leue god mānes ſynne wondres cauſe hydeous tempeſtes enfecte enuenym ayer cauſe morayne ſekeneſſe hongre drought dyſcenſyon warre deſtruccyon chary • e myſpryde couetyſe lechery wrathe enuye ſuche thynges done purſue haue done aforne made telle byfore alſo ſygnes bodye outwarde knowe dyſpoſycōn man woman inwarde ſygnes helthe ſekeneſſe vyce vertue ofte token outwarde knowe mānes thought inwarde moche may knowe certayne ſuche thynges god knoweth certayne thynges ben come oftyme god letteth theyr malyce whan y• men wyll amende theym therfore proude ſpyryte wyll telle ſuche thynges people ſodaynly hym ſelfe eaſely y• ſette theyr fayth theyr truſte hym ben wytches faytours aſtronomers yf theyr ſawes foūden fals ſhall haue velonye yf foūden true fende ſhall haue worſhyppe alſo may knowe thynges y• come boke prophecye whiche vnderſtande naturell wytte better ony man caplm xxxij diues sothe nygh euery ſynne neuer ſo preuy done techyng entyſyng fende therfore wonder ony lecherye thefte myſchyef murdre leſynges ſynnes may hydde kepte preuy ſythen fende knoweth ſo well may knowe thynges ben ſoo preuy ſoo many wayes thou haſte ſayd ¶pauper full fayne wolde fende dyſcouere mannes ſynne womannes brynge theym ſhame velonye ſoo deſtroye charyte make euery man ſlee god mercy letteth hym may nought ne telle hath graūt god therfore fynde goſpell math viij fende myght entre ſwyne wende beſydes drenche hem tylle graūte cryſte alſo myght dyſeaſe iob neyther bodye ne catell tyll hadde graūte god iob et ij coude dyſceyue kyng achab leſynges fayte byheſtes hym fyght myght lyue pea yet myght tyll hadde graunte god thyrde boke kynges xxij chapytre knoweth moche thynge ſuffraunce god may nought without graūte permyſſyon ſuffraūce god fende ſo feble ſo faynt may man ne woman ouercome temptacōn wyll ouercome hym ne may dere leſte childe waye haue graūte god whiche ſomtyme graūted power therto ſynne fader moder ¶diues ſuffreth god hym ſoo moche tempte mankynde ¶pauper manyfolde encreſynge blyſſe mede ſaynt poule ſayth ther noo man worthy haue crowne lyfe withſtande fende ghooſtly ſtryfe ſayth place god ſuffreth hym tempte v may well withſtande yf wyll yf falle hath ordeyned v remedye penaunce ſoone ryſe ayen better fyght yf wyll temptacyon ſhall tourne v mede yf wyll withſtande ¶diues sythen fende knoweth ſo many treuthes wote done euery wycked dede meruaylleth moche ſo redye lye ſo falſe ¶pauper hateth god ſouerayne treuthe myght euen god ſoueraynte treuthe ne haue name ſouerayne treuthe god therfore lykyng trauayll ſouerayne falſhede ſoueraynly falſe therfor cryſte ſayth goſpell fende ſtode neuer treuthe ther treuthe hym whan ſpeketh ſpeketh leſynges waye kynde lyer fader leſynges iohānes viij ſo whether tale true falſe ſaye ſothe falſe alwaye felſe alwaye lyer ¶diues may ſay treuthe yet lye yf ſayth treuthe thynketh lyeth ¶pauper ſoo euer man fende dooth ſpeketh ayenſt good conſcyence ayenſt pleaſaunce god wyll intencyon dyſceyue man woman childe leſynge lyer doth ſayth therfore lawe ſheweth well xxij q̄ ij hoy • autē yf man ſaye treuthe whiche treuthe wened falſe yf ſaye dyſceyue euen cryſten lyeth ſoo ſoth ſawe man ye fende may lye yf ſaye yt daye let thy iourney wenyng ſelfe daye though ſayd yet lye ſame maner fende telleth treuthis thynges ben come ſothes alſo wenynge hym ſelfe falſe ſo ſothe ſawes lyeth ſayth treu vnwyttyngly dyſceyte weneth ſaye falſe yf ſaye ony treuthe wyttyng wyllyng ſayth oonly dyſceyue men wycked ende doo folke one ſoth ſawe byleue hondred leſynges ſo alwaye falſe dyſceyuable ſomtyme compelled myght god telle treuthes ayenſt wyll ſhame ſhenſhyp hym fynde goſpell math viij marce luce iiij et vij ſuche ſothe ſawes neuer trewer alwaye falſe lyer ſuche ſothe ſawes ben ayenſt wyll yf may wyll tourne hym dyſceyte make men ſuche ſothe ſawes whan falle byleue leſynges therfor called holy wryte spiritus mendax ſpiritus fallax ſaye ſpyryte lyer ſpyryte dyſceyuable therfore fendes hadde ſayd treuthe cryſte compelled theym ſaye anone put ſcylence ſayth gloſe ſame place wolde ellys vnder ſothe ſawe haue tolde many leſynges caplm xxxiij diues whan coniured ſo boūde vertue holy wordes muſt nedes ſaye trouthe whiche knoweth yf axed hym ¶pauper suche wytches charmer iapers faytours vſe ſuche craftes haue power bynde hym ne compelle hym telle ſuche ſothes ne right nought ne tell may noughte ne telle without haue graūte god therfore ſuche iapers wytches bynde fende fende byndeth full harde ſeruage kepeth thralles hym paſſynge whoſe boundage full harde theym eſcape without ſpecyall grace god ¶diues contra ofte men knowe clerkes cloſe hem rynges thynges make hem telle many wondres ¶pauper fende fayneth hym boūde ſuche iapers wordes dyſceyue yet cloſed ne bounde gooth abrode dyde byfore whan called ſomtyme redy anſwere full ſwyfte ſome tyme redy anſwere ne theyr wyll often though wolde may god wyll ſuffre hym ¶diues yet contra te men wote well many londes preſtes clerkes holy coniuracōns holy prayer ordeyned holy chirche catche wycked ſpyrytes men wymen ¶pauper ſoth oonly good lyuers wycked lyuers many londes catche fendes men wymen childern vertue goddes wordes holy coniuracyons holy prayer ordeyned holy chirche ſooner good man good woman ſhall doo wycked suche bynde fende hym leſe power lordſhyp ſhame ſhenſhyp hym suche ſeke worſhyp god ſhenſhypp fende helpe mannes ſoule therfore haue power god bynde hȳ compelle hym yet gloſe ſayth marce v ſuꝑ illud quod eſt tibi nomen ben ſo trauaylled fende muſte fyrſt clene ſhreuen ferre may knowe telle maner fendes doynge temptacyon haue eyther wakynge ſlepynge ſyght herynge felynge ony theyr wyttes ony thought fantaſye dyſcouere fendes counſeyll ſe wytches faytours iapers ſeke fendes worſhyp goddes worſhyp ſeke helpe fende forſake goddes helpe ſacrefyce fende forſake goddes ſacrefyce take fende ther lorde make hym theyr god ſoo fende hath power ouer ouer fende caplm xxxiiij therfore ſayth lawe xxvi q̄ vij non obſeruetis ſuche wytches axe ony counſeyll helpe ſette ony fayth brynge theyr houſes go theyr houſes haue helpe coūſeyll take hede dyſmale dayes vſe nyce obſeruaū ce newe mone newe yere ſettynge mete drynke nyght benche fede holde gobelyn ledynge ploughe fyre good begynnyng yere ſholde fare better yere folowyn ge take hede iudycyall aſtronomye dyuynacyons chyterynge byrdes fleynge foules aſſente ony ſuche nyce obſeruaunces dyuyne mannes lyfe dethe nombres ſpere pictagoras make ony dyuynynge therby ſonguary ſompnarye booke dremes booke called appoſtles lotte vſe ony charmes gaderynge herbes hangynge ſcrowes man woman childe beeſt ony ſekeneſſe ony ſcrypture fygures caractes yf pater noſter aue crede ony holy wordes goſpell holy wryte deuocyon curyouſyte oonly token holy croſſe vſen ony maner wytchecrafte ony myſbyleue y• ſuche forſaken fayth holy chirche theyr cryſtendome become goddes enemyes dyſ pleaſe god full greuouſly falle dampnacyon withouten ende amende theym ſooner therfore lawe commaūdeth byſſhopes ſholde beſye deſtroye maner wytchecraftes yf fonde ony man woman gaaf wytche crafte wolde amende ſholde chace theym theyr byſſhoryke open deſpyte xxvi q̄ v epiſcopi ſame place lawe ſayth tho wymmen y• whiche wene nyght ryde dyuerſe beſtes paſſe dyuerſe londes contrees folowe gloryous quene whiche called dyana ellys herodyana ony name wene ben theyr ſeruyce bodely moche myrthe ſuche wymen ben dyſceyued blynded fende whome ſerue therfore fende hath power diſceyue ſuffre fantaſy dreme iapery fende wene ſo bodely dede ſo tho ſay byleue men wymen myght wytchecrafte torned beſtes lykeneſſe beſtes byrdes bodely ben worſe ony paynym hate wrath bere ayenſt ony man woman take away clothes aultre clothe ye aultre dolefull clothynge beſette aultre croſſe thornes withdrawe lyght chirche ſynge ſynge maſſe requiem ben alyue hope ſholde fare worſe ſooner deye preeſt ſholde degraded preeſt ſtered hym therto ſholde exyled euer maner wytches leue wytchecraft ſholde acurſed ſolempnely wolde amende lawe ſayth ſame place next chapytre folowynge et ca• si quis lawe ſayth ca• contra yf wytches boūde men wymen ſholde beten harde ſore yf free ſhlod punyſſhed harde pryſon lawe imperyall vt ca• de maleticijs nullus et l nemo et l culpa lawe canon xxvi q̄ v qui diuinaciones gloſa suche wytches ſholde heded brente theyr faytours exyled theyr goodes forteteth lawe holy chirche byleue theym mayntene theym ſholde fyue yere penaūce xxvi q̄ v non liceat et ca• qui diuinacōes alſo forboden lawe wytchecrafte thynges come ayen ſcrypture boke table aſtrola bye ext li v ti xxvi ca• et n• ¶diues holde full good dede take thefe thefte crafte y• man may ſaluacyon people punyſſhe ſlee theef lawe enſample caplm xxxv pauper lefull ony man ſlee theef ayenſt kynges lawe without proceſſe londes lawe without auctoryte lyege lorde ne without lawfull iuge ordeyned lyege lorde yet thefe worthy deye ¶diues ſothe yf euery man myght ſlee thefe owne wyll owne dome men ſholde vnd colour thefte ſlee many true man wrath couetyſe hate ¶pauꝑ sythen men ſo moche reuerence kynges lawes londes lawes flee myſchyues ſholde falle yf lawes kepte moche reucrence ſholde goddes lawe holy chirche lawe eſchewe forfete ther ayenſt ſythen goddes lawes holy chirche lawes ben ſo reſonable good kynges lawes englonde neuertheleſſe kynges lawes yf iuſte goddes lawes many perylles moo ſholde falle yf men toke theues wytchecrafte ayenſt goddes lawes holy chirche lawes yf ſlewe ayenſt kynges lawes londes lawes ¶diues shewe ¶pauper yf man ſlee theef hym defendaunt ayenſt kynges lawe forfeteth ayenſt kynge worthy deth yf make hym iuſtyce owne auctoryte though kepe proceſſe lawe traytour kyng moche forfeteth ayenſt kyng heuen taketh theef wytchecraft ayenſt goddes lawes ſythen god holy chirche hath forboden dothe ſleeth theef ayenſt kynges lawes ſythen maketh deuyll wytches ben mooſt goddes enemyes iuge werketh theyr dome deſſpyte god y• hath forboden hem ful hygh traytour god ſo doth ten folde ſynne therfor worthy hanged theef ouer moche fende lyer alwaye redy lye leſynges dyſceyueth mankynde bryngeth men murdre ſhedyng blood rather ſlee innocentes ſlee theues yf ſuche wytchecraftes vſed many innocentes many good man woman ſholde taken ſlayne theues ſholde go free fende fauourable theues manquellers lecherous ſynfull wretch ony good man good woman hath lykynge ſlee good man good woman ſlee theef alſo god ſayth goſpell fende hath euer ben lyer ſtode neuer trenthe manqueller fader lyers leſynges therfor thoo gyue fayth tale doo therafter moche theym make god falſe forſake theyr god ſouerayne treu take theym deuyll ſouerayne falſhode ſoo worſhyppe fende dyſpyſe god yf ſuche craftes ſuffred euery man myght accuſe ſynne wolde ſaye fende wytches tolde hym maner euery man myght kylle ſlee therfore theſe ſkylles reaſons many moo flee theſe perylles many god hath forboden maner wytchecrafte done withouten helpe fende dayes god grete mercy ſuffreth fende full ſelden ſaye ſothe yf ſuffred hym ſaye ſothe englyſſhe people ſholde forſake god attones ſette theyr truſte theyr fayth fende notwithſtandynge fynde fendes tale craftes full falſe grete ofte experyence ſpende full grete therabout leſen done myſhappen yet wyll leue ceaſe noo loſſe noo prechynge ſhame neyther punyſſhyng neuertheleſſe grete wonder fende holdeth theym full harde bounde boundes churles thralles ſuche done paſſynge homage ſacrefyce ſeruyce fende forſaken god ſayd fyrſte caplm xxxvi diues suche craftes cō mracyons holy prayer done ben holden full good lyuers gyue theym faſtynge penaunce dooynge bede byddynge many good dedes therfore men gyue fayth credence byleue better ſemely fendes crafte ſholde done ſuche holyneſſe ¶pauper holy thynge holy prayer man woman vſed fendes ſeruyce worſhypp pleaſaunce doo fende deſpyte offence god worſhyppe prayer ſeruyce ſholde god fende thynges ben ordeyned oonly goddes ſeruyce ſpende deuylles ſeruyce therfore vſe holy wordes goſpell pater noſter aue crede holy prayer theyr wytchecraftes charmes comuracy • n vſe holy water fonte holy cryſme maſſes ſyngynge faſtynges contynence wullen goeynge ſuche theyr wytchecrafte make full hyghe ſacrefyce fende hath ofte ben knowen y• wytches ſayeng theyr pater noſter droppynge holy candell mānes ſteppes hated hath done foot roten ¶diues ſholde pater noſter holy candell therto ¶pauper right nought wytche worſhyppeth ſende ſo hyghely holy prayer holy candell vſed ſuche holy thynges ſeruyce deſpyte god therfore fende redy doo wytches wylle fulfyll thynges done ſo ſtandeth deuyll myſbyleue wytche pater noſter ne holy candell yet fooles mene otherwyſe fende wolde theyr wyll hym ſuche hyghe ſacrefyce whan lyght candell ſaye theyr pater noſter intente god fende forſake god worſhypp fende god clayme fende theyr fader ſayeng hym ought ſaye god pater noſter qui e celis • oure fader art heuens halowed thy name foloweth ſaye fende therfore y• fende may clay hem childern god may reſonably forſake ſay ſayd iewes vos facitis opera patris veſtri vos ex patre dyabolo eſtis et deſideria patris veſtri vultis facere io viij ye done ſayth werkes fende fader ye ben fader deuyll deſyres fader ye wyll doo ſame maner theyr chaſty te theyr faſtynge theyr penaūce doynge moche doo pleaſe fende wycked ende ſeruyce ſacrefyce fende full fewe men wymen wyl ſo moche penaunce loue god wytches loue fende pleaſe fende ſoo moche ſomtyme cutte theym ſelfe knyues prycke ſelfe launcettes ſo offre theyr fleſſhe theyr blood ſacrefyce y• fende fynde thyrde boke kynges xviij chapytre therfore byleue frendes ſythen maner ſynne ſo greuoꝰ ſo hydeous ſo abhomynable goddes ſyght ſuffre neuer none houſholde loſſe ne thefte ſekeneſſe noo helthe welthe wo yf ye ſelfe done aſſente doynge ſuffre done whan ye myght lette ye acurſed offende god full hyghely full greuouſly aſſente doynge ſette theyr fayth therin forfete ayenſt fyrſte cōmaundement full greuouſly forſake god make fende theyr god worſhyppeh hym god thynge y• theyr wytchecrafte fyre ayer water erthe deed bone ony thynge theyr mawme trye make ſymylytude god moche theym worſhyp god therfore god forbode fyrſte cōmaūdement man ſhode make hym lykeneſſe y• heuen ſaye neyther fyrmament ne fyre ne ayer ſo worde forbedeth iudycyall aſtronomye pyromancye wytchecrafte done fyre aeromancye wytchecrafte done ayer alſo forbedeth men make lykeneſſe ony thynge erthe forbedeth geomancy wytchecrafte done erthe alſo nygromancye wytchecrafte done deed bodyes ben erthe buryed erthe alſo forbedeth men make ſymylytude ony thynge water vnder erthe whiche wordes forbedeth ydrom ā cye wytchecrafte done water badde men ſholde worſhyppe none ſuche thynges god ne ſette theyr truſte ne theyr fayth therin yf doo make ſuche thynges lyke god moche make ſuche thynges lyke god maner alſo make fendes lyke god whiche dwelle ſome fyre ſome ayer ſome water ſome erthe tempte mankynde ben beſy nyght daye leſe mannes ſoule womannes ¶diues shewe ſome example maner wytchecraftes ¶pauper beſy deſtroye wytchecrafte teche wolde god noo man ne woman wyſte neyther knewe theſe ne none ther ben many yt knowe theſe many mo therto practyſe newe yere yere fendes techynge tylle moche londe blente ſhente ſuche folye ouer moche wytchecrafte reygneth openly moche pryuely namely amonges theſe olde men wymmen whiche theyr age wolde fayne holden wyſe begyn mooſt dote teche theyr yonger many folyes many nyce fantaſyes ben wytchecraftes therfore bothe olde yonge ſholde axe coūſeyll wyſe men holy chirche wyte yf ſuche thynges doynges teche lefull lefull caplm xxxvij diues comon ſawes clerkes god fyrſte cō maundement forbedeth thre pryncypall ſynnes pryde y• vnderſtand lykeneſſe aboue heuen began y• proude man woman wolde alwaye aboue worlhyp pryde god y• proude man woman wyll haue forth theyr proude wylles wyll god therfore iob myſcouetyſe ſtandeth mooſt erthly thynge therfore ſaynt poule ſayth auaryce ſeruage mawmettes ydolatrye ſaynt ierom ſayth auaryce man maketh moneye richeſſes god alſo ſaye y• ſame cōmaūdement ¶pauper vſe game recreacyon playe may ſuffred ſoo done maner honeſtly place tyme cō uenyent moche ſeſyng tyme vſe wynne therby put thynges auenture dyce full grete ſynne euyll goten good men gete praye telle generall wytchecraft ¶pauper euery craft man woman vſeth knowe ony thyng ony thyng may knowe ne waye reaſon ne werkyng kynde wytchecrafte though waye kynde vſe therto ony charmes nyce obſeruaū ce doynge wenynge myght done without charme ſuche obſeruaunce ellys ſuche charmes oonly blynde people ſholde truſte hym charmes werkyng kynde wytchecrafte yf ſay pater noſter doynge holden charmer y• people truſte hym pryncypally charmes though ſayth charmes werketh kynde yet wytche doynge wytche crafte ſuche doynge blyndeth people dyſceyued doth truſte wytchecrafte ſo worſhyp fende deſpyte god ſo euer man woman waye kynde reaſon yf vſe ony crafte iapery faytrye blynde people byleue wytche dyde waye kynde charmes ſorcery wytche goddes ſyght doynge wytchecrafte crafte make men worſhyppe fende moche doth people truſte wytchecrafte ſo ſpende theyr good fendes ſeruyce ſeke helpe fende forſake goddes helpe hath leuer hym ſelfe holden wytche deuylles ſeruaunte holden goddes man woman vncertayne tyme ſhall deye ſholde alway dredeful amys beſy well right ſo wyll men vncertayne theyr frendes whan ben deed ſtate ben ſholde alwaye beſy helpe theyr ſoules maſſes ſyngynge almes conne phyloſophre ſayth euery man woman waye kynde deſyreth knowe conne omnes homines natura ſcire deſiderant ¶pauper ſaye ſothe ayenſt lefull euery man woman deſyre conne knowe lefull deſyre knowe errour bachytynge wycked demynge yf people demed euyll ſpake euyll byfore theyr dethe ſpeke deme moche worſe theyr dethe ſoo brynge people full depe ſynne ſomtyme gone bodyes theym yt ben deed buryed ſodayne deth ¶pauper grete foly truſte therin ſayd late god wyl man woman vncertayne tyme ſholde deye maner god wyll man woman alwaye beſye flee ſynne well drede deth alway redy tyme god wyll ſende theym yf men certayne ſuche faſtynge ſholde deye ſodaynly haue tyme repentaūce ſhreuen houſeled ſholde recheleſſe theyr lyuynge ſholde leſſe care doo amys hope amendemente theyr dyeng therfor god graū teth ende effecte faſte greter ſodayne deth wyſte neuer men wyſte theym haue haue faſted ſuche faſtes vij yeres ne dyſpytefull ſhame full open punyſſhyng theyr ſynne ther neuer ſoo moche ſodayne bounden without ony dreme oftymes bothe fende fendes lymmes teche well though doo full euyll man ſo dremynge muſte full well ware ſuche dremes take none hede dremes ſtyre vanyte curyoſyte knowe afterwarde ¶pauper suche people fare worſe theyr myſbyleue theyr nyce fantaſye ſynne full greuouſly full euyll dyſceyued gyle fende whan fende ſeeth man ſhall haue dyſeaſe maketh hym nyght byfore oftymes faren full euyl whan dreme neyther god ne lady caplm xlvi ſame maner man hadde leuer mete froude frogge waye mete knyght ſquyre ony man relygyon holy chirche ſaye byleue ſhall haue golde ſomtyme metynge frogge tode haue reſceyued golde ſo falle myſbyleue deſpyſen theyr euen cryſten wote well reſceyue golde men wymen frogges ne todes deuyll lykeneſſe frogge tode mete many foule frogge tode yere yet reſceyue golde metynge yf reſceyued ony golde ſholde thanke god theyr euen cryſten frogge ne tode may nought gyue theym theſe labourer deluers dykers mooſt mete frogges todes ben full poore comonly men paye theyr hyre haue lytyl nought alſo maner ſome byleue yf kyte puttoke flee ouer waye afore ſholde fare well daye ſomtyme haue faren well ſee kyte ſo fleynge ſo falle wanbyleue thanke kyte theyr well fare god ſuche foles take none hede often men mete kyte ſo fleynge yet fare neuer better ther folke mete ſo ofte y• kyte ſo fleynge begge theyr mete fro dore dore caplm xlvij made ſcourge bette temple ſayd theym wyſe myne houſe ſholde houſe prayer ye haue made denne theues bere ye ſayd marchaūdyſe lede hen theſe beſtes make ye fad houſe houſe marchaū dyſe denne theues ſuffre thynges ſolde temple worſhyp god helpe temple moche wyll ſuffre thynges ſolde temple longeth temple oonly ſeculers ¶diues sythen god ſo offended men ſolde therin yt nedefull temple eaſement came fro ferre contrees ſholde haue done yf foūde byeng ſellynge thynges ſeculers yf foūde theym bacbytynge glotony dronkenſhyp lecherye ſonge ſpeche rybaudrye men vſe dayes holy chirche ¶pauper saynt auſtyn ſayth troweth ſholde haue caſte pytte helle ¶diues myght cryſte ſo poore man haue caſte ſuche multytude people wondre withſtoden hym ¶pauper gloſe ſayth ther came ſuche lyght face waye godhode lō ge wolde aferde ſyght face fledde awaye ſame cauſe tyme paſſyon whan came take hym ſayd ye ſeke twyes wente bacwarde drede felle downe groū de ¶diues ſayd made houſe denne theues ¶pauper ſo begyle ony man woman good theef byeng ſellynge eyther begyle ben theues goddes houſe ther caſte theyr herte pryuely ſlyghely may begyle euen cryſten therfore make goddes houſe denne theues comonly ſuche feyres markettes ſo euer holden ben many theues mychers cutte purces ¶diues drede ful often ſuche feyres goddes houſe made tauerne glotones bordell lechours marchaūtes chapman kepe theym theyr wyues lēmannes nyght daye ¶pauper yf ony man comyne fleſſhely wyfe lēmen chirche chirche yerde alſo ben pollute yf myght preued ther ſholde noo preeſte ſynge ne ſaye noo maſſe therin ne bodye buryed tyll recoūſeylled ayen byſſhop de con di si motū et c• ſignificaſti et io ſūma ſua liiiij ti• ccxliij vtrū liceat et durandꝰ ſn̄ia ſua liij ꝑ di viij q̄ xxxiij ¶diues yf prelate curate y• place take moneye chapman place ſtonde couenaūt made byfore ony ſymonye ſoo ſelle londe ſentuary ¶pauper ſy • onye full grete ſelle ony groūde ſentuarye buryenge lawe ſheweth well xiij q̄ ij q̄ſta et c• ſeq̄nti moche ſelle lette hyre marchaundyſe therfore ſuche marchaundyſe holy chirche forboden oonly goſpell alſo comon lawe xviq̄vij et hec diximus men holy chirche ſuche ſymonye takynge thynges haue moche deſpyte god holy chirche though deſpyte ſelfe wonder ¶pauꝑ ſoth god ſayth holy wryte pri• regūij ſo worſhyppeth ſayth ſhal make hym worſhyfull deſpyſe ſhall deſpyte ¶diues thanke alle myn herte thought ſome tyme noo ſynne knowe well full greuous dedely ſynne ſynnes errours haue ſpoken ben openly ayenſt worſhyppe hyghe mageſte god ayenſt fyrſte cōmaundement mooſt ought charged thy reaſons ben ſoo grete thy ſpeche ſo open ignoraunce myght excuſe ne ony thyng ellys reaſon yet people euyll cuſtome ignoraunce men holy chirche ſelfe alſo couetyſe pryde clergye ſo blent thynke theym ſynnes ſoo goo ſynne blente folye wante grace ¶pauper wycked cuſtome engendred ſynne excuſeth ſynne therfore lawe ſayth euery wycked cuſtome ſholde done awaye ¶here endeth fyrſte cōmaundement begynneth paſſe vnpunyſſhed ¶pauper thre maners goddes name taken vayne myſlyuynge myſpeche myſhe rynge fyrſte myſlyuynge whā man woman cryſtened forſaketh fende werkes lordſhypp whan godfader godmoder anſweren hym ſayeng abrenuncio ſaye forſake knytteth hym cryſte maketh couenaunt hym true ſeruaunt without ende taketh name cryſte vpon hym cometh cryſten cryſten poeple named cryſte pryncypall godfader cryſten cometh cryſte ſo cryſten people bere y• name cryſte vpon ſo moche ben called cryſten goddes people bere name god vpon v therfore ſayth prophete tu nobis e dn̄e et nomen ſanctum tuum inuocatum eſt ſuper no ne derelinquas no dn̄e deus noſter ieremye xiiij lorde ſayth thou arte amonges v lorde amonges ſeruauntes thyn holy name called vpon v lorde god forſake v yf ſo lyue name haue taken cryſte ne lyue cryſten menne goddes ſeruauntes forſake hym torne ayen fende lyue cryſten folke iewes ſaraſyns paynyms ellys worſe take goddes name vayne name lyfe accordeth ſayth ſaynt poule wycked cryſten people theyr wycked dedes theyr wycked lyuynge forſaken god therfore wycked lyuers namely ypocrytes beren name holyneſſe cryſtus ſeruauntes ben fendes ſeruauntes take goddes name vayne grete deſpite goddes name therfor cryſte ſayth ſuche wycked cryſten people per vos tota die nomē meū blaſphemat genti bus yſaye lij et ad ro ij name deſpyſed euery daye amonge nacyons hethen men wycked lyuynge cryſten people name cryſte aſhamed therfore ſaye prayer sanctificet nomē tuū halowed worſhypped thy name ſaye graūte v grace thynge ne wyll ne ſpeke wherby thy name ſholde vnworſhyped aſhamed v caplm ij alſo goddes name taken vayne moche ſpeche many wyſe fyrſte namynge goddes name vayne tale tellynge iapery ſcorne ſuche vanyte goddes name ſholde named ¶diues telle ſome enſample ¶pauper yf one ſayd ye ſcorne whan wroth god make good man ſome ſaye ſcorne god hath forſaken iapers dyce player comonly name goddes name vayne maner though ſwere none othe ſuche take goddes name ydleneſſe teche ony errours hereſyes ayenſte fayth ayenſt god preche teche treuthe oonly couetyſe enuye vayne glorye helthe mannes ſoule ne worſhyp god therfore prophete ſayth thus peccatori autē dixit deus quare tu enarras iuſticias meas et aſſumis teſtamentū meum peros tuum god ſayth ſynfull man telleſt thou rightfulneſſes takeſte teſtament lawe thy mouth ſo ofte nameſte name tho teche well ſpeke well wyl therafter take goddes name vayne alſo goddes name taken vayne curſynge ſwerynge whan men wymen wrath elles nyce myrthe ſaye god gyue myſchaūce god gyue euyll grace euyl deth alſo taken vayne oftymes vowes makyng dyuerſe maner fyrſte yf man make ony vowes ony creature vowes makynge dyuyne worſhyp ought done god creature therfore prophete ſayth vouete et reddite dn̄o deo veſtro make ye vowes lorde god yeldeth hym alſo taken vayne whan people kepe theyr vowes ben lefull breke retcheleſly wylfully freylte without nede without auctoryte theyr ſoueraynes whiche haue power dyſpenſe chaū ge theyr vowes alſo yf men make vowes vnlefull ayenſt charyte doo ony thynge ayenſt goddes lawe yf thou madeſt vowe ſlee thyn euen cryſten yu ſholdeſte neuer good poore men perauēture ſome poore man hath aggreued alſo whan men make vowes vnwyſely lyghtly without auyſement comon cuſtome ſpeche caplm iij diues ſuche vowes ben made dayes full many moche folke one ſpoken ben thought ben ſo comon theyr mouth ¶pauper therfore ſynne full greuouſly ſo takynge goddes name vayne ther ſholde vowe made thynge charyte good auyſemente fynde holy wryte iuducum vndecimo ther leder iuge goddes people whoſe name iept whan ſholde go fyght ayenſt goddes enemyes people amon made vowe god yf gaue hym y• vyctory enemyes whan cam home ayen lyuyng thynge mette fyrſte houſholde comynge home ſholde ſlee offre vp god ſacrefyce god wolde vyctory came home grete worſhyp whan doughter herde theſe tydynges ſhe full gladde toke tymber honde came gre • e haſte fyrſte houſholde daū ſynge playnge ſyngynge ayenſt fader welcome hȳ home whan iept ſawe doughter ſo comynge ayenſt hym bethought hym auowe yt made bycame full heuy childern loued full well ala doughter ala ſayd haſte thou done comeſt thou ſo ſoone ayenſt haue opened mouth god haue made vowe ayenſt muſte auowe ſlee offre vp ſacrefyce god woman doughter yet clene mayden ſo gladde goddes worſhyp faders worſhyp goddes enemyes ſo ſlayne ſhe made lytyll ſorowe none deth ſayd fader iept sythen yu haſte made ſuche vowe god hath ſente vyctorye enmyes fulfylle thy vowe take deth gladdly praye one boone er deye lete go maydens playferes morne bewayle maydenhode amonges hylles mountaynes two monethes tyme repreef woman deye without yſſue bodye iept graū ted bone two monethes ſhe came ayen fader iept mekely ſuffred deth goddes ſake loue fader thus frendes byle • e yt womās deth whiche clene mayden betokeneth cryſtes paſſyon right ſhe toke deth wylfully ſaluacōn goddes folke deſtruccōn goddes enemyes cryſte clene mayden yt neuer defouled ſynne neuer dyde amys ſuffred wylfully bytter deth ſaluacyon mankynde deſtruccōn fendes power ¶diues vowe lefull ¶pauper lefull vowe yf fyrſte mette catte hounde comynge ayenſt hym ſholde haue made ſacrefyce god therof whiche ſacrefyce ſholde haue ben abhomynacōn god neyther able offred ſacrefyce moche made vowe ſo vnwyſely god ſuffred hȳ falle myſchyef ſlee innocent owne doughter ayenſt goddes lawe god ſayth innocentē et iuſtū nō occides thou ſhalt ſlee innocent ne ye right full man ne woman ſo vowe ſo folyſly made dyde ful grete dedely ſynne forfeted full hyghely ayenſt goddes lawe therfore ſayth mayſtre ſtoryes ioſephus alſo foole vowe makynge wycked ouer cruelly done fulfyllynge therfore ſayth grete clerke yſydorꝰ synonimis liij et xxij q̄ iiij mali ꝓmiſſis reſcinde fidem turpi voto muta decretū quod incaute nouiſti ne facia impia eſt promiſſio que ſcelere adimpletur wycked byheſtes cutte awaye fayth ſaye fulfyll wycked byheſtes kepe fayth amys ſhrewed byheſtes better holden falſe true ſo fulfylleth falſe god vowe ſayth foule vnleful chaūge thy dome thou haſte wyſely auowed doo wycked byheſte fulfylled done ſynne caplm iiij diues aſſente ſaye forth praye ¶pauper alſo goddes name taken vayne blaſphemye ſpytefull ſpeche god whan men grutche ayenſt goddes dome ſekeneſſe trybulacyons dyſeaſe ſaye god vnrightfull cruell grutched ayenſt mercy whan may haue vengeaūce theyr aduerſaryes wolde haue ſaye god pacyent mercyable alſo fallen wanhope ſayen god wyll forgyue theym theyr ſynne alſo preſume moche goddes mercy wyll amende theym ſaye god wyll forgyue theym fyrſte worde alſo ſome ſaye god ſlepeth whan helpeth theym wolde haue ſpeke thus ſaye ony thynge god ayenſt worſhyp godhode take goddes name vayne blaſphemy alſo goddes name taken amys vayne euyll ſpeche othes ſwetynge ſo wyll lyghtly ſwere thynge nought charge cuſtomably falſely wote well ſwereth falſe dyſpyteouſly dyſceyuable ſwereth ony creature vſeth ony nyce othes vnlefull othes theſe take goddes name vayne ought noo man ne woman ſwere treuthe charge whan nedeth ſwere wytneſſe treuthe whan man ſhall ſwere ſhall ſwere god noo creature ¶diues moche folke ſo brought cuſtome ſwerynge vnnethe ſpeke thre wordes togydre ſwere god ſome creature ſome grete nyce othe ¶pauper ſayd fore wycked cuſtome excuſeth ſynne accuſeth aggregeth ſynne therfore drede yt yt ſwere ſo cuſtomably ſoo lyghtly ſynne dedely yf ſwere ſoth falſe therfore salomon ſayth iuracioni ne aſſueſcas o tuū • eccle xxiij lete thy mouthe ſayth vſeth ſwerynge many harde happes ſwere ſoth ſaye ſwere ther wyll man byleue ¶pauper theſe ben excuſacōns greuous accuſacōns grutchynges ſynne y• fyrſte poynte falſe ſuche falſe ſwerers loue theyr god kepe cōmaundement haue hym full lytyll mynde ſwere many horryble othes vanyte ſhrewedneſſe bycauſe myſuſe whan thynke god therfore excuſacōn open ſcorne grete blaſphemynge god yf thy ſeruaunt hadde done thynge thou haddeſt hym forboden ofter dyde worſe thou woldeſte payed yf ſcorned ſayd dyde thy loue haue y• mynde thou woldeſt holde full grete ſcorne ben moche angred hym namely yf thou ware lyege lorde kyng moche god lorde kyng thynges angred ſo ſwere ayenſte cōmaundement excuſe ſo ſcornfully ſaynge yt haue god mynde therfore drede yt ſhalbe put mynde amonge goddes choſen people cryſte complayneth hym ſuche folke fader heuen ſayth thus qm̄ quē tu ꝑcuſſiſti ꝑſecuti ſūt et ſuꝑ dolorē vulner • meo rum addiderūt fader heuen ſayth aſmoche theſe wycked ſwerers haue purſued ſmyten hym theyr wycked tongue thou ſendeſte ſuffre deth ſaluacōn mankynde put newe ſorowe aboue ſorowe bytter paynes woundes ſuffred ſynne theyr ſake therfore fader putte ſynne ſynne ſaye lette theym falle fro ſynne ſynne lette entre thy rightwyſneſſe ſaued put theym boke lyfe amonge theym ſhall blyſſe without ende lette theym wryten rightwyſſe folke ſhall ſaued theſe ben cryſtus wordes complanynge hym y• fader heuen ſuche foule ſwerers p̄o lxviij ¶diues ſemeth herby ſuche ſweryng fulgrete horryble ſynne full peryllous ſayſt yu ſeconde excuſacōn ¶pauper ben bounde neuer lye nothyng ſaye ſoth neuertheleſſe boūde ſaye al ſothes ne ought ſwere euery ſoth ſpeke ſayth ſaynt thomas de veritate theologie bothe forſwereth hym ayenſt treuthe ſwereth treuthe without grete cauſe take goddes name vayn forſwereth wyttyngly name lefull ſwere ¶pauꝑ vij caſes clerkes lewde folke may ſwere lefully fyrſte ſaue man woman harme theyr bodye fro leſynge good whan y• treuthe none wyſe preued alſo confyrmacōn pea alſo kepe fayth treuthe amonge mankynde alſo kepe obedyence ordynall ſubgeccyon ſubgettes theyr ſoueraynes alſo ſaue fredom holy chirche alſo purgacyon ſaluacyon mannes name fame alſo aſſoylynge curſe extra lii de elect ſignificaſti euery othe men muſte haue thre thynges whiche ben treuthe dome rightwyſneſſe ſayth prophete ieremye iiij ſo ſhall ſwere muſte haue treuthe cō ſcyence wote wel yt ſwereth treuthe yf ſyker weneth ſyker ſhal ſwere yt ſo weneth ſo ſayth alſo muſte haue hym dome good dyſcrete auyſemēt er ſwere ſwere treurhe nede whome ſwereth wyll ellys byleue hym thynges charge prouffytable byleued ſwere alſo muſte haue rightwyſneſſe thynge ſwereth maner ſweryng rightfull honeſt lefull extra liij de iure iurando et ſi xp̄s ¶diues wolde fayne flee ſuche othes ſayd fyrſte men wyll bylene ſwere ¶pauꝑ yf treuthe charge right profytable byleued men wyl byleue thy ſymple worde leful y• ſwere haue ſayd yf thyng charge nenedefull ſwere yu yf thou vſe ſwere comonly thynge nought thou ſynneſt greuouſly makeſt wanbyleue yt ſholde nomore byleue thyn othe without othe wyſe men wyl leſſe byleue thyn othes comonly grete ſwerers vſaunt ſwerers ben full falſe ¶diues ſo ¶pauper take goddes name ſo vayne ben falſe god theyr ſwerynge ſythen ben falſe god theyr ſwerynge gyue lytyll tale falſe man womā theyr ſwerynge begyle othes therfore yf yu wylt men byleue ye nay vſe ſpeke truly dyſcretly flee othes ſo worſhyp goddes name true god byeng ſellynge ſpeche lyuynge men ſholde byleue redely without ony othe doo ſoo ſpeke men may holde trewe man men ſhall byleue ye nay better theyr greter othes yf thou varyenge vntruſty thy worde thy dede men wyll neyther byleue y• othe neyther without othe ¶diues therfore ſome ſaye cryſte forbade maner ſweryng whan hae ſayd goſpell ego autē dico vobis nō iurare oino mathei v ſaye ye ſwere wyſe ¶pauꝑ englyſſhe cryſtus worde englyſſhe ſaye ye ſwere ony maner ſaye maner cauſe lyghtly ne cuſtomably alſo badde tho wordes men ſholde ſwere creature wytnes neyther heuen goddes trone ne erthe ſtole vnder fete ne ierlm cyte grete kyng ne thyne hede thou canſte make one thyn here whyte ne blacke lete worde ye ye nay nay mathei v ¶diues muſte ſaye twyes ye twyes nay ¶pauper yu muſt yf yu wylt true ſame ye thou ſayſte thy mouth yu muſte ſaye thyn herte thy mouth thyn herte muſte accorde togydre yf thou ſaye ye thy mouth nay thyn herte yu arte falſe doſte ayenſt cryſtus lore ¶diues yet contra te saynt iames ſayth ante oīa frēs mei nolite iurare • iacobi v byfore thynges leue brethern wyll ye ſwere neyther heuē ne erthe ne ony othe wherby ſemeth lefull ſwere ¶pauper saynt iames forbedeth v vtterly ſwere byddeth men ſholde wyll ſwere ony othe men ſholde ſwere nede ¶diues yet contra te cryſte byddeth goſpell mathei v worde ſholde ye ye nay nay qd autē habundanciꝰ eſt malo eſt ſpeche full euyll wherby ſemeth yf men ſay ye nay othes ſwerynge amys ¶pauper cryſte ſayd euyll ſaye ye nay ſwere whan nedeth ſayd full euyll men ſwere ſaye ye nay cometh wanbyleue hym wyl byleue euen cryſten ſwere alſo cometh falſhede people moche people ſo falſe vnnethe men may byleue theym without othe othe ¶diues fyndeſte yu god badde men ſwere leful ſwere ¶pauper goſpell yu allegeſt ayenſt mathei v cryſte ſayth thus reddes dn̄o iuramenta tua thou ſhalt yelde thy lorde god thyn othes ſaye yu ſhalt ſwere hym none therfore ſayth deut vi thou ſhalt drede thy lorde god ſerue hym allone ſwere name caplm vij diues forbedeth cryſte men ſwere creature ¶pauper ther two maner ſwerynge one takynge wytneſſe thynge man ſwereth ſo lefull ſwere ony creature ſaynt poule ſayth hoīes ꝑ maiorē ſuū iurant ad hebre vi men ſwere ſayth theyr ſaye hym credence reuerence ben ſelfe god dygnyte ordre kynde man bothe god man therfore wyll take ſwerynge wytneſſe hym ſouerayne treuthe therfore ſuche maner ſwerynge dyuyne worſhyp longeth oonly god creature god wyll whan men may haue wytneſſe treuthe nedefull prouffytable byleued take hym wytneſſe ſwere hym ſouerayne treuth creature ſuche maner ſwerynge dyuyne worſhypp longeth god creature gloſe ſayth mathei v ſuꝑ illud non ꝑiurabis ſaynt auſtyn ſayth ſame place ſo ſwereth ony creature ſwereth god made yt creature therfore cryſte badde y• men ſholde ſwere creature yf lyghtly fall double ſynne ydolatry periury fyrſte ydolatry worſhyp longeth god creature alſo falle • e ſo periury men drede leſſe lye forſwere whan ſwere creature whan ſwere god allone caplm viij maner ſwerynge execracyon imprecacōn whan man woman theyr ſwerynge prayeth openly pryuely ayenſt hym ſelfe ayenſt ony thynge loueth ony thyng ſayth thus ſome man ſwereth hede ſome man thedame ſaynt auſtyn ſayth ſwereth ſoo byndeth hym ſelfe leyeth hede thedame plegge god prayeth god leeſe hede thedame neuer thryue ſayth ſayth behoteth ſwere theyr ſoule theyr chaffre goodes haue ſo bynde theym leſe theyr ſoule theyr chaffre theyr goodes bynde theyr ſoule fyre helle without ende ſaye ſwere theyr fader moders ſoules ſo moche may bynde theyr fader moders ſoules paynes helle without ende ſaye byhoten theyr ſwerynge praye openly ayenſt themſelfe whan ſaye ſo helpe god forſake helpe god ſaye som ſaye ellys deuyll brenne god gyue ellys myſchaūce ſuche maner ſwerynge ſolempne othes men make dome dome whan men ſaye ſo helpe god holy dome ellys ſo helpe god holy dome othe men forſake helpe god lady al company heuen daye dome ſoo ſaye ouer yf ſwere falſe calle god wytneſſe thynge falſe ſayen god whoſe name treuth bereth wytneſſe thynge falſe ſoo lye god doo hym grete velonye neuer falſe wytneſſe ne neuer ſhall ſouerayne treuthe dyſceyueth ne may dyſceyueth ſhall theſe falſe ſwerers fele daye dome amende ¶diues lay men theyr hondes boke whan ſhall ſwere byfore iuge ¶pauper men ſholde charge theyr othe whan layeth honde booke forſaketh fayth holy chirche holy prayer wryten boke ſayth alſo forſaketh ioyes heuen wryten boke byndeth hym paynes wryten booke ſayth layeth honde booke ſwerynge forſaketh gode dedes euer dyde euer ſhall doo ſothe ſwereth holy wryte hondes ben vnderſtonden werkes ſwereth ſoo mouth kyſſeth booke forſaketh holy prayer good wordes euer ſpake mouth euer ſhall ſpeke yf ſayth ſwere ſoth yf forſwere hym mouth maketh vnnable reſceyue holy ſacrament aultre cryſte hym ſelfe ſouerayne treuthe vnder fourme brede caplm ix diues ſayſte thou theym though ſwere ſoth yet ſlyghe ſafte wordes dyſceyue theyr euen cryſten whiche vnderſtonde theym ¶pauper suche forſworen two maners man may forſworen ſwerynge ſoth fyrſte yf ſwere ſoth begylynge wordes ſlyghe begyle euen cryſten yſydorus ſayth xxijq̄ quinta quacū que crafte ſayeng euer thou vſeſt thy ſpeche thyne othes dyſceyue thyn euen cryſten god knoweth thyn thought thy conſcyence taketh thou meneſt vnderſtandeth thou ſwereſt ſo dyſceyte ſayth thou doſt double ſynne ſo ſwerynge yu takeſt goddes name vayne alſo thou dyſceyueſt thyn euen cryſten ¶diues telle ſome example ¶pauper fynde lyfe ſaynt nycholas iewe lente cryſten man grete ſomme golde vnto certayne daye toke ſykerneſſe hym fayth ſaynt nycholas borowe daye paſſed cryſten man payed wherfore iewe chalenged golde ye cryſten man byfore iuge ſayd falſely payed hym whan iuge ſholde ſytte cauſe cryſten man bethought hym begyle fayned hym ſeke cam lenyng ſtaffe byfore iuge whiche ſtaffe put al golde ought iewe therto ſtaffe holowe ſholde laye honde boke toke iewe ſtaffe honde prayeng hym holde whyles made othe iewe thought gyle toke ſtaffe holde prayed hȳ falſe cryſten man layd honde boke made othe maner god ſaynt nicholas ſo helpe god holy dome toke y• moneye thou chalengeſt therto ſayd ſoth taken hym tyme ſtaffe iewe wroth ſayd hym trewely yu haſte forſworen god ſaynt nycholas praye god ſaynt nycholas thy borowe harde vengeaunce come cryſten man toke ſtaff ayen iewe wente ayen homewarde lenynge ſtaffe ther felle ſuche heuyneſſe ſlepe hym yt layde hym downe waye ſlepe lytyl cyte made othe layde ſtaffe golde faſte beſydes hym ther came carte wente vpon hym ſlew hym brake ſtaffe tyll golde ſcatered anone people iewe alſo ranne ſee fallen whan ſawe ſtaffe broken golde ſoo ſcatered knewe gylfully ſworen thanked god ſaynt nycholas treuthe ſo tryed ſhewed iewe gaue golde poore folke bycame cryſten man ¶diues enſample open ſee gylefull othes ben full peryllous saye forth praye ¶pauper alſo man may forſworen ſweryng ſoth vnwyttyngly weneth ſwere falſe dyſceyue euen cryſten yf ſwore daye dyſceyue hym lette hym iourney wenynge ſelfe daye thoughe daye ferre daye yet forſworen lawe ſheweth well xxij q̄ ijc• alſo yf man ſwere treuth blaſphemye goddes name yf ſwore goddes body herte eyen woūdes ony ſuche yf vſed therto forſworen ſoth falſe ſwereth caplm x wherfore frende ye ſhal vnderſtonde vi maners man forſworen fyrſte yf ſwere ayenſt cōſcyence whā ſwereth falſe wyttyngly though drede alſo yf ſwere ony thynge vnlefull ayenſt charyte yf ſwere ſlee man defoule woman bodye yt ſhall neuer almeſſe poore men ne come neyghbours houſe alſo yf man ayenſt othe whiche lefull though drede deth yf othe tourne none euyll ende alſo yf ſwere treuth dyſceyte gyle ſayd late alſo yf ſwere vnwyſely ſayth durandus ſūma ſua extra de iureiurando c• sicut et c• tua yf auyſement vſaūtly dedely ſynne ſayth euery othe made vnwyſely periurye alſo yf compelle ſwere wyttynge well wyll forſwere hym lawe ſheweth well xxijq̄iiij inter cetera ſaynt auſtyn alſo 〈◊〉 ſermon maketh decollacyon ſaynt iohan baptyſte •• leth tyme good ſymple true man hadde lente certayne moneye falſe man whiche forſoke ſayd lente hym none wherfore true man prouoked hym ſwere knowynge well wolde forſwere hym ſoo dyde true man loſte moneye nyght folowynge true man thought ſtode byfore grete iuge whiche ſayd hym wyſe dydeſte yu man ſwere ſythen thou wyſte well ſholde forſwere hym lorde ſayd denyed good iuge ſayd hym better haue loſte thy good ſlee ſoule god boughte ſoo dere precyous blood anone dyde hym bete full harde ſore ſoo moche whan awoke backe appyred ful woū de beten full blacke blew whan repented hym axed mercy ſynne forgyuen hym caplm xi diues myght well ſo bothe toke goddes name vayne dyde dyſpyte therto ſwerer forſwore hym wyllyngly wyttyngly made hym ſwere wyllyngly wyttyngly dyde hym forſwere deſpyſe goddes name ſo aſſented • eriury lawe doth ſynne aſſenteth therto ben gylty ſynne ben worthy ſame payne praye ſayſt thou theym ſwere ſo dyſpytefully horrybly goddes bodye herte blood ſuche ¶pauper maner ſwerynge open blaſphemye grete deſpyte god yf man woman vſed therto ſwere ſoth ſwere falſe ſynneth dedely ſuche take goddes name vayne alſo grete deſpyte therfore forboden lawe xxijq̄ si quis per capillū ther ſholde noman ſwere heere cryſte ne hede ne parte cryſte ne vſe ſuche blaſphe mye ayenſt god ony maner wyſe yf dyde wolde ceſſe amende hym yf man holy chirche ſholde depoſed degraded yf lewde man ſholde acurſed purſued cenſure holy chirche tyll wolde amende hym lawe imperyall gloſe ſayth ſuche foule ſwerers ſholde punyſſhed vttreſt payne torment ſaue deth therfore almayne ſuche folke ben punyſſhed ſhamefully dyuerſe cōtrees therfore tho contrees ben vſed none othes byfore iuge ellys grete nede ther theyr ſpeche y• goſpell techeth ya nene y ye nay englyſſhe kepe treuth ya nene doo grete othes vſe londe ſuche foule ſwerers ſpeketh saynt poule ſayeng moche theym goddes ſone ofte croſſe make iape ſcorne paſſyon rurſum crucifigentes ſibimetipſis filiū dei et oſtentui irriſioni habentes ad hebre vi ſpeke vnreſonable beſte rente cryſte theyr othes nyght daye repreue cryſte ſhamefull deth ſuffred theyr ſynne theyr ſake ought take mooſt mater loue hym worſhyp hym take mooſt occaſyon vnkyndneſſe deſpyſe hym deyed bytter deth ſhamfull gylte ſynne ſake ſholde neuer ellys haue ſworen goddes deth wepte ſalte teerys eyen ſake owne ſholde neuer ellys haue ſworen goddes eyen percyd herte ſhedde precyous herte blode waſſhe v ſynnes ſholde neuer elli haue ſworen goddes herte ne goddes blood ſuffred depe woūdes bytter paynes bodye bone ſaue v paynes helle ſholde neuer ellys haue ſworen woūdes bodye bone ne blood alſo ayenſt endleſſe loue ſhewed v ſhewe hym grete vnkyndneſſe ayenſt grete worſhyp dyde v brought v endles worſhyp hym ouer grete velonye fynde y• myracles lady ſomtyme ther ryghtfull iuge demynge ful gylty ſuche othes ſwerynge somdele deuoute lady grette euery daye certayne auees wherfore lady nyght appyred hym ſhewed hȳ childe blody eyen put y• hede henge downe chekys herte rente bodye henge downe ſyde bodye corne wrappyd blood ſhe ſayd hym thou art iuge gyue ryghtfull dome man worthy haue thus hath arayed childe iuge anſwered ſayd worthy hanged necke fyre helle without ende lady anſwered hym forſothe thou art ſame man hadde neuer childe allone whiche borne bodye ſaluacyon mankynde thou moche haſte putte eyen whan thou ſworeſt goddes eyen thou renteſt herte whan thou ſworeſt goddes herte thou haſt rente hym thyne foule othes therfore amende yu ſhalte haue ſame dome thou haſte gyuen ſhalte hanged necke fyre helle without ende caplm xij diues ſayſte thou theym ſwere cock ſtede god ſome god holy dome ſome laken ſome lady ſome cockes bodye ſome theyr hode ſome theyr tytpat cap many ſuche nyce othes men vſe theſe dayes ¶pauper yf ſwere ony ſuche othes begyle theyr euen cryſten vnderſtande theym ſynne dedely ben alſo forſworen couple knytte gydre god holy dome ſwerynge erneſt game full greuous ſynne grete deſpyte ſcorne goddes name yf ſwere ſuche othes dyſceyte flee gretter othes yet ſynne full greuouſly yf ben vſed therto ayenſt cryſtus cōmaundement byddeth v ſwere creature ne ſwere grete nede prouffyte ellys outwarde ſholde ye ye nay nay yf man compelled ſwere ſhal ſwere god none ſuche nyce othes moreouer frende whan man ſwereth cap hode ony ſuche eyther ſwereth ſoo waye wytneſſe takyng waye execraccyon yf ſwere ſoo waye wytneſſe takynge dooth hymſelfe foule velony maketh hode worſhyp credence hymſelfe ſaynt poule ſayth ther ſholde noo man ſwere wytneſſe takynge better offendeth god full hyghely worſhyp longeth god doth hode ſwerynge bere wytneſſe dyuyne worſhyp longeth god yf ſwere hode waye execracyon ſo muſt leſe hode ſaye ſoth ouer ſcornefull othe grete loſſe man leſe hode wynne hondred poūde ¶diues yet ſuche ben true theyr worde ſwere gretter othes ¶pauper somtyme ſo fende tempteth leſſe leſſe ſynne holde theym ſtylle y• gretter ſo drawe ſame ſynne yt perceyue ſynne robbe god worſhyp robbe man catell ſuche ſwere theyr hode dyuyne worſhyp ther hode take god make worſhyp theyr hode goddes holy name ofte ſuche ſwerers kepe treuth ſmale thynges comon dyſceyue men greter thyngis charge therfore praye vſe ſuche nyce othes lete thy worde ye ye nay nay cryſte byddeth ſo ſayd mekeneſſe reuerence yf nede ſaye ſaye ye truly nay truly ſykerly ſothly maner ſpeche none othe ellys ſaye ſaye ye truly falſely ſaye ye ſykerly dyſceyuably vſe none othes yu compelled thy ſouerayne thyng charge men ſhall byleue well thy ye ye thy nay nay without ony caplm xiij diues ſynne man ſwere god hode ¶pauper ſynne holyer thynge man ſwereth greter ſynne periurye lawe ſayth ſynne man forſwere hym god creature falſe goddes mawmettes thou yf yu ſwere ony othe ony creature lefull ſwere thou ſynneſte greuouſly yf thou ſwere ſoth ſwere falſe yet periury god ſynne ony creature ¶diues yf man ſwere hode bounden kepe othe ¶pauper yf othe lefull ſpedefull ellys dooth ſynne ſynne lawe ſayth xxijq̄i mouet te ¶diues lefull cryſten man take othe hethen man ſwereth falſe goddes ¶pauper lefull yf may none ſykerneſſe haue hym lefull cryſten man ſtyre hym ſo ſwere example haue gen̄ xxxi laban ſwore iacob falſe goddes ¶diues whan ſeruauntes ben ſworen theyr lorde ſhall true hym warne hym harmes ben boūde telle hym myſchyues falſe dedes velonyes done lorde houſholde houſholde yf knowe ¶pauper yf lorde fell cruell baratoꝰ ſuſpecte ayenſt perſone gylty trowe ſeruaunt othe boūde telle lorde therof accuſe perſone alſo othe vn •• full ſo kepynge othe ſholde brynge lorde greuous ſynne therfore ſholde haue made othe begynnynge ſemely yt moche dyſeaſe myght come therof yf kepte natheleſſe yf ſeruaunt ſoo ſwore knewe ony thynge berynge takynge awaye waſtyng lordes good hath kepynge ought warne lorde therof yf peaſybly haue ayen ſaue lordes prouffyte euery ſeruaūt boūden warne lorde harme done lorde offyce good fayth ſaluacyon owne perſone yf ellys peaſybly redreſſed yf ony defaultes yt touchen offyce yf preue boūde telle lorde yf lorde pacyent reſonable cruell yf preue boūde telle lawe ſheweth full well xxxv q̄ vi ep̄s ſynodo et ijq̄i si peccauerit et q̄vij plerū que viq̄ij si tm̄ yf ſeruaūt whan made othe thought bynde hym telle lorde harmes knewe whan preue othe lefull therfore byndeth euery ſeruaunt bounden othe fayth true lorde warne hym harme velonye comon maner bounde accuſe ſpecyall yf preue full preuely ſuche one wyll prouffyte perſone harme hym ne defame hym amende hym accuſynge ſpecyall yf playnt preued maketh hate fyghtynge manſlaughter dyffamacyon grete dyſeaſe caplm xiiij diues whan comunyte college ſwereth theyr ſucceſſours doo kepe certayne thynge tyme comynge yf theyr ſucceſſours neyther kepe theyr couenaunte ben theyr ſucceſſours forſworen ¶pauper nay othe byndeth perſones ſwore theyr ſucceſſours periury neuertheleſſe ſucceſſours ben bounden good fayth doo kepe theyr predeceſſours boū de theym ſoo ſwerynge yf lefull yf haue ſame prouffytes therof theyr predeceſſours hadde extrahe veritatis et ray li pri• ti de periurio item pone ¶diues yf man make othe man may man yt maketh vnbynde hym othe forgyue hym ¶pauꝑ yf ſoo yt othe made pryncypally fauour goddes worſhyp man made aſſoyle hym ne vnbynde hȳ othe ne none may chaūgynge ſome better thynge nede vnpower excuſe hym yf othe made pryncypally fauour man ſwereth man may wel vnbynde hym fro othe yf made yt othe fauour man man may vnbynde hym othe ony condycōn put othe lette ſwore ſholde gyue thy fader x ſhelynges yu myghteſt vnbynde fro yt othe thy fað myght well vnbynde therof ¶diues whether man harder boūde auowe othe ¶pauper auowe byndeth harder auowe byndeth v fayth treuth owe god paye hym byheſtes othe bynde v pryncypally true euen cryſten reuerence goddes holy name ſayth iohēs ſū con liitiixq̄xiiij quero ¶diues yf man woman haue doo ony dedely ſynne whiche ſhreuen contryte may ſwere ſykerly gylty ſynne auoyde ſclaundre hymſelfe frendes wyll byleue hym ſwere ¶pauper aſmoche knoweth ſykerly yt ſuffycyently contryte ſyker whether ſynne forgyuen hym therfor ſholde myſchyef ſwere ſoo folyſly moche ſholde ſwere owne profer whan hym nedeth ſwere ſū con ti ixq̄ xij • de vxore extra liv purgacōe canonica accepimus ¶diues yf man woman make two othes contrarye may kepte togydre ¶pauper fyrſte ſhall kepte yf lefull hoſtrienſis liij rubrica de iureiurando quot comites • item ſi duo yf man make two auowes contrarye may kepte greter ſhal kepte yf lefull ſhal ſatyſfaccōn dome prelate sū cō ti viijq̄lxxxiij caplm xv diues auowe proprely ¶pauper auowe byhotynge ſome good thynge made god auyſement raymunde ſayth ¶diues whan man woman anguyſſhe dyſeaſe maketh auowe holpen ben bounden fulfyll yt auowe though anguyſſhe dyſeaſe brought theym therto ¶pauꝑ yes forſoth yf thought cauſe whan made vere purpoſe bynde theym yf theyr deſyre helpe yt nede ſo yt kepyng theyr auowe ben better dyſpoſed kepe goddes cōmaūdementes therto ſholde comon auowes deſerue wyfe peryl childe beryng ſekenes maketh auowe yf ſhe ought none make without leue huſbonde yet ſhe ought doo ayenſt auowe owne dome ne without dome ſouerayne yf ſhe fele holpen auowe neuertheleſſe trowe huſbonde may vnbynde therfro confeſſour alſo chaūgynge ſome good dede namely yf kepynge auowe ſholde tourne preiudyce yt huſbonde lettynge better dede wyues ought make grete auowes ſholde dyſeaſe preiudyce theyr huſbonde ne childern within age ſholde make none auowe without aſſente theyr fader theyr tutour ne ſeruaūte preiudyce hyndryng lorde mayſtre yf lorde mayſtre may reuoke ſo may fader childes huſbonde wyues auowes ben preiudyce huſbonde wyfe may ſaye certayne bede grete pylgremage ne grete abſtynence ne contynence ne gyue grete almeſſe yf huſbonde euyll dyſpoſed wyttes ruled cuſtome reaſon yf huſbonde haue pyte nedy people ſhe may make auowe gyue poore people yt pleaſaūce god power ſauynge theyr bothe aſtate ¶diues whether medefull good dede auowe without auowe ¶pauper auowe vowe makynge one hygheſt worſhyp man may quia eſt actus latrie alſo auowe man meketh hym mooſt god gyueth god mooſt gyfte gyue free wyl alſo gyueth greter gyfte gyueth tree fruyte gyueth fruyte reſerueth hym tree alſo vowe mannes wyl ſtabled goodneſſe neuertheleſſe moche man woman ben full frayle chaūgeable therfore men ſholde make auowes fewe good auyſement brekynge auowes grete dyſhonour god ¶diues yf man make vowe oonly vnder condycōn ¶pauper yf condycōn falle bounde ellys yf man bynde hym dyuerſe cauſes yf ther one falle bounden though fallen yf made ony auowe go ſaynt iames hope fynde brother alſo haue redempcōn ſynnes though wyſte afterwarde certaynly ye ſholde fynde brother yet boūde go thyder y• cauſe ¶diues many cauſes man woman vnboūde auowe ¶pauper four cauſes fyrſte yf pryncypall cauſe auowe makynge fayle yf man make auowe faſte yt ſatyrdayes haue helth childe yf childe amende boūde therto alſo yf made vnder condycyon ne falleth alſo yf ſouerayne vnbynde hym therof alſo yf haue power kepe ¶diues yf mayden make auowe lyue maydenhode lyfe durynge yf ſhe corrupte leſe maydēhode ſhe vnboū de auowe ſhe lenger lyue maydenhode ¶pauper yf ſhe lenger lyue maydenhode yet ſhe boūde contynence lyfe kepe auowe moche ſhe may ſo auowes men may ben boūde may moreouer ye ſhall vnderſtonde ſome auowe nede auowe make bapty forſake fende kepe fayth holy chirche auowes free wyll whan man byndeth hym frely good dede without whiche may ſaued faſtynge contynence pylgremage two thynges nedefull chaungynge auowe rightfull cauſe auctoryte ſouerayns dyſpen ſacyon auowe abſtynence ſuche muſte taken hede richeſſes pouerte y• perſone poore man caas ought haue moche dyſpenſacōn peny right nought grete lorde hondred marke condycōns ben vnderſtonden auowes though man ſaye ſhall yf lyue yf god wyll condicōns ben ſpecyal ſhal vyſyte ſaynt thomas yf go kent bothe maners theſe condicōns yf fayle man excuſed auowe yf ſtande yt condycōn huſbonde may entre relygyon wyfe make fyrſte auowe perpetuell cōtynence neyther wyfe ne ye huſbonde may make auowe cōtynence without others aſſente solempne auowe cō tynence letteth matrymony done yf ſolempne yf perſone wedde yt matrymony holdeth muſte paye dette bodye wyfe may axe solempne auowe made takynge holy ordre entre relygyon though man woman breke faſte bycauſe ſekeneſſe breketh abſtynēce extra liv de regulis iuris qd non eſt licitū caplm xvi diues yf man woman ſwere thynge haſtyneſſe whiche othe wolde haue ſworen yf auyſed theym ¶pauper yf theyr othe meane kepe better goddes cōmaundement flee therby ſynne loue god boūde kepe othe ellys ¶diues yf childern ſwere doo thyng leful whyle within age may theyr fader moder reuoke othe ¶pauper fader moder tutour may reuoke childerens othes theyr vowes ſoone knowe therof ſo may huſbonde wyfe ſhe boūde obeye reuocacōn yf go forth whan wote therof reuoke begynnynge afterwarde may lawe reuoke ne fader childes othe ne vowe ¶diues ſuppoſe reuoke afterwarde ¶pauper bothe wyfe huſbonde childe fader whyle within age ought obeye auyſe hym peryll ſo reuoketh caplm xvij diues whether periury ſynne manſlaughter ¶pauper periury ſaynt poule ſayth ad hebr vi men ſholde ſwere theyr better theyr gretter euery contrauerſy ſaye euery cauſe debate conferme true parte laſte ende othe euery ſuche cauſe termyned ended othe ſythen ſo cauſe manſlaughter euery open ſynne touchynge mannes dome muſte termyned othe periurye muſte taken paſſynge ſynne ſoo ſoo forſwereth hym wyttyngly forſaketh god therfore periury greteſt ſynne ſynnes next ydolatrye ayenſt ſeconde cōmaundement inmedyatly ayenſt god deſpyte forſakyng god manſlaughter inmedyatly ayenſt man though man manſlaughter greued god full ſore yet forſaketh god ne deſpyſeth hȳ ne dyſhonoureth hym ſo moche doth periury yt phyloſophre ſayth princi• meta• amonges hethen men othe hath euer worſhypfull euery ſecte iewe saraſyn paynym fleeth ſwere falſely goddes name mooſt inconuenyent yf māſlaughter ſynne periury folye trye cauſe manſlaughter othe ſemely aferde grete ſynne manſlaughter ſholde lytyll drede falle yt ſynne periury yf leſſe thus ſayth ſaynt thomas qōe qðlibe et io ſū lii ti q̄ xxiiij vt rum ¶diues yf men charged periury falſe othes yu doſt many man ben hanged drawen ſlayne otherwyſe yet lyue fare wel full harde ſo lyghtly ſlee man worde whan lyfe may ſaued worde man coſteth full moche come man ¶pauper therfore men ſholde beſyly flee periurye falſe othes ther thynge cauſeth ſo moche manſlaughter ſhedynge blood periury doth ¶diues praye yf thou ¶pauper salomon ſayth eccle x kyngdome fletted chaū ged fro nacyon nacyon wronges vnrightfulnes deſpytes done goddes name dyuerſe gyles periury cauſe falſe dome wronges vnright fulneſſe cauſe gyle treaſon grete dyſpytes ben done god man ſayd fyrſte euery cauſe muſte ended wytneſſes queſtes whiche ben ſworen ſaye treuth alſo iuge whiche ſworen god kyng deme rightful dome yf ben charged ſaye treuth gyue none anſwere forſwere lye ſhall dyſceyue iuge hym gyue falſe dome suche periurers robbe men theyr good dyſhereted moche folke ſaue ſtronge theues ſlee true men suche robbe folke theyr good name ſuche ben falſe god kyng prelate holy chirche suche ben cauſe londe poynte loſte chaūged nacyon newe tongue may without ſhedynge moche blood manſlaughter ſo periury cauſe moche manſlaughter alſo periurye cauſe haue ſoo many theues manquellers londe hope alwaye ſaued periury falſhode queſtmongers yt lytyl good wyll forſwere therfore hope periury ben ſo bolde theyr ſynne robbe ſlee brenne though ben taken yet hope ſcape periury yf ſyker ther wolde man ne womā forſwere hȳ ſaue wolde neuer ſoo bolde ſynne ſholde y• aferde ſynne yf wyſte wel true dome ſholde paſſe periury suche ſynfull wretch ꝓphete yſaye ſayth xxiij haue put theyr hope leſynges ꝓiury leſynges falſhode periury ben mayntened chaſty ſed alſo ſynne ayenſt kynde ſaue theef dyſpyte god whoſe name forſwere ayenſt cōmaū dement byddeth ther ſholde man take name vayne alſo ſayth non ſuſcipies vocem mendacij nec iunges manū vt ꝓ impio dicas falſū teſtimoniū exo xxiij thou ſhalte take voyce leſynges ne ioyne thyn honde makynge couenaunt bere ony falſe wytneſſe wycked man ſaue maleficos nō pacieris viuere exodi xxij thou ſhalte ſuffre wytches open malefactours neyther felones lyue ſlee theym chaſtyſynge slee one ſaue many one alſo ſynne ayenſt kynde ouer grete folye man ſlee owne ſoule without ende ſaue theef neuer wolde doo hym good tourne alwaye redy robbe hȳ perauenture ſlee hȳ whan may grete folye offende god periury pleſe theef manqueller offendeth god al contree suche ben lyke iewes ſaued barrabam y• ſtronge theef manqueller ſlewe ſwete iheſu ſouerayne treuth neuer dyde amys holy doctours tellen yt man ſholde rather ſuffre mooſt dyſpytous deth bodye ſholde ſwere ony dedely ſynne moche ſholde forſwere hym ne dedely ſynne ſaue theues lyfe god londes lawe cōmaūde ſlee felle late londe scotte appeled englyſſhe man hygh treaſon whan ſholde fyghte byfore iuge theyr cauſe iuge maner put theyr othe whan scotte ſholde ſwere ſayd iuge lorde came hyder ſwere cam fyght chalenge fyght therto redy ſwere wyll made chalenge ſwere iuge ſayd yf wolde ſwere appele true ellys ſholde taken cōuycte taynt traytour hanged drawen without fyghtynge ſo wolde ſwere wyttynge wel appele falſe made malyce knowleched er • e deyed man myght haue ſworen happely haue hadde better aduerſarye eſcaped deth grete worſhypp worlde yet leuer deye dyſpytefully dyſpyte goddes name ſwere falſe therby leuer deye bodely periury god ſlee owne ſoule helde gretter ſynne manſlaughter though wolde auenge hȳ man rancour herte yet god wolde venge hym periury ſo god ſaued fro periury māſlaughter gaue grace dey charyte make amendes god man caplm xviij diues sythen periury ſo grete ſynne payne ordeyned therto lawe ¶pauper lawe ſayth xxij q̄ p̄dicandū aſmoche penaūce ſholde enioyned periury manſlaughter auoutry ſholde neuer taken ſwere bere wytneſſe ony dome ſhall forſaken euery dome taynt falſe alwaye ſuſpecte falhode londes lawes many contrees yf taynt forſworē byfore iuge ſholde dyſhereted euer theyr houſes drawen downe theyr wodes hewen downe theyr tree alſo mānes hyght aboue y• groūde ſtockes ſtonde ſtylle endeles repreef theym al theyr kynrede ther ſynne ſo noyous royalme euery comunyte periury yt cauſe yt ther may ſynne punyſſhed ne malefactours ne felones chaſtyſed ne wronges redreſſed men holy chirche ſholde degraded lewde people accurſed xi q̄ conſpiracionūet c• coniuracionū al ſynnes whan haue done penaū ce theyr fynne ben amended ben lawe reſtored ayen theyr ſame ſo y• may bere wytneſſes dome theyr othe ought reſceyued periurers ben taynt ſhall neuer reſtored theyr fame ne taken wytneſſe ne othe accepted noo dome ſayth hoſti liij ru de teſti bus si • poſſit excipit et • hoc idē et extra worſhyppe ¶diues periurye ſo harde punyſſhed lawe ¶pauper ſynne ouer greuous ouer moche haūted mooſt openly ayenſt ſubſtaūce treuth wytneſſe mooſt maynteneth falſhode letteth mooſt treuth rightwyſneſſe ſayth ſame clerke hoſtyenſis ſame place suche periurers may ſaye wryten yſaye lix concepimus et locuti ſumus de corde verba mendacij • haue conceyued falſe contryuynges haue ſpoken herte wordes leſynges therfore rightfull dome tourned bacwarde rightfulneſſe ſtode ferre durſte putte forth hede treuth felle downe openly ſtrete borne downe openly noo man wolde helpe hym vp equyte ſayth ne euenhode ſhyftynge demynge myght entre treuthe forgeten fledde wyckedneſſes euery mānes pray ¶diues ſee periurye full greuous ſynne full peryllous euery comunyte cauſe moche manſlaughter ſhedyng mannes blood leſynge royalmes haue redde y• royalme englonde periurye falſhode tranſlated brytons saxon afterwarde tranſlated periurye saxon englyſſhe men dane afterwarde whan englyſſhe men kyngdome ayen deth dane kepte two kynges tymes saynt edwarde heraldes anone trāſlated ayen periurye vnto norman wyllyam duke normandy whiche ſlough well nyghe chyualrye londe chaūged lordſhyp prelacye londe nyghe vnto frenſſhe men murdre ſhedynge blode fell theſe periurers theſe thre tymes chaūgynges full harde telle allas newely dayes ben fallen periury hygheſt degree one nygh blood hath ſhedde ſythen bycauſe periurye tonge telle londe ſhedynge blood ſo feblyſſhed euery aſtate power without ſpecyall myracle god lenger withſtande ſo full moche drede y• royalme ſhort tyme periurye ſhall tranſlated ayen brytones ellys ſome tongue praye ſaye forth thou wylt caplm xix pauper furthermore ſayd goddes name taken vayne myſherynge yf yu haue lykynge grete othes men omy myſſwerynge yf thou wayte vayne othes ne art myſprayſed whan thou hereſte thou takeſt goddes name vayne thou dooſt worſhyppe therto thou oughteſt doo salomon ſayth mannes heere ſholde aryſe fere ſholde ſtop eres whan herde goddes name ſo deſpyſed yf man ſwere y• ſadly goddes name auyſely thou art boūden byleue hȳ worſhyp goddes holy name thou haue euydence contrarye yu accepte othe gyue credence therto ye knowe contrarye ellys yu takeſt goddes name vayne thou dooſt due worſhyp therto grete deſpyte thou wylt byleue ſo worſhypfull wytneſſe god taketh wytneſſe ſoo ſwerynge many ſymple man wolde euyll payed yf thou forſokeſt hym wytneſſe treuthe ¶diues yf fynde man ofte falſe othes though byleue hym god dyſhonour ¶pauper ſoth thou may well wote god ſouerayne treuth bereth hym wytneſſe faſholde therfore worſhyp othe goddes name repreue falſhode deſpyte doth goddes holy name moreouer yf thou men ſwere blaſpheme goddes name name goddes name vanyte yf thou haue lykynge therin thou takeſt goddes name vayne thou rebuke repreue yf yu haue power ouer grutche ayenſt theyr ſynfull ſpeche ellys thou takeſt goddes holy name vayne herynge alſo yf thou haue lykynge errours ayenſt fayth holy chirche conſente ſhrewde tale vayne tale medled goddes name vnhoneſt ſpeche ayenſt worſhypfull name cryſte cryſtendom whiche ſpeche good cryſten man ne woman ought thou takeſt goddes name vayne herynge yf thou loue well thy god thou ſholdeſt paciently ony ſpeche ſowneth dyſhonour holy name yf thou louedeſt well ony man woman thou woldeſt ſpeche ſownynge ayenſte theyr name worſhyppe ne myght cauſes theyr offence velonye ſuche couenauntes whether touche theym take goddes holy name vayne grete deſpyte therto ſythen pea couenaunt made goddes holy name confermed alſo rede alſo holy wryte ioſue ix whan ioſue goddes people began fyrſte conquere londe byheſte people gabaon gyle ſente meſſagers ioſue make pea ioſue goddes people meſſagers gyle dyde olde clothes clowted olde ſhone patched torne toke hored brede theyr ſcryppes ſoure wyne theyr botels loded aſſes olde hored brede olde ſackes came ſo ioſue made preſaunt hym olde vytayles ſayd hym name ſpryngeth ferre wyde ther may kyng nacyon withſtande therfore come ſaluacyon lyues make pea ioſue people ſayd theym yf ye dwelle londe god hath gyuen v may pea make ioſue axed theym whens cam syr ſayd ben thy ſeuaūtes come fro full ferre contrees ſente fro lordes leders londe make pea thou may ſee arraye come fro ferre whan came clothes ſhone newe ben al torne al rente brede newe baken hored botels wyne newe botels nygh bruſten wyne ſoure vytales preſaunt haue brought ben nyghe loſte elde thus lyed almooſt euery worde deſceyued ioſue dwelleden xx lytyll myle then ioſue toke theyr preſaunt made pea prynces goddes people ſwore theym ſholde haue theyr lyues salomon ſayth spes que differt affligit aiam ꝓuer xiij hope deſyre longynge delayde tormenteth • oule man woman longeth thyng dyſeaſe tyll hath dyſeaſe longynge ſo reſte myrth eaſe welfare yt god hath heuyneſſe dulleth letteth maner lykynge ¶pauper therfore dauyd ſayth seruite dn̄o leticia serue ye lorde myrthe gladneſſe two thynges frende muſte kepte goddes ſeruyce good lyuynge ſadneſſe gladneſſe god gaue moyſes lawe mount synay toke hym x cōmaūdementes wryten two table ſtone fyrſte table wryten thre fyrſte cōmaūdementes whiche techen v ſholde worſhypp god loue hym aboue thyng therfore ben called cōmaūdementes fyrſt table worthyne sſe themſelfe wryten y• fyrſte table ſeconde table wryten vij cōmaū dementes techen v loue euen cryſten ſelfe ben called cōmaūdemētes y• ſeconde table ſo x cōmaūdementes ben cōprehended cloſed y• two cōmaū dement charyte fyrſt cōmaū dement charyte ye yu ſhalt loue thy lorde god thyn herte al thy ſoule al thy mynde al thy myght whan ſayth yu ſhalt loue thy god thyn herte excludeth maner ydolatrye yt forboden fyrſte cōmaūdement man ſette herte ne faythe ne truſte creature god ne ayenſt goddes worſhyp ſo loueth well hath kyndely truſte fayth hym loueth ſo truſteth truſteth mooſt comonly loueth mooſt therfore god badde yu ſholdeſt loue hym thyn herte yt ſaye thy fayth ſoo yu ſette thy fayth thy truſte hym byfore hym almyghty may beſt helpe nede therfore fyrſte cōmaūdement theſe thre applyed pryncypally fader almyghty alſo god byddeth yu loue hym thy ſoule ſaye ſaynt auſtyn ſayth thy wyll without contradiccōn thy wyll contrarye wyll alwaye confourmed wyll yt byddeth yt yu take name vayne yu haſte taken name cryſte art called cryſten ſo confourme thy wyll thy lyfe thy ſpeche y• wyll cryſte yu wyll thynge ne thynge ne ſaye thynge ayenſt wyll thy wyll thy wyttynge ne make none othe ne auowe ayenſt wyll wor • hyp tho thou haſte made worſhyp kepe hope ſykerly yf thou fulfylle goddes wyll erthe ſhall fulfyll thy wyl heuen loke thou ſpende thy lyfe thy beynge worſhyppe loue loueſt thou hȳ thy ſoule whiche pryncypally thy lyfe thy beynge therfore yf thou ſpende thy lyf thy beynge loue thou loueſt hym thy ſoule therto thou takeſt name vayne name qui eſt ſaye thynge taketh beynge hym therfore yf y• ſpende thy lyfe thy beynge ſynne vanyte yu takeſt name beynge vayne alſo loke thou ſpende thy wytte loue yu ſtudye knowe treuth cryſtus name ſayth ego ſum verytas ſo ſtudy flee falſhode folye helpe cryſte goddes ſone yt al wytty therfore ſeconde cōmaundement applyed y• ſeconde perſone trynyte yt ſone wytty alſo byddeth yt yu loue hym alle thy mynde without forgetynge benefyces gyftes mankynde byddeth kepe well holy daye whiche ordeyned pryncypaly men ſholde withdrawe thoughtes theyr mynde worlde thynke god heuenly thynges thynke theyr owne vnkyndneſſe goddes goodneſſe ſayd fyrſte therfore ſayth memento thynke thou halowe well holy dayes ſaye loue god thy thought al thy mynde thou wyll thynge thynke ayenſt pleſaunce thou haue lykynge thynke hym grace holy ghooſt whome thyrde commaundement applyed without whome ſaynt poule ſayth may thynke noo good thought fyrſte cōmaundement applyed fader almyghty may beſt helpe nede mawmettes ydolatrye may helpe ſeconde cōmaundement applyed ſone alwytty whoſe name treuthe ſouerayne wyſdome knoweth may dyſceyued treuth ſholde taken vayne alwaye worſhyped wyſely mayntened thyrde cōmaundement applyed holy ghooſt whiche called para • litus ſaye comforter holy daye ordeyned comforte ſoule bodye comforte man beſte holy ghooſt comforteth v ſorowe care bote euery bale gyueth reſte trauayll ſolace dyſeaſe abateth carefull thoughtes gyueth pea reſte herte therfore prophete ſayth hym cogitacio hominis confitebitur tibi et reliquie cogitaciones frende goſpell ſayth marci xij ye ſhall loue god herte ſoule mynde myght ſaye ſaynt bernarde ſayth ye muſte loue hym dulciter prudenter fortiter swetely wyſely myghtely swetely herte ſoule ye haue trybulacōn hongre ne thruſte hete ne colde lyfe ne deth ne creature ſholde departe v charyte cryſte yf loued hym ſholde loue ye ſhal loue god wt herte ſo ye loue nothynge hym hym ye ſhall loue hym ſoule ſo ye ſpende wyll affeccōn loue ye ſhall loue hȳ mynde ſo ye ſpende thoughtes loue ye ſhall loue hym myght ſoo ye ſpende myghtes loue ſo ye aſſente nothynge ne thynke nothynge ne nothynge
