cōmaūdemēt god techeth v fayth right byleue ſeconde techeth v hope ſayth prophete qm̄ ſperauit liberabo eum ꝓtegam eū qm̄ cognouit nomen meū hoped ſhal delyuer hym ſhall defende hym hath knowen name beatus vir cuius eſt nomen dn̄i ſpes eius et non reſpexit vanytates et inſanias falſas p̄o xxxix bleſſyd man whoſe hope name lorde hath taken hede vanytees ne falſe wytneſſes forſwere hym take goddes name vayne ſaynt poule ſayth ther name whiche may ſaued goddes ſwete name iheſus therfore haue goddes name worſhyppe may haue ſyker hope ſaued tho yt haue deſpyte ought grete drede thyrde cōmaūdement god techeth v charyte charyte good loue reſte euery wo trauayll loue maketh trauayll lyght eaſy ſholde elly • full vneaſy fyrſt cōmaūdeme charyte boūde ſhewe loue god herte worde werke therfore god byddeth ſholde loue hym herte ſoule mynde ſaye ſpeche ſpeche outwarde token thoughtes inwarde alſo byddeth v loue hym myghtes ſaye werkes ſo fyrſt cōmaundement fyrſte table techeth v loue god hert ſeconde techeth v loue hym al worde ſhewe hȳ loue ſpeche ſo loueth wel wyl ſpeke good worſhyp hym loueth gladde good name ſpeke hym good worſhyp ſory name deſpyſed dyffamed thyrde cōmaūdement ben taught ſhewe loue god dede leue owne occupacōns ye holy dayes gyue v pryncypally ſerue god occupyed hȳ nothyng loue worſhyp grete nede ſelfe ſo loueth wel wyl ſeke tyme ſpeke hym dele hym therfor god byddeth v halowe well holy dayes attende well hym occupye v hym dere loue made v nought bought v full dere precyous blood ſaueth v kepeth v gyueth v haue ony good fyndeth v al v nedeth moche yf loue hym maner myghtes dedes werkes halowe thus holy daye ſabbot hat boden v halowe ſholde gyue v ſabbot reſte heuen ꝓphete yſaye ſayth ſhall ſabbot ſabbottes y• ſaye endeleſſe reſt betokened temporel reſt ye holy daye moneth monethes ſaye endeleſſe myrthe betokened fygured temporell myrth holy daye yſaye lxvi amen ¶here endeth thyrde cōmaundement begynneth fourthe caplm primū diues thynketh thou haſte declared cōmaundementes fyrſte table full well parfyghtely mannes ſoule praye goddes ſake perfourme thou haſte begonnen wyll declare commaundementes ſeconde table may better knowe lawes god pleſauntly ſerue god kepe peaſyble charyte myn euen cryſten haue vnderſtanden ſeuen cō maūdementes ſeconde table ben knytte togydre ſeconde cō maūdemēt charyte byddeth v loue euen cryſten ſelfe ¶pauper mankynde hath two begynnynges fyrſte begynnynge begynner god ſeconde begynnynge begynner fader moder fyrſte cō mau dement fyrſte table caught worſhyp god aboue al thynges hym begynnynge v creature fyrſte cō maundement ſeconde table taught worſhyp fader moder ben begynnynge next god therfore ſayth fyrſte cōmaundement ſeconde table honora patrem tuum et matrem tuam ſaye worſhyp thy fader thy moder cōmaūdementes fyrſt table taught v loue god aboue thynge cōmaundementes ſeconde table techeth v loue euen cryſten ſelfe moche charyte mooſt ſhewed worſhyppynge helpynge euen cryſten therfore begynneth techynge worſhyp y• ought done theym owe waye charyte mooſt worſhyp god mooſt helpe fader moder therfore ſayth honora patrem tuum et matrem tuam worſhyp thou thy fader thy moder whiche cōmaundement ben bounden helpe bodely fader moder nede theym buxom meke flee theyr dyſpleaſaūce deſpyſe angre vnreſonably banne ne warye ne harme ne ſcorne none age none vnclene sſe wanteneſſe ne folye ſaye ſupporte theyr age febleneſſe ſupported v youthe holpe v kepte v febleneſſe whan coude ne myght helpe ſelfe fynde geneſis ix noe hadde thre ſones sem cham iaphet whan flood done happed theyr fader noe dranke wyne ſoo dronke knewe myght wyne byfore flood men dranke noo wyne ne ete noo fleſſhe whan noe thus dronke myddell ſone cham foūde hym lyggynge bare ſo yt myght ſee preuy membres anone laughed fader ſcorne wolde couer fader wente tolde brethern iapynge ſcornynge fader brethern wolde ſee nyce ſyght tourned theyr face frō theyr fader caſte clothe vpon hym couered hyw honeſtly whan noe awoke wyſte myddell ſone cham done hym wrothe wt hȳ curſed chanaan chams ſone ſholde come hym made hȳ thrall boūde sem iaphet theyr childern thus ſcornyng vn worſhyp ſone dyde fader began fyrſte boundage thraldome confermed god ¶diues sythen cham dyde y• ſynne chanaan whiche yet childe curſed noe y• childe chanaan cham y• childes fader ¶pauper noe wolde curſe cham owne perſone god hadde bleſſyd hym perſone brethern anone y• flood therfore curſed chanaan ſone hym ſone punyſſhed hym ſone ſholde come hym goddes dome right hadde done ſhame fader ſo childern ſholde ſhame ſhenſhyp hym noe hadde ioye hym ſo ſholde haue ioye childern ¶diues reaſon good rightfull ſaye forth ¶pauper therfore salomon ſayth oculum qui ſubſannat patrē et deſpicit partum matris ſue ſuffodient eum corui de torrentibus et demones prouerbio rum xxx eye ſcorneth fader deſpyſeth byrth moder rauyns brokes ſaye fendes helle brokes ſhal delue pyke eye therfore ſayth place honora patrē tuum et gemitus matris tue ne obliuiſcaris memento quo niam niſi per illos non fuiſſes et retribue illis quomodo illi tibi eccle vij worſhyp thou thy fader yette uot ſyghynges thy moder ne payne ſhe hadde whan ſhe bare bodye thynke theym thou haddeſt ben yelde theym theym dyde god badde hym ſelfe olde lawe ſoo curſed waryed fader moder ſholde ſlayne leuitici xx caplm ij diues many childern wolde ful fayne ſee theyr fader moder dede y• myght haue herytage lyue theyr owne gouernaūce oft whan may haue theyr good wyll ne theyr deth wyll haue plee mayſtrye ¶pauper suche childern full late ſhal thryue ſhal haue full lytyll ioye worſhyp owne childern moche ſhame ſhenſhypp salomon ſayth y• curſed fader moder dyſeaſeth theym lanterne ſhall quenched y• myddes derkeneſſes ſaye eyther ſhal haue ne ayer yf haue ſhal worſhyp herytage ſayth whiche childern haſten faſte maner ſhal want bleſſyng grace god laſte ende prouer xx place ſayth ſo withdraweth ony thyng fader moder ſayth noo ſynne wycked manqueller particeps homicidie eſt prouer xxviij alſo fynde ſeconde boke kynges xvc• abſolon ſone dauyd wolde haue putte fader dauyd kyngdom droue hym cyte ierlm barefote cam ſo ſodaynly hym dauyd fayne flee ſaue lyfe soone abſolon gaaf batayll fader felde god wolde ouercomen moche folke ſlayne ſwerde wylde beſtes abſolon fledde rydynge mule bare heded rode vnder oke heere full longe full fayre ſmote vp amonges bowes faſtened ſo mule paſſed forth rennynge abſolon henge ſtylle heer tyll ioab chyef captayne prynce ooſt dauyd came hym ſmote hym herte thre ſperes made hym forth ſtoned deth mooſt dyſpyteous deth lawe ſoo abſolon y• fayreſt man lyuynge haſte herytage wronge y• dyde fader loſte herytage lyfe alſo adony brother wolde haue ben kyng whyles fader dauyd lyued dauyd pryued hym kyngdome euer made salomon xi yere olde kyng afterwarne adony ſlayne wolde haue ben kyng ayenſt faders ordenaūce therfore god badde olde lawe deut xxi yf ther ony vnbuxom childe y• wolde obeye fader example whan yt yonge folke wexe rebelle ayenſt fader moder gyue ſuche ryot welfare ydleneſſe ben chaſtyſed withſtonde begynnynge ſhall aſhame comynte people robbery murdre manſlaughter euyll wycked goddes worſhyp holy chirche repreued tho men holy chirche ſo enfourme childern ſaye theyr fader moder may worſhyp god holy chirche coſte doo ſuſteyne theym ſelfe ſo make fader moder lyue myſchyef y• men holy chirche may lyue delyces caplm iij oonly cōmaundement god ben boūden taught worſhyp helpe fader moder alſo example kynde mayſtre telleth propretees whan ſtorke called ciconia latyn ſhe hath brought forthe byrdes flyght male female ben bycomen full feble trauayl bredynge bryngynge forth theyr byrdes ben ſo feble may well helpe theym ſelfe male female ſytten dyuer se tymes egges chaunge theyr trauaylle bredynge theyr byrdes fetchyng mete drynke ſelfe theyr byrdes therfore whan byrdes ben growen may flee fetche mete theyr fader moder neſte longe tyme trauayle • brynge forth theyr byrdes tyll releuyd may trauayle helpe ſelfe alſo telleth ther byrde called pellycane pellicanus ther grete enemyte bytwene pellycane addre addre wayteth whan pellycane hath byrdes whan ſhe neſte gete mete byrdes addre crepeth vp neſte ſleeth byrdes whan pellycane cometh ayen fyndeth • de ſlayne maner ſhe mourneth thre dayes thre nyghtes deth byrdes thyrde daye ſhe ſetteth ayen ouer byrdes bylle ſhe ſmyteth ſelfe ſyde ſpryngeth blood byrdes vertue blood ſhe rayſeth fro deth lyfe bledynge ſhe wexeth ſo feble ſhe may trauayle fede ſelfe ſome byrdes loue pyte put trauayle fede theyr moder ſome care oonly fede theym ſelfe whan moder amended waxen ſtronge tho byrdes helpeth ſhe loueth cheryſſheth wolde helpe ſhe beteth bylleth caſteth company caplm iiij diues cōmaūdement byddeth v worſhypp fader moder may without ony coſte lytyl trauayle may ryſe ayenſt knele take theyr bleſſynge ſpeke reuerence ſo kepe cōmaūdement ¶pauper cōmaūdement byndeth v worſhyp fad mod ſuche reuerence doynge alſo worſhyp thē helpe nede ¶diues fyndeſt yu helpe nede called worſhyp ¶pauꝑ fyrſte pyſtle yt ſaynt poule wrote byſſhop thymothee v badde ſholde worſhyp wydowes ſaye ſholde ſuſteyne theym goodes holy chirche called wydowes good ſuſteyned theyr owne yf ſhe childern fader moder wherof lyue badde ſhe ſholde lerne rule hyr huſholde helpe fader moder holpen ſame chapytre byddeth preſtes men holy chirche rule wel ſubgettes ſholde haue double worſhyp people ſaye gloſe peple ſholde obey reuerence fynde al theym nedeth namely trauayle prechynge techynge goſpell ¶diues folye whan folke age cūctis patron layfe may abyde four monethes preſentacōn college clerke patrone may abyde ſix monethes yf paſſe ther tyme retcheleſneſſe bryge byſſhop ſhall ordeyne yt chirche benefyce noo man ought naboth achab hadde ſixty ſones ten lyuynge deth byheded vengeaunce deth naboth iiij regnm x caplm viij alſo gylty manſlaughter defraude ſeruauntes theyr hyre therfore wyſe man ſayth taketh awaye fraudem facit mercenario ſunt tratres eccleſiaſtici xxxiiij therfore ſaynt iames ſayth thus falſe ryche couetouſe men see ye hyre werke men labourer haue reped feldes defrauded payde cryeth god ſugettes good enſamples gynynge helpe nede therfore cryſte ſayd twyes ſaynt peter fede lambes thyrde tyme ſayd fede ſhepe longe lambes gyue neyther mylke ne wolle whan theſe waxen ſhepe gyue bothe mylke wolle ſo cryſte wordes bad prelate curate holy chirche ſholde haue double cure poore people fede theym gooſtly alſo bodely bodely helpe nede bounde fede ryche folke gooſtly haue nede holy chirches goodes poore folke gyue tale pylle haue gette theym may ypocreſy fraude drede vyolence therfore god vndernemeth theym prophete ezechyell ſayth theym thus paſtoribus iſraell woo ſhepeherdes iſraell ſaye prelate curate holy chirche whiche ſholde ſhepeherdes goddes ſhepe ſoules cryſte bought ſo dere woo ſhepeherdes fede themſelfe poore people gyue noo tale ye ete ſayth mylke clothed wolle fatte ye ſlowe fede well wombe ye fede flocke people feble ye helped ne conforted ſore ſeke ye heled broke ye bounde ayen caſte awaye fordreuen ye fetched ayen ne ledde ayen peryſſhed ye ſought ferenes hardenes power without pyte ye commaunded theym many grete thynges greuous reygned amonges theym emperours ſo ſhepe ſcatered ſhepeherde gyueth ony tale ezechielis xxxiiij nother place ſayth wedded two wyues ſo departeth fleſſhe dyuer se wymen yrreguler vnable aulter therfore preſtes dekenes ſubdekenes aſtent preeſt makynge ſacrament muſte without ſuche departynge contrarye ſacrament endeles charyte onehede bytwene god holy chirche bytwene good cryſten people y• charyte alle one come togydre ſacrament reſon leful men holy chirche ſhed mānes blood ne ſlee ne mayme newe teſtament lawe loue therfore cryſte wolde yt mynyſtres auter ye newe teſtament ſholde mynyſtre ſacrament endeles loue endles mercy mankynde ſhewe loue mercy pyte token cruelte olde teſtament lawe drede dureſſe nygh ſacrefyces preſtes made done ſhedynge blood fygure cryſtus paſſyon alſo token yt yt ſynned worthy ſlayne beeſt ſlayne offered ſynne therfore ſwerde graunted preſtes mynyſtres olde lawe punyſſhe rebellours whan nedeth moche theyr offyce ſhedde blood ſo theyr offyce dyſpoſed crueltee ſoo moche afrede flee goddes ſone ther lorde ther ſouerayne ther god preſtes olde lawe cruelte ſlough cryſte god lorde therfore ſhedynge blood manſlaughter forboden preſtes newe lawe maketh vnable aultre ſhedde mannes blode helpe therto caplm xviij sheddynge blood men holy chirche ſo abhomynable horryble goddes lyght y• yf ony clerke dye batayl fyghtyng playes hethen men whiche foloweth ſhedynge blode deth playnge ſwerde bokeler ſtaffe twohandſ werde hurlebat tourmentes iuſtes clerke holy chirche ſhall make noo ſolempne maſſe ne ſolempne prayer hym ſholde buryed without ſolempnyte holy chirche xxiijq̄viij • cū que clericꝰ yf man woodnes rauynge ſlee man woman childe though woodnes paſſe yet yrreguler vnable goddes aulter xvq̄i ſi • inſaniens netheleſſe yf preſt caas falle hym whan wodenes paſſed hope ſeker helthe may ſaye maſſe alſo yf man ſmyte childe man woman waye chaſtyſynge dye y• ſtroke yrreguler xvq̄i si • nō iratꝰ et extra livde homicidijs ca p̄ſbiterū alſo yf doubte whether dye ſtroke ſhall abſteyne hym goddes aulter extra ead audiencia alſo yf preſt clerke ony man ſlee theef robbeth chirche yrreguler extrae ſignificaſti alſo yf clerkes fyght ayenſt ſaraſynes ayenſt hethen men yf ſlee ony man womē childe yrreguler yf doubte whether ſlough nay ſholde abſteyne fro y• aulter extraepeticio alſo y• iuge aduocate acceſſour offycere wytneſſe whiche man woman ſlayn wryter ſayth ſentence redeth dome examynacyon cauſe wryteth endytement lettres whiche man woman ſlayn yrreguler though cauſe dome ryghtfull rayliijtii yf man dryuen nede ſlee man woman yf fledde nede owne defaute fledde nede whan myght haue fledde full yrreguler yf ſuche nede yt myght flee nede cam defaute holy chirche ſuffreth ordres hath taken mynyſtre therin ſhall take none hygher ordre yf ony man ſlee man woman childe caſuelly myſhappe whether occupacyon lefull lefull yf dydde beſyneſſe flee manſlaughter full yrreguler yf occupacyon leful dyde beſynes flee manſlaughter though ſawe chaūges yt myght fall yrreguler rayliijtii hym ſleeth man woman childe wyllyngly hande tonge dyſpen sacōn ibm̄ yf man ſmyte woman childe whan childe quycke poyſon hyr wt venym yf yt childe deed born ellys born tyme dye yt poyſon ſtroke yrreguler yf childe quycke yrreguler ſhall punyſſhed lawe holy chirche manqueller ſo ſhall man gyueth venym ony drynke ony thynge let woman yt ſhe may conceyue ne brynge forth childern yf y• woman wylfully take ſuche drynkes ony mys crafte let hyrſelf ony berynge childern ſhe manſleer yf many men fyghte togydre one mo ſlayne knowen whome cō pany ſmeten came ſlee fyght though ſmeten manſleers alle came helpe manſleers though ſlough ne wyll ſlee come conforte helpe ſleer wrong ſyde yrreguler yf man wuman dye defaute leche vnkunnynge mys medycyne leche yrreguler therfore forboden men holy chirche gyue ony peryllous drynkes borne men ſurgery kytte often deth mayme tometh therof alſo mayme ſelfe without nedefull cauſe maymed men ther owne foly yf dyde theym gelde chaſte ſo pleaſe god yrreguler ther ſholde man ſerue goddes aulter ony greate foule mayme yf man withdrawe hym wolde ſaue man fro deth yf wyll hymſelf ſaue fro deth yf may namely yf longe hym offyce yrreguler hec rayliijtii yf ony clerke bere ony wood fyre ony mater brennynge ony heretyke yf deed therby deth haſted therby yrreguler though pope byſſhop gyue pardon helpen deth heretyke ſūma confeſliijtiq̄xxvquid de ill yf preeſt ſende yonge childe water horſe though bydde hym beware water childe ſendynge drenche preeſt yrreguler put ſo childe auenture ibidēq̄xxvij quid de preſbitero et hoſtilivru de homicidio quid de preſbitero ¶diues yf preeſt ſende childe erande bare legged bare foted euyll clothed froſte ſnowe yf childe dye colde take ſuche ſekene sſe colde dye therof preeſt yrreguler ¶pauper yes forſoth ought dylygence ſaue yt childe flee peryl whiche myght lyghtly fall weder ¶diues yf ony prelate ſende wetyngly ſuget bare legged bare fote ſuche weder euyll clothed yf dye yt colde taketh ſo ſendynge yt preeſt yrreguler ¶pauper yt ſleeth hym ſo colde yrreguler manqueller caplm xix diues saye forth thou wylt ¶pauper prelate holy chirche may fyght ne ſlee yet may ſtyre men armes people fyght fayth truthe goddes lawe holy chirche though men ſlayne therby yrreguler lawe ſheweth well xxxiijq̄viij igitur cum alijs • yf thou goo waye hym gooth ſlee ony man though thou counſeyll hym ceſſe purpo se wyll ceſſe thou go forth hym defende hym ſlee thou art yrreguler hoſti ſayth livrude homicidioq̄quid ſi quis yf clerke playne hym y• iuſtyce hym yt robbod good haue ayen good purſue deth though iuſtyce ſlee y• theef clerke yrreguler exepoſtu laſti • tua no sad vltimū yf clerke helpe take theef bynde hym lede hym iuſtyce wryte lettre take ony man yf theef ſlayn man ſlayn clerke yrreguler netheleſſe may calle holde theef tyl haue good holde hym hymſelfe yf crye holde theef crye theues theues yf ſemely hym yt manſlaught • ſholde folowe therof yrreguler yf ony man ſlayn ther yf hope therby haue ayen good without manſlaughter yrreguler though manſlaughter foloweth therof clerkes may bere wepen whan paſſe peryllouſe place afere theues ought ſmyte yf clerke leue ony man bowe arblaſt ony wepen fyght yf ony man ſlayne therwith maymed yt clerke yrreguler yf clerke erre anſwerynge mys anſwere folowed manſlaughter yf clerke holde wyſe man yrreguler though ſymple lettred erre ſo ſuche thynges yt ought knowe manſlaughter come mys anſwere yrreguler yf clerke ſaye le full ſlee theef ſlee lecherors ryſe ayenſt ther ſouerayns ſlee yf men folowe counſeyll ſlee yrreguler yf clerke bydmen ſtoppe theues mouth crye ſo lede hym ſlyly ſekerly iuge yf ſlayne clerke yrreguler yf men purſue theef ony man take hym aſke clerke yf ſawe ony ſuche yf teche wyſſe theym wetynge ſuppoſynge ſeke hym dyſeaſe hym yf yt man ſlayne clerke yrreguler yf haue fantaſye ſeke good yrreguler though man ſlee negyue coūſeyll ſlee yf ſuffre wetyngly ony thynge wherof ſemely come manſlaughter yf therof come manſlaughter yrreguler alſo yf counſeyll men take caſtell caſte engyne towne caſtell ſhote houſe walled townes caſtell men dwell yf ony man ſlayne therby yrreguler yf ony man counſeyll another man go ſlee ſlayne hymſelfe gaue counſeyll yrreguler though preeſt clerke coūſeyll men fyght ſaluacyon contre fayth ſoo byd ſlee yrreguler though ſlee byd put hymſelfe deth ſaluacōn contre truthe yf ony man wolde flee enemyes another man coūſeyll hym flee vpon truſte abydeth ſlayne gaue hym coū ſeyll yrreguler hope haue ſaued lyfe myght haue ſaued lyfe power frenſhyp truſte therof dyde hym abyde yrreguler yf preſumed moche hymſelfe retcheles kekynge gylous yrreguler yf ony man nede ſlee aduerſarye ſaue owne lyfe yf may elles wel ſaue hymſelf ſynneth ſo yt nede come folye yf foly brought hym yt nede ſynneth yrreguler hec ſūma • feſſo rum liijtii caplm xx diues meruayleth moche ſheddynge blood ſwerde ſo ſtraytly forboden men holy chirche rede goſpell cryſte bad dyſcyples ſelle theyr clothes bye ſwerdes whan ſayd qui non habet vendat tunicam ſuā et emat gladium lucexxij hath ſwerde ſelle cote bye hym ſwerde ¶pauper cryſte ſayd tho wordes apoſtles iudas traytoure byddynge hym bye ſwerde ſo ſhewynge ſaynge byfore wycked wyll wycked purpoſe iudas begge ſwerde come betray cryſte take hym whan iewes came ſwerdes ſtaues take hym goſpell ſayth ſholde haue ſwerde redye defende hymſelfe yf ony cryſtus dyſcyples wolde ſmyte hym therfore cryſte ſayd tho wordes plurell nombre many ſynguler one iudas alone purpoſe betray hym begge hym ſwerde drede knockes tho wordes cryſte bad hym begge ſwerde wordes vndern • hym malyce ſuche maner y• iudas ſholde vnderſtande none apoſtles cryſte wolde publyſſhe eyther diſcure hȳ y• apoſtles vndernam hȳ ſuche ſpeche iudas ſholde wyte cryſte knewe wycked purpoſe wolde dyſcure ſo ſhewed goodnes ayenſt malyce ſtyre hym repentaunce ¶diues anſwerde apoſtles ſayd domie ecce duo gladij hic lorde lo two ſwerdes redye lorde ſayd satis eſt ſuffyſeth ynough ¶pauper ſayd appoſtles vnderſtode ne cryſte ſayd tho wordes therfor wende moche folke weneth yet yt cryſte hadde bode theym haue bought ſwerdes fyght therfore anſwered maner began ſpeke ſwerdes fyghtynge cryſte dyſpleaſed ther ſpeche badde ſtylle ſuche ſpeche satis eſt ynough ſuffyſeth yt ye haue ſpoken maner ſpeche nomore mater therfore luke ſayth ſame place ceſſed ther ſpeche anone went cryſte y• moute olyuete ſame maner god ſayd moyſes prayed hym yt myght entre londe byheſtes sufficit tibi ynough yu haſte ſayd ſpeke nomore mater deu iij alſo god ſayd angell ſlough people sufficit contine manum tuam ynough withholde thy honde cryſte ſayd dyſcyples tyme paſſyon whan founde ſlepynge sufficit ynough ye haue ſlept awake ye made ende ſlepynge worde ſufficit ſuffyſeth ſoo made ende theyr vnkunnynge ſpeche whan began ſpeke ſwerdes worde satis eſt ynough ſaye ye haue ſpoke ynough mater nomore therof wyſte cryſte ment nomore wyſte cryſtement whan ſayd iudas quod facis fac cicius thou dooſt doo anone ſuche wordes cryſte vnd nam iudas euyll purpoſe yt ſholde amende hym yet cuſtom wt moche foke whan theyr childern ſeruaūtes ſpeke vnwyſely put ſylence theym ſtylle ſame worde ſaye ſone ynough thou haſte ſayd ynough ¶diues many clerkes ſaye whan apoſtles ſayd loo two ſwerdes cryſte ſayd ayen satis eſt ynoughe tho wordes cryſte graunted men holy chirche two ſwerdes bothe ghooſtely ſwerde bodely ſwerde ¶pauper erre apoſtles dyde vnderſtode ne cryſte ſayd tho wordes cryſte graūted neuer clerkes bodely ſwerde ſhedde blood forbad theym ſame tyme whan vndernam peter ſmytynge ſwerde badde hym put vp ſwerde ſhethe ſayth ſmyteth ſwerde ſhall peryſſhe ſwerde ſo proceſſe goſpell yf men vnderſtode well ſheweth cryſte hath forboden men holy chirche y• bodely ſwerde therfor ſaynt ambroſe ſayth ther armuer theyr fyghtynge ſholde bytter teeres holy prayer ¶diues yet contra te cryſte ſayth goſpell non veni pacē mittere ſed gladiū cam ſayth ſende pea erth y• ſwerde math x ¶pauper ſwerde yt place vnderſtande ſwerde goddes worde y• gloſe ſayth ſuche ſwerde man departed ſynne wycked company goſpell ſheweth well ſwerde ſynne ſlayn mane ſoule ¶diues sythen god forbad men holy chirche ſwerde ſheddynge blood manſlaughter ſlough ſaynt peter ananyam sapharyā wyfe hyr falſe couetouſe hyr leſynges actuū v ¶pauper lawe ſayth xxiijq̄viijpetrꝰ ſlough materyall ſwerde power god gyue hym myracles prayer reyſed woman dethe lyfe who name tabyta actuū ix wordes blamynge toke hyr lyfe ananyam saphyram prayed hyr deth onely vndername ther ſynne anone feldowne deed vertue ſwerde goddes worde peter ſpake holy gooſt peter ſaynt poule ſayth ſwerde goddes worde full often departeth y• ſoule bodye therfore worde curſynge vndernemynge holy men men holy chirche moche drede cllys ſuffraunce god anone ſaynt pater vndernam repented y• fende sathanas toke power ouer ſlough bodely ſlough fyrſt gooſtely ſynne falſe couetyſe caplm xxi diues lefull ony caas ſlee ony man woman vngylty ¶pauper caas lawe ſayth openly xxq̄v ſi nō ¶diues ſuppoſe queſte dampneth man iuſtyce knoweth vngylty ſhall y• iuſtyce gyue ſentence dampne hym ſythen queſte ſayth gylty ¶pauper god forbede falleth iuſtyce manſlaughter may lawe ſlee knoweth vngylty xxiijq̄vſi non ¶diues ſhall ¶pauper yf haue noo iuge aboue hym ſhall ſaue hym playne power yf haue iuge aboue ſhall ſende man hym tell hȳ • aa yt may playn power delyuer hym ſaue hym y• deth elli ſeke ſome waye ſaue hym ſhall gyue ſentence deth pylate trauayled full beſely ſaue cryſte deth wyſte hym vngylty moche cryſten iuge ought trauayle ſaue innocentes lyfe cryſte bought blode flee falſe ſentence pylate myght ought lawe haue ſaued cryſte pleaſe people drede yt ſholde haue accuſed hym emperour folowed ther wyll put cryſte deth therfore afterwarde dampned falſe queſte pylate wolde haue dampned hym yt wyſt vngylty drede pleaſe people dampned hym ſythen hethen lawe ſledth noo man vngylty moche cryſten lawe ſhal ſlee man vngylty iuge ſhall beſynes flee ſheddynge blood without gylte therfore made iuge deſcuſe ye truthe ſaue vngylty punyſſhe gylty lette malyce foly aud falſehode queſtes fals wytneſſes therfore god ſayth thus euery iuge thou ſhalt take voyce leſynges ne thou ſhalt ioye ne thyn honde ſaye fals wytneſſe wycked man ſaye thou ſhalt make couenaunt ſaye fals wytneſſe ne aſſent therto thou ſhalt folowe people wyll ony euyl thynge ony falſenes dome thou ſhalt aſſent ſentence many go awaye truthe exoxxiij therfore lawe byddeth iuſtyce lyght ne redy leue ne redy take vengeaunce dilxxxvi ſi quid etxiq̄viiij quam uisetxviq̄viij si quid ende euery dome ſhall iuſticia yt ryghtwyſnes englyſſhe ryghtwyſneſſe vertue ſtedfaſte wyll alwaye yeloe euery man woman ryght extra de ver ſignificacione ca fo rum gloſa therfore whan iuſtyce dooth wronge ſentence gyuynge noo ryghtfull dome endeth ryghtwyſneſſe wronge may man woman robbe hym lyfe ſlee hym without gylte therfor iuge ſleeth man woman vngylty wytytngly iuge tyraūt doth ayenſt lawes whiche ordeyned ryght euery man punyſſhe gylty ſaue vngylty therfore ſayth lawe iuge yf ryghtwyſneſſe hym non eſt iudex ſi non eſt eo iuſticia xxiijq̄ijiuſtū caplm xxij diues leful ony man woman ony caſe ſlee themſelfe ¶pauper caſe yt many reaſons fyrſte waye kynde euery man loueth hȳſelf beſy ſaue hȳſelf wt ſtande al thynge wolde deſtroye hym therfore ſynne ayenſt al kynde man woman ſlee hymſelfe alſo ayenſt charyte eche man bounde loue hymſelfe euen cryſten hymſelfe alſo doth wronge comonte mankynde phyloſophre ſayth v•o ethico rum euery man parte comonte euery mēbre parte bodye alſo mannes lyfe hygh gyft god gyuen man ſerue god god may take awaye whan wyll therfor ſleeth hymſelfe ſynneth ayenſt god ſleeth ſeruaūt ayenſt wyll thoughe god gyue man auctoryte ſlee man myſdede yet god gyueth man auctoryte ſlee hym ſelfe therfore ſayth lawe xxiijq̄vnon licet man ne woman ſholde ſlee hymſelfe neyther flee myſchyfe worlde ne flee mennes ſynne ne ſorowe one ſynne yt hath done ne go ſooner heuen yf ſlee hymſelfe lawe ſayth gooth endeleſſe myſcheef falleth ouer greuous ſynne yt ſleeth hymſelf falleth wanehope dooth deſpyte mercy god iudas dydde deth may amende hym yt greuous ſynne manſlaughter yt manſlaughter ſleeth lyf worlde lyf heuen blyſſe gooth deth helle without ende therfore ther ſholde noo woman ſlee hyrſelfe ſaue hyr chaſtyte ſhe defouled yf ſhe defouled vyo ence ayenſt hir wyl ſhe ſynneth ſaynt lucye ſayth y• tyraūt paſcaſius bodye defouled aſſent ſoule ye ſynne hym ſoo defouleth hyr leſſe ſynne fall lechery man woman ſlee hymſelf noo helpe ne ſholde man ne woman ſlee hymſelf ne mayme hymſelf drede yt ſholde conſent ſynne truſte god yt may kepe conſentynge lette occaſyons ſynne though man woman conſtrayned ſynne drede deth better fayrer yt ſlee hym ſlee hymſelf yt dampned euery lawe ¶diues contra te sampſon dyuerſe ſlough thē ſelf rede holy wryt ¶pauꝓ ſaynt auſten ſayth de ciuitate dei ſlough themſelfe preuy coūſeyll holy gooſt yt wolde ther deth myracles whan sampſon toke two pylers paynyms temple whiche bare vp temple ſhooke gydre armes tyl broſten temple fell downe ſlough many thouſandes hethen people gadred wondre sampſon deſpyte god heuen who ſeruaūt sampſon caplm xxiij diues whether ſynne ſlee ryghtfull man wycked man ¶pauper ſynne ſlee ryghtfull man yt ſleer noyeth mooſt hym whome ought loue alſo doth wronge hym haue deſerued ayenſt ryghtwyſneſſe alſo pryueth robbeth comonte manhode grete iewell euery good man good woman welle comonte mankynde alſo dooth deſpyte god good cryſte ſayth qui vos ſpernit ſpernit deſpyſeth deſpyſeth ¶diues contra yf good man ſlayn ſhal ſoone go heuen wycked man yf ſlayne vnwarly ſhall goo helle leſſe ſynne ſende ſleynge man heuen helle ¶pauꝑ saynt poul ſayth ad co rum iij euery man woman ſhall take owne mede yt trauayll therfore good man ſoo ſlayn ſhal go heuen good dedes y• malyce ſleer wycked man ſo ſlayne ſhall goo • helle owne wycked dedes wycked dedes ſleer ſleer ſhall goo helle bothe ſleynge good wycked ſhall depper helle ſleynge good wycked ſheweth malyce aggreueth god courte heuen ſleynge good y• wycked ſhall anſwere good dedes good man ſholde haue doo yf lyued lenger ſhall puny sſhed ſleynge wycked man yt ſleeth hym ayenſt goddes lawe letteth hym yt may haue tyme amende hym ¶diues lefull ony man ſlee wyf yf take hir auoutre ¶pauper ſlee hyr lawe cyuyle lawes ordeyne man woman done auoutre ſlayne lefull ſo loue ryght wyſneſſe clenneſſe hate ne auenged hyr lete hym well charge conſcyence yf ought gylty ſame eyther wyll dede take hede owne freelte thynke yt lawe well ordeyned punyſſhe yf amys punyſſhe woman ony man ſlee wyte owne auctoryte hyr ſlayne without lawfull iuge lefull goddes lawe thoughe ony londes lawe gyue men leue ſlee ther wyues ony caas holy chirche ſhall punyſſhe theym enioyne full harde penaūce mauſlaughter ¶diues whether ſynne man ſlee wyfe ſlee fader moder ¶pauꝑ bothe greuous ſynnes moche ayenſt kynde man wyf one fleſſhe one blood ought ſelden ſeen auoutrye therfore full ſclaunderous whan falleth harde punyſſhed men ſoo comon ther vnnethes ony ſclaundre therof wymen dare ſpeke ayenſt lecherye men men wyll ſpeke repreue lecherye man ſo moche gylty synne ſeldome falleth mooſt ſclaunderous yet caſe leſſe greuous ſynne often falleth mooſt vſe leſſe ſclaunderous yet mooſt greuous cuſtomable bolder men ſynne leſſe drede ſhame men haue ther ſynne greuous ther ſynne therfore ſaynt auſten ſame place ſpeketh mater ayenſt lecherye men ſayth thus peraduenture thy wyf hereth chirche prechynge leful take ony thy wyfe cometh home grutcheth ayenſt thy lecherye ſayth thou dooſt thynges lefull cryſten chaſtyre thou axeſte yelde thou iowe fayth thou oweſt fayth owe fayth cryſte though thou deſceyue thou deſceyueſt god whoos ſeruauntes thou deſceyue ste hym bought v bothe knoweth weneſt thou ſayth ſaynt auſten man wyl heled amende hym hyr wordes nay nay ſayth anone ſhall wroth ſhall wode wyfe prechoure curſe tyme wyfe came chirche trouthe theſe wordes ſaynt auſten ſame boke yet ſame booke ſayth thus peraduenture thou lechour wylt excuſe ſaye take none mannes wyfe take myn owne ſeruaunt wylt thou ſayth thy wyfe ſaye take none huſbonde take ſeruaunt god forbede thy wyf ſholde ſay ſoo better ſhe haue ſorowe thy ſynne folowe take wycked exſample thy wyfe chaſte holy woman true cryſten woman hath ſorowe thy lecherye fleſſhe charyte thy wyf wolde thou dooſt amys ſhe dooth amys ſpedefull yf ſhe kepte hyr chaſte dyd lecherye yu ſholdeſt lecherye yf thou dooſt lecherye ſhe ſholde lecherye yt good woman kepeth chaſtyte onely fayth yt ſhe ought alſo fayth ſhe ought cryſte though man amys yet woman gyueth hyr chaſte god therfor ſayth ſaynt auſten ſame place cryſte ſpeketh hertes good wymen within theyr ſoule ther huſbonde hereth worthy conforteth doughter ſuche maner wordes thou art euyll dyſeaſed wronges thy huſbonde hath praye y• haue pacyence ſory myſdede folowe hym amys muſt folowe goodneſſe dooth amys lete hym thy hede lede lete thy god thyn hede yf thou folowe hym hede ſhrewedneſſe hede body ſhall fall downe helle therfore myght bodye yt wyf folowe wycked hede myght ſhe holde hyr hede holy chirche cryſte hym wyfe ought hyr chaſte hym pryncypaly ſhe muſte worſhyp pryncypal huſbonde hyr huſbonde preſent abſent good woman ſhall alwaye kepe hyr chaſte cryſte hyr huſbōde pryncypaly ſhe ought hyr chaſte neuer abſent chaūge lyfe ye letcherous men ſayth ſaynt auſten fro then forwarde ye chaſte ne ſaye ye ye may kepe chaſte ſhame ſaye man maye woman dooth ne ſo chaſte womas woman ryght hath freell fleſſhe y• man woman fyrſte deſceyued adder chaſte wyues ſhewe ye may chaſte yf ye wyl theſe wordes ſaynt auſten caplm vi diues wymen may better chaſte men haue moche kepynge vpon theȳ lawe byddeth chaſtyte theyr huſbondes beſye kepe theym harde lawes ordeyned punyſſhe theym yf de amys ¶pauper anſwereth ſaynt auſten ſame booke ſayth thus moche kepynge maketh woman chaſte manhode ſholde make man chaſte woman ordeyned moche kepynge ſhe freell woman aſhamed hyr huſbonde amys thou art aſhamed cryſte doo amys thou art free woman thou art ſtrenger lyghtelyer thou myghteſt ouercome fleſſhe fende yf thou wylt therfore god hath bytaken thyſelfe woman hath moche kepynge hyr huſbonde dredefull lawe good norture grete ſhame faſtneſſe god pryncypall thou man haſte god aboue thy wyfe fleeth lecherye drede ſhame drede lawe good norture pryncypaly god theſe thou kepeſte thyſelfe chaſte neyther thou leueſte thy lecherye neyther drede god ne goddes lawe ne ſhame worlde ne ſhame thy wyfe thou art bounde true ne thou wylt leue good norture lyue harlotte vſe harlottes maners thou art aſhamed thy ſynnes ſayth ſaynt auſten ſo many men falle ſhrewedneſſe man ſoo greate men aſhamed chaſtyte lecherye manquellers theues periurers falſe wytneſſe rauenours falſe men abhomynable hated amonges people ſoo wyll lye woman bolde lechoure loued prayſed woundes ſoule tourne game yf ony man ſo herdy ſaye chaſte holde man theſe wordes ſaynt auſten boke de decem cordis ¶diues meruayleth moche ſaynt auſten alſo accuſe man ſoo moche lecherye put defaute man woman ¶pauper cryſte dyde ſame rede goſpell ioviij tyme whan cryſte ſatte temple ieruſalem techynge people lawes ſcrybes men lawe phareſeys brought woman newely taken auoutrye ſette hyr byfore cryſte ſayd hym gyle mayſter woman ryght take auoutrye lawe moyſes byddeth v ſtone ſuche ſayeſt thou ſayde gyle hadde bode ſtone hyr hadde ſayd ayenſt owne prechynge prechynge techynge full mercy pyte yf hadde ſayd ſhe ſholde haue ſtoned hadde ſayd ayenſt moyſes lawe wolde haue ſtoned hym therfore ſayd ne one ne ſtouped downe wrote fynger erthe whan hadde wryten whyle ſette hym vpryght ayen ſayd whiche without ſynne caſte hyr fyrſte ſtone afterwarde ſtouped downe wrote erthe whan accuſers woman herde theſe wordes cryſte ſee wrytynge aſhamed went eche eldeſte wente fyrſte none lefte ſaye theſe clerkes eche theym ſawe wrytynge euyll ſynnes done lecherye ſpouſebreche ony ſynne eche wende ſeen ſynne ſo drede ſhame went ſawe well gylty lecherye woman worthy ſtoned cryſte goodneſſe wrought ſoo eche theym ſawe owne ſynne none mannes ſo gyuynge v enſaumple hydde mennes ſynne defame euen cryſten whyle ther ſynne preuye whan gone drede ſhame ſayd cryſte woman accuſed man hath dampned lorde ſayth ſhe ſoth noo man hath dampned cryſte ſayd hyr ne ſhall dampne goo wyll ſynne ¶diues • lawe ſhe worthy deed wolde cryſte gaue lawe ſaue hyr ¶pauper though ſhe worthy dye yet hyr accuſers people brought hyr thyder worthy dampne hyr ne purſue hyr deth gylty woman therfore ſayth gloſe place though lawe byd ſlayne gyltye yet lawe wyll ſholde ſlayne gylty ſame ſynne vngylty ſame ſynne ſhall punyſſhe hym gylty therfore ſayth gloſe ſo accu sed woman ryght y• lawe muſte haue lete hyr go elli ſtoned hyr gylty yt ſynne woman ſoo lawe cryſte delyuered hyr ryghtfully ſaued hyr mercyably therfore ſayth lawe holy chirche tho gylty ony grete ſynne ſholde take accuſers ne wytneſſes dome man queller theues ne wycked iogulers robber chirches rauenours ne open lechours ne auoutrye ne poyſon folke ne periurers ne fals wytneſſes ne axe counſeyll wytches theſe ſuche vnable accuſe dome bere wytneſſe dome yf accuſe felowes helper ther ſynne ii q̄r conſtituimus et viq̄li q̄ crimen ſaynt ambroſe ſayth onely worthy domeſman dampne errours hath nought hymſelfe dampnable ſuꝓ beati imaculati etiijq̄vijiudicet therfore lawe putteth many caſe whiche huſbonde may accuſe wyf lecherye fyrſt yf gylty ſame xxxijq̄nichil iniquiꝰ alſo yf gyue hir occaſyon nycacōn withholdynge dette bodye xxijq̄vij si tu alſo yf ſhe defouled ſtrength grete vyolence ayenſt hyr wyl xxxijq̄v ita ne alſo yf ſhe wene yt hyr huſbonde deed xxxiiij q̄iſi ꝑ bellicā yf ſhe wedded wenynge yt hyr huſbonde deed whan cometh home ſhe muſte forſake ſeconde huſbonde go ayen fyrſte ſhe forſaketh y• ſeconde anone ſhe knoweth yt hyr fyrſte huſbonde lyue ellys ſhe falleth auoutrye hyr fyrſte huſbonde may accuſe hyr forſake hyr alſo yf ſhe deſceyued medle wenynge yt hyr huſbonde xxxiiijq̄ij lectū alſo yf knowe hyr lecherye ſuffreth hyr hyr ſynne meddleth hyr knoweth hyr ſynne forgyueth hyr recoū ſeyll hyr hym may accu se hyr xxxijq̄i si quis vxorem alſo yf hyr huſbonde put hyr doo mys extra liiij ti xiij diſcrecione alſo yf hethen man forſake hethen wyfe ſhe wedded hethen man tourned cryſten fayth bounde take hyr ayen ſhe felle ony fornycacyon withſtandynge ſhe knowen fleſſhely ſeconde huſbonde extra liiiij de diuorcijs ca gaudemus sſi ergo caplm vij diues man bounde forſake wyfe whan ſhe falleth fornycacōn ¶pauper eyther fornycacōn preuy open yf preuy may preued ſhall forſake hyr openly ne bounde forſake hyr preuely anentes bedde yf hyr fornycacōn open eyther ther hope amendement none hope amendement yf ſhe wyll amende hyr good hope amendement may lefull kepe hyr ſtyll yf ther none hope amendement ought kepe hyr ſtylle yf ſemeth yt conſent hyr ſynne ſūma • feſ liiiij tixxijq̄ vi q̄ro ¶diues may man owne auctoryte forſake wyfe yf ſhe falle fornycacōn ¶pauper anentes hyr bed may forſake hyr owne auctoryte anentes dwellynge togydre without auctoryte holy chirche yf forſake hyr company anent dwellynge without auctotyte holy chirche ſhalbe compelled dwelle wt hyr may anone preue hyr fornycacōn yf man medle wt wyf yt knoweth hyr fornycacyon yrreguler though cō cōpelled therto holy chirche ſūma • feſ liiiij ti xxijq̄viij vtrū vir yf huſbonde departed wyfe auctoryte holy chirche may yf wyll entre relygyon without hyr leue whether entre nay bounde contynence hyr lyfe may none wyfe haue longe ſhe lyueth deth departeth boūde wedlecke ¶diues contra yf man wedde woman may entre relygyon medle hyr ſhe may take huſbōde yet neyther deed ¶pauꝑ ther bodely deth gooſtly deth entre relygyan man woman dyeth ayenſt worlde yf medle hyr bodely onely bodely deth may departe ayenſt boūde wedloke yt medle hir bodely gooſtly deth entre relygyon may departe tyll whan medle togydre bodely boūde ther wedloke gooſtly therfore gooſtly deth breketh boūde moche leue frende huſbonde well boūde kepe fayth wyfe wyfe huſbonde therfore yf huſbonde treſpaſſe falle fornycacyon ſhe hath greate accyon ayenſt hym ſholde haue ayenſt wyfe yf ſhe dyde mys quia quo ad fidem matrimonij iudican • ad paria caplm viij heuen ¶pauper pyſtle ſaynt poule ſayth fornycaryes ne yt auoutrye ne ſodo mytes ne theues ne mawmetrers ne glotons ne wycked ſpekers ne yt lyue rauyn ſhall haue kyngdome heuen ad co rum vi chaptre ne falſe couetous man ſhall haue herytage y• kyngdome cryſte god therfor ſayth late ye fornycacyon ne vnclenneſſe ne auaryce named ne fylth ne foly ſpeche ne harlottre maner honeſte becometh ſayntes gyle ¶pauper many man hath deſceyued wycked wymen owne foly dyſceyte wymen many wymen haue deceyued malyce men euer men deceyued malyce wymen therfore woman lechour called ſnare fende yt hunteth beda ſayth mayſter ſtoryes ſhe dyſceyued fayre byheſtes falſe ſlye ſpeche behyght hyr ſholde dye goddes knowynge good euyll adam temptacyon outwarde ſymple worde wyfe profered apple fynde ſhe ſayd hym bodely one huſbonde huſbonde hath departed fleſſhe two wyues wyfe departed hyr fleſſhe two men therfore ther defaute ſacramēt matrymonye ſygnefyeth perfyghtly vnyte bytwene cryſte holy chirche many maner man falleth bygamye ſo yrregularyte fyrſte yf haue two wyues lawfully one knoweth fleſſhly alſo yf haue two gydre mo one lawe openly dome holy chirche lawe conſcyence knowe fleſſhely alſo yf knytte hym dede corrupcyon falleth dyd dede knyt hym matrymonye therfore ryght man yrreguler corrupte hymſelf whan weddeth weddeth woman corrupt ryght ſoo yf woman able holy ordre ſhe ſholde yrreguler ſhe corrupt ſhe knytteth hyr man corrupt ſhe corrupt byfore matrymonye reaſon may knot vnyte made bytwene cryſte holy chirche bytwene godhede manhede one one made euer therfore betokened bodely knyttynge gydre fyrſt matrymonye whan man paſſeth ſeconde wyfe weddeth alſo bodely yf ſhe corrupt gooth vnyte pluralyte therfore ſeconde matrymonye may fygure parfyghtly coniunccyon cryſte holy mayden ¶pauper wordes ſaynt poule thus vnderſtande may noo man preeſt yt hath two wyues bodely bygamus ¶diues yf man wene wedde mayde fynde hyr corrupt ¶pauꝑ yrreguler yf wedde mayde ſhe medle ony man hyr huſbonde medle hyr yt ſhe knowen thoughe huſbonde wyte yet yrreguler yf man accuſe wyfe auoutrye medle hyr yt one axynge wyues axynge yrreguler ſhe gylty ſhe gylty comon opynyon thoughe compelled holy chirche yelde hyr det bodye yf yelde yrreguler yf man wedde mayden ſhe dye mayden wedde another mayden knowe hyr fleſſhely yf knowe fyrſte ſeconde caſe yrreguler departeth fleſſhe two wyues ne goſtly auoutre lechery ¶pauper thre take one pryncypally called ydolatrye whan man woman withdraweth loue truſte fro god ſetteth creature god worſhyp longeth godhede dooth creature thankynge creature theym ¶pauper yt nede ſhe boūde gyue ſhall gyue thynke yt hyr huſbonde ſawe nede ſholde myſpayed rede fyrſte boke kynges xxvi ca ther grete nygard angry ſhrewe whoſe name naball good woman wyſe fayre wyf whoſe name abygaell tyme dauyd fled perſecucōn kynge saul lyued deſerte vi hondred men wt hym outlawes myſcheef ſent x men ryche naball praynge hym ſome almeſſe mete drynke naball deſpyſed dauyd meſſangeres called theues outlawes flemyd men wolde good gyue hem notwithſtandynge yt ſaued good beſtes y• tyme deſerte whan dauyd herde theſe tydynges wrothe came iiij hondred men ſlee naball longed hym happened yt ſeruaūt naball tolde wyfe abygaell dauyd ſent meſſangers naball deſpyſed theym anone abygaell without wyttynge naball charged aſſes brede wyne ſoden fleſſhe fyue ſhepe fygges reyſens vytales grete plente ſent dauyd hyr ſeruau te ſhe folowed happened mete dauyd comynge dauyd repreued hyr huſbonde naball vnkyndeneſſe ſayd ſholde ſlee hym longd hym yt good woman abygaell felle downe groūde worſhypped dauyd prayed hym audyence ſhe axed mercy hyr huſbonde naball excuſed hyrſelfe ſhe wyſte meſſangers whan prayde dauyd ſholde ſo venge hymſelfe taught hym moche goodneſſe prophecyed hym moche welth prayed hym wolde accepte hyr preſaunt ſo dyde dauyd ſayd hyr bleſſyd lorde god yt ſent daye bleſſyd thy ſpeche bleſſyd yu daye haſte letted fro ſheddynge blood venge myſelfe dauyd tourned ayen deſerte ſhe came home ayen foūde hyr huſbonde naball ſouper ſolemply nyght ſhe ſpake nought hym mater full dronken morowe whan ſobre ſhe tolde hȳ ſhe ſaue lyf anone herte dyed ſorowe wexe heuy ſtone within ten dayes dyed wycked deth dauyd wedded wyfe abygaell alſo yf man woman ſtele awaye mannes ſwerde whan wood lette hym manſlaughter hymſelfe doth theeft ne ſynne alſo cauſe ryghtwyſnes man may take awaye mennes goodes ayenſt ther wyll ryghtful batayle ſo yt fyght ryght fully ayenſt vnryghtful take ther goodes couetyſe ryghtfulne sſe ſhewe yt haue occupyed tho goodes wrongfully yf talke ther goodes euyll couetyſe rauayne though dede ryghtfull themſelfe caplm vij diues yf thynge loſte fyndeth kepeth ſtyll theeft ¶pauper fyndeth boūde reſtytuco n yf may wete whome longeth therfore ſhall men wyte fyndynge open ſpeche towne ſtrete chirche yt ought may chalenge yf man chalenge yt founde may auctoryte wyſe confeſſour kepe ſtylle yf poore nedy praye hym ought ellys gyue nedy maye praye hym yt ought ſoo make reſtytucōn therfore ſayth ſaynt auſten omelia yf yu haſte foūde ony thynge made reſtytucōn thynge yu haſt ſtolen ſayth god taketh hede herte honde therfor theeft done ſmale thynge well grete god charged thynge yt ſtolen wycked wyll ſteler ſaynt auſten ſayth ſaynt gregory therfore yf childern ther youth ſtele pynnes apple ony ſmale thynges anone perceyued ſholde harde chaſty sed begynnynge phylo sophre ſayth principijs obſta ſtande begynnynge vyces mycherye whan childern yonge begynnen haue lykynge mycherye though thynge ſmall value theyr ſynne leſſe ne ſynne ſuffre theym therfore goddes dome yt whan chaſtyſed ther youthe ſuche mycherye afterwarde ſtele gretter thynges hanged ſhame ſhenſhyp ther kynne therfore boecius de diſciplina ſcolariū telleth whan mannes ſone rome ſholde hanged prayed fader kyſſe hym bote faders noſe ſaynge thynke well fader token chaſtyſe better thy childern haddeſte thou chaſtyſed youth ſholde haue hanged therfore wyſe man ſayth qui parcit virge odit filiū ſuū c̄ ſpareth yerde hateth ſone loueth ſone chaſtyſeth hȳ techeth hym beſely prouer xiij rede tyme poore man tempted ete goo fleſſhe durſte ſtele drede hangynge daye mette fende bad hym ſtele goo ete ynough one dyd ſo ſoone ſtale oxe take ledde galowes fende mette hym ſayd hym wheder awaye theef ſayd fende woo worth wycked wyght yu haſte brought ende ſayd fende blame thou myghteſt ſee byll goo caplm viij diues ſuppoſe man haue borowed thynge lent hym taketh awaye fro hym preuely ayenſt wyll ayenſt y• couenau lenynge doth man theft ſo takyng away owne good ¶pauper doth theefth yt tyme fully owne good raymūde ſayth liij ti de furtis yf lord lady ony man betake ſeruaūt offycer ony thynge kepe take away fro hym without wetynge falſe couety se malyce endaūgere ſeruaūt doth theft though thynge owne yet frely owne longe ſeruaūt aſſent hath kepynge dyſpenſacōn therof ¶diues ſuppoſe mā weneth take owne good whan taketh mānes good ayēſt wyll yf take owne good vnlefully wenynge yt lefull ſo take dooth ony theeft caſe ¶pauper nay though caſe vnlefully yet caſe doth theft ne dedely ſynne yet boūde reſtytucōn theeft encludeth alwaye gyle falſenes wt whiche theft yf man take mannes good wyttynge yf haue iuſte cauſe wene yt ſholde myſpayed tho wyſte doth theft ne ſynne yf take mānes good wenynge yt wyll tho wyl yt take yet doth theft dedly ſynne goddes ſyght boūde reſtytucōn whan knoweth yt yt lordes wyll ne lorde may axe reſtytuco n ſyth wyl yf man woman mys eggynge take awaye mānes ſeruaūt doth theft yf man ſelle bye man woman yt fre gyuet hym taketh hym gyft ayenſthys wyl doth theft ſayth raymū vbi ſu • yf man woman take pryſoner tyme ryghtfull batayl fre therfor mayſter may gyue ſelle hym lawe armes wa • e hȳ lawe conſcyence charyte ¶diues yf man haue hyred borowed hors ony thynge certayn place certayn tyme paſſe yt place tyme ayenſt wyll ought yt thynge doth theeft ¶pauper yf ſo purpo se couetyſe ſome euyll cauſe doth theft yf falle ſodayne caſe whan cometh place hyred knewe caſe whan hyred thynge muſte nedes perfourme caſe ellys falle grete harme may take horſe thynge ferther lenger without theeft ſo may truly paye paſſeth fyrſte couenau ¶diues yf man lene awaye mannes good without aſſent hym whiche good lent vſe ¶pauper doth theft haue iuſte cauſe wene yt lorde yt thynge ſhal myſpayd yt lenynge vſeth mānes good ayenſt wyl lucre wynnynge frendſhyp yf man lene ony thynge vpon wed vſed wed without leue hym ought doth theeft ſaluacōn thyng yf vſe ſparyng owne good lucre fals couetyſe ayenſt wyll yt ought doth theft ſayth y• ſame clerke yf thyng ſtolen peryſſhe though y• thefe haue ꝓfyte therby yet boū de reſtytucyon muſte yelde good better whan toke boūde make reſtytuco n yt thynge y• profyte yt cam therof hȳ yt profyte ſholde haue come therof y• lorde tyme yt occupyed ayenſt wyl yf haue amended y• thynge yt ſtale may axe ayen ne withholde expenſes ſhal make reſtytucōn y• thynge worth whan ſtale better yf y• theef profre lorde couenable tyme place y• ſtolen thynge lord wyll receyue yf thyng yt myſhap peryſſhe lorde hath none accyon ayenſt theef y• lettynge reſtytucōn ne profyte myght haue come therof profred hym tyme byfore yf man haue ſtolen thynge boūde reſtytucōn yt thynge alſo value vſe ¶diues yf man woman bye open market thynge ſtolen wenynge ſtolen whan knoweth ſothe may axe pryce yt thynge hym ought withdrawe tyll haue payed hȳ moche payde therfore ¶pauꝑ reymūde clerkes ſaye nay therfor beware tyme loſſe alſo ſuſpeccōn theft lyghtly beggȳg ſtolen thyng myght take theef netheleſſe may ryghtfully axe payment hym ſolde hym whan hath reſtored lorde yt thynge yf ſpent ony thynge amendement yt thyng whyle kepynge may good fayth axe hym ought thynge without reſtorynge profyte yt yt thynge byfore wyſt ſtolen whan knoweth yt ſtolen mennes kepeth ſtylle couetyſe ony vnleful cauſe boūde reſtytucōn fro yt tyme longe kepeth profyte lorde yf thynge pery sſhe whyle kepe knowyng yt ſtolen good fayth boūde reſtytucōn yf ſolde awaye gaue knowe y• ſtelynge boūde reſtytucōn y• thynge y• profyte yf amended therby good lawe conſcyence yf man ſtele ryche negard vſurer ony thyng almes doth theeft quia nō ſūt faciēda mala vt veniāt bona xxxijq̄ iiij ſicut nō ſūt ſaynt auſten ſayth though gyue almeſſe yt hath taken ſtelynge excuſed theft putteth ſynne ſynne fyrſt ſteleth yt gyueth awaye maketh hymſelf vnable make reſtytucōn though man purchaſe moche good falſely almeſſe myſgoten good excuſed rauayne yf ſeller moche amended yt ſellynge byer moche apeyred ¶diues harde knowe y• ryght value thynge ¶pauper ryght value iulte pryſe thynge comon market gooth yt tyme ſo thynge moche worth may ſolde comon market tanti valet quanti vendi poteſt hec ſm̄ con liij tiviijq̄ietq̄ix yf man woman ſelle thynge good knowe defaute therin whiche defaute byer deſceyued doth gyle theeft alſo yf byer begyle ſo ſeller therfore god ſayd falſe iewes argentū tuū verſū ē ſcoriā et vinū tuū mixtū eſt aqua thy ſyluer tourned droſſe ſyluer falſe metall thy wyne medled water yſai • therfor yt begyle folke falſe moneye wyttyngly grete ſynne peryllous theeft alſo yf ſelle wyttynly falſe meſure falſe weyghtes therfore god ſayth thou ſhalt haue dyuerſe weyghtes leſſe bye ſelle leſſe ne yu ſhalt haue buſſhell leſſe buſſhell ne none falſe dyuerſe meſures thou ſhalt haue iuſte weyght true euen buſſhell true yu may lyue longe londe god ſhall gyue god hateth man dooth ſuche gyle hateth maner vnryghtfulneſſe deutro xxv alſo yf man woman ſelle ſeke thynge hole thynge wyttyngly begyle byer doth theeft boūde reſtytucōn though knowe yt defaute whan ſelleth whan knoweth yt defaute boūde make ſome recō penſacion ſayth ſame clerke ſame booke place q̄xi alſo yf ſeller ſelle better thynge weneth ſelle grete dammage hymſelfe yf ſelle golde laton yf ſelle good thynge ſmale pryſe wenynge yt lytyll worth yf moche harmed therby byer boūde reſtytucōn recō pen sacōn ¶diues ſeller holden telle byer defautes thynge yt ſelleth ¶pauper yf defau • preuy peryllous holden telle byer ſelle yt thynge better chepe yf ſelle haltynge horſe ſwyft horſe ruynous houſe ſtronge houſe peryllous harme byer bounde reſtytucyon yf defaute open though may ſerue ſeller may ſerue byer nedeth ſeller telle defautes bounde ſelle leſſe pryce ¶diues maye man ſelle thynge derrer bought ¶pauper ellys myght man lyue marchaū dyſe ne craft muſt take vp coſtes ſuſteyne hym meſure worſhyppe god holy chirche helpe poore nedy aſtate ende lefull nedeful chapman werkman ſelle thynge derrer bought therfore ſaynt poule ſayth noman holden trauayle owne coſtes comunyte neyther knyghthode ne chapmanhode ne werkmanſhyp falſe othes leſynges llye ſpeche begyle folke byeng ſellynge ſynne greuouſly holden reſtytucōn yf begyle ſo folke wyttyngly ¶diues yf two perſones betake thyrde perſone thynge kepe couenaūt ſhall delyuer theym gydre boūde kepe couenaūt ¶pauꝑ ye torſoth ¶diues yf delyuer one abſence without wyttynge ¶pauper doth amys yet neyther hem hath lawfull accyon ayenſt hym compelle hym yelde yt reſceyued ayen hath none accyon hym toke hym ayen yt hath none accyon ayenſt hym bounde hym without yt made couenaunt hym hath reſceyueth ayen thus la • • hoſtienſis ſū liiij rub de depoſito sicui detur v ſi vero caplm xi diues may man doo almeſſe euyll goten good ¶pauper salomon ſayth immolantis ex iniquo oblacio eſt maculata offerynge hym yt offereth euyll goten good ſpotted foule goddes ſyght yt offereth ſacrefyce poore mannes good lyke hym ſleeth ſone ſyght fader god yt hygheſt approueth gyftes wycked men ne taketh hede theyr offerynge ecc • 〈…〉 therfore salomon ſayth 〈◊〉 deum de tua ſubſtancia worſhyp thy lorde god thyne owne 〈◊〉 mennes good prou • iij tobye ſayd ex ſubſtancia • fac elemoſinā thyne owne good almeſſe tobie iiij ¶diues contra god byddeth goſpell men ſholde make theym frendes blyſſe heuen rycheſſes wyckedne sſe facite vobis amicos de mā mona iniquitatis therfor ſemeth lefull almeſſe euyll goten goodes ¶pauper thre maners thynge may euyll goten ſomtyme ſo mys goten muſte yolden ayen hym ought theeft raueyne viirye yf may founde ſoo mys goten good men ſholde none almeſſe yelde ayen alſo thynge mys goten whan gyuynge takynge thynge ayenſt goddes lawe gyuer taker leſe theyr ryght ſymonye therfore neyther may doo pleſaūt almeſſe good ſo mys goten alſo thynge mys goten whan dede crafte goten ſo vnlefull taker may kepe ſtylle lefully gyuer may axe ayen thynge goten lecherye ſynfull iapery yrregulers mynſtralles wytches ſuche whiche maner wynnynge called foule wynnynge turpe lucrū latine ſuche euyll goten good may none almeſſe ſholde make non open offrynge aultre ne ſacrefyce ſo mys goten good therfore god ſayth non offefres mercede ꝓſtibuli domo dnī dei tui • abominacio ē apnd deū thou ſhalt offre mede woman comon lechour houſe thy lorde god deutroxxiij offycers kynges prynces lordes ladyes byſſhoppes prelate take gyftes men comon cuſtome proufre y• ſholde mayntene gyue fauour theyr cauſes may almes goodes ſo goten though full ofte euyll goten xiiijq̄vnō ſane ſuche cryſte badde ſholde make frendes heuen rycheſſes wyckedneſſe ſaye rycheſſes ſo mys goten taketh hath ryght therto ¶diues prayſed cryſte goſpell falſe bayly ſo forgaue men theyr det fraude lorde haue thanke hem helpe nede forgaf one y• halfdele deth fyfth parte deth ¶pauper cryſte prayſed falſe baylye cryſte ſayth lorde prayſed hym fraude ſlyght dyde helpe hymſelfe ne cryſte telleth parable goſpell men ſholde take example fraude helpe themſelfe fraude robberye mēnes good teche men make theym frendes dedes mercy almeſſe forgyue men theyr dettes wyll god gyue ther dettes make frendes heuen wt rycheſſes worlde ¶diues called cryſte rycheſſes worlde rycheſſes wyckedneſſe ¶pauper ben moche fo • ke occaſyon moche wyckedneſſe moche dyſeaſe hate wrath enuye debate plee grete dyſcenſyon full harde gete kepe without ſynne grete dyſeaſe therfore ſaynt poule ſayth coueyte ryche worlde falle fendes ſnare wyſe man ſayth yf thou ryche worlde y• ſhalt vngylty ne clene ſynne alſo leue frende ye ſhall vnderſtande wyckedneſſe holy wrytte taken ſynne alſo payne dyſeaſe myſcheues worlde ſoo goodes worlde ben called rycheſſes wyckedneſſe ſay payne dyſeaſe myſcheef brynge men payne trauayle moche dyſeaſe men haue moche trauayle gettynge moche drede kepynge moche ſorowe leſynge diues diuicias nō ogregat abſ que labore non tenet abſ que nec deſerit abſ que dolore behote ſykerneſſe brynge folke grete peryll grete drede grete enmyte behote man haue luſte lykynge brynge hym endeleſſe hongre salomon ſayth couetous man hath neuer ynough auarus nō implet ur pecunia alwaye coueyteth alſo byhote man eaſe reſte brynge hym moche trauaylle nyghe trauayle worlde gete good cauſe ther ben called rycheſſes wyckedneſſe lawe ſaythxq̄i dilectiſſimis waye kynde al men ben euen lordſhyppes rycheſſes wyckedneſſe falſe couetyſe people men ben vneuen rycheſſe ſome haue moche ſome lytyll ſome ben ryche ſome ben poore god hath gyuen rycheſſe one man dyſpenſacōn gouernaunce many refrayne wyckedneſſe falſe couety se people wyckednes cauſe one man rycher therfore called rycheſſes wyckedneſſe ne hadde wyckedneſſe adam ſynne falſe couetyſe mannes herte el men ſholde haue ben euen ryche ben vneuen rycheſſe ſynne ſhrewedneſſe therfore goodes worlde ben called rycheſſes vneueneſſe wyckedneſſe iniquitatis nō equitatis therfore rycheſſes one man hath paſſynge another rycheſſes vneueneſſe vneuen euen cryſten therfore ben called rycheſſes vneueneſſe therfore god byddeth ryche men ben bayllyes reues worlde make frendes poore folke gyuynge forgyuynge bayllye dyd harde theyr ſugettes mercyable forgyue hem theyr dettes whiche ought god god ſo grete lorde ſo ryche ther may man hym fraude good ne hyndre ne leſe lordſhyppe caplm xij diues fyfth cōmaū dement thou ſaydeſt ryche men y• wyll helpe poore folke manſleers thou ſayeſt y• theues ſo ſemeth ayenſt cōmaū dementes ¶pauper y• poore man may dye ryche man holdeth good hym y• ryche man manſleer doth ayenſte cōmaūdement non occides yu ſhalt ſlee y• witheldeth good poore man nede theef dooth ayenſt cōmaundement non furtū facies yu ſhalt theeft y• ryche man hath paſſynge nedefull lyuynge aſtate dyſpenſacōn poore mānes therfore ſayth ſaynt ambroſe y• noo leſſe ſynne ryche man denye y• poore man helpe nede whan may helpe hym habondaū ce robbe man good brede ſayth yt yu withholdeſt ſuperfluyte poore folkes yt haue hongre waſte clothynge yt yu ſhetteſt vp ſuperfluyte poore wedowes moneye yt yu hydeſt erthe waſte raunſome pryſoners myſcheuous folke delyuere pryſon boundes helpe woo therfore ſayth wytte thou well many goodes yu art theef rauenour thou myghteſt gyue helpe poore folke yf thou gyue noo man ſholde ſaye ony thynge owne comon al ¶diues aſſent well thy wordes ryche men ſholde gyue almeſſe theyr habondaūce ſauynge aſtate theyr dyſpenſacōn full harde doo moche thynge nedefull ryche man poore bycauſe aſtate dyſpenſacōn mo thynges ben nedefull kynge erle mo erle ſymple knyght ſoo aſtates kynges prynces lordes nedefull haue treaſoure wage men armes defence realme wage theyr offycers gouernaunce realme ther lordſhyppe therfore emperour ſayd qui omni bus pree st omnibus indiget lorde dyſpenſacyon thynge worlde hath nede thynge ſoo lordſhyppe worlde nede ¶pauper therfor ſuche thynges ſo nedeful man aſtate dyſpenſacōn boūde gyue poore grete nede ſuperfluyte nedefull hym degre boūde gyue alwaye y• comon profyte ought charged profyte one perſone ¶diues ſemeth thy wordes men holy chirche whiche ſpende goodes holy thirche wycked vſe pompe pryde glotonye lecherye vanytees theues witholde poore mennes good ſpende myſuſe ayenſt wyll god poore folke ¶pauper ſoth ſaynt ierom ſayth yt clercles haue holy chirche goodes poore mennes helpe poore folke prȳcypaly holy chirche endowed haue benefyces goodes holy chirche longeth pryncypally gyue almeſſe haue cure poore people therfore ſaynt bernarde epyſtola ad eugeniu ſayth thus naked cry hongrye playne ſaye byſſhoppes doth golde brydels may put waye coldene hongre fro brydell yt ye ſo ſpende pompe vanytee ye take v cruelly ſpende vaynely pyſtle wrote chanon ſayd thus yf holy chirche boode ther ſhone boocles ſyluer vſe grete ſyluer harneys theyr gytdelles knyues men relygyon monkes chanones ſuche vſe grete ouches ſyluer golde theyr cope faſtene theyr hodes ayenſt hath ordeyned yt yt preche goſpel ſhal lyue goſpell prima ad co rum ix natheles frely yt man precheth ye mede thoughe axe people boūde gyue frely ſaynt auſten ſayth ſuꝑ illud producens fenū iumentis ſymonia ca dilecto filio caplm xviij diues payne ordeyned ayenſt ſymonye ¶ꝓauꝑ yf clerke ſymonyēt takȳg ordre ſuſpended ordre anentes hymſelfe anentes ſo yt may excecucōn ordre whether ſymonye preuy aperte ſuſpended yf conuycte byfore iuge ſhall depoſed vnabled euery worſhyp leſe moneye yt payed therfore yt ordred hȳ wyttyngly ſymonye gaf benefyce ſymonye yt reſceyueth ony benefyce ſymonye mene therto though theyr ſynne preuy yet ſuſpended anent ſelfe yf open ben ſuſpended anentes themſelf anentes yt taketh benefyce ſymonye muſte reſygne make reſtytucyon profyte yt hath take therof profyt yt myght haue taken therof tyme general rule ye lawe yt ſo occupyeth ony thynge ryghtfull tytle boūden reſtytucōn ye harmes al profyte yt cam therof myght haue come therof yt tyme ſauynge expen s yt ſpent profyt ſaluacōn yt thynge clerke lewed man yt doth ſymonye acurſed ye dede yf may preued yt lewde man ſholde acurſed openly holy chirche prima q̄i reꝑiunt ¶diues yf offycer ye byſſhop axe cuſtome ony gyft makynge ordres ſacrynge byſſhopes bleſſynge abbottes yf yt ſholde ordred blyſſed ſacred gyue theym ſuche gyftes cuſtome yt allege ſymonye ¶pauper yf gyue pryncypaly ſuche hyde open ſynne paryſſhen obſtynat ſynne recoū ſeyll hȳ yt wyll amende hȳ hate enmyte wyl recounſeyll hym wyll amende hym hate loue gyft prayer putteth ony man woman ye ſacramē te holy chirche yeres annuelers done raymunde ſayth et extra ne prelati vice ſuas et ca vltimo yf haue ſuffycyent lyuynge boūde ſaye maſſe dirige ſhall ſaye frely elles ſaye elles ſemeth dooth pryncypally couetyſe yf preeſt haue ſayd maſſe yf ſaye maſſe daye moneye haue thanke worlde doth ſymonye de con diiſufficit caplm xix diues yf relygyouſe ſeculer clerkes auaūſement theyr kynneſmen make couenau gydre ſaye ſymonye lawe ſayth abut dnis ꝑactio ceſſet omnis conuencio q̄ijqiii pro ſpyrytuell thynges euery couenaut ſholde awaye euery conuencyon ceſſe yf curate wyll burye deed bodye ne ſuffre buryed couenaunt good cuſtomes yf yt myght well pouerte extra e ad apoſtolicam yf preeſt wyll baptyſe haue moneye therfore doth ſymonye rather lewed man woman ſholde baptyſe childe gyue moneye therfore yf age ſholde
