man hope ye pryncypally haue mede god ytbyddeth leue whether borower paye paye god ſhall yelde mede ¶diues may lener axe thynge ye borower lenynge ¶pauper noo moneye ne thynge yt may meſured moneye neyther mete ne drynke ne clothe ne gyft honde tonge ne ſeruyce thynge yt may meſured moneye may axe loue charyte good wyll good frendſhyp lenynge ¶diues vſurye holden ſoo grete ſynne ¶pauper vſurer ſelleth togydre thynge yt leneth vſe thynge therfore vſure cometh ye ſellynge ye vſe vſurer ſelleth thynge yt leneth yt taketh ouer vſe thynge wherfore thou ſhalt vnderſtande many thynges ther may vſed without waſte deſtruccyon thynge mete drynke ſuche ſuche vſe maye departed thynge nedes graunteth thynge graunteth vſe thynge may ſolde ſondre ſuche thynges yf ſeller take vſe ſelleth thynge twyes ſelleth thynge nought vſe thynge full waſte therof ſuche ſellynge vſe called vſurye vſurer ſelleth thynge ſelfe vſe ouer thynges whiche vſe full deſtruccyon thynge vſe houſe dwellynge occupacōn therof ſuche lordſhyp thynge may graūted without ye vſe ye vſe without lordſhyp ſo man may take houſe yt leteth hyre ayen hym ouer take vſe houſe phyloſophre ſayth viij politico rum ye vſe moneye chaūgynge one helpe eaſe comonte whiche chaūgynge deſtruccōn moneye waſtynge maner chaūgeth thynge ſo ſpent awaye therfore vnlefull take ony thynge vſe ought comon ordeyned helpe eaſe therfore ſuffyſeth lener take ayen euen value yf take ouer vſe doth vſure boūde reſtytuco n ¶diues contra god gaaf leue iewes take vſure nacōns ¶pauper flee euyll el wolde haue taken vſurye theyr brethern couetyſe god forbadde graunted take vſure nacyons amonge ſpare theyr owne nacōn alſo gete ſo ayen parte yt longed ye graūt god al y• londe enhabyte wt hethen people longed ye iewes ye graūt god wrongfully ye hethen peple withelde moche londe fro caplm xxv lordes mylles lene moneye baker folke couenaūt ſhal grynde theyr mylles vſurye ſo let theym yt may grynde frely wyl yf harmed therby leners boūden make reſtytucōn yf harmed therby boūde reſtytucōn let theyr fredom ſomdele boūden ſame chapman ſelle creaunce let byer chapman bycauſe lenynge ſelle derer suche ſellers ben boūden reſtytucyon byer harmed hyndred yf lener ony man wyll gyue dettour lenger tyme paymēt whan may kepe daye aſſygned haue ſome gyft though axe gyft openly doth vſure yf chapman ſelle derer lenynge pryce ſholde ſelle yf payed anone doth vſure boūden reſtytucyon extra lieti conſuluit yf borower vpon vſure fayle daye payment y• borowe may paye moneye y• vſure lener dettour whome borowe paye hym ayen moneye vſure borowe none vſure wynneth nought therby ſo fleeth myſcheue ſholde elles falle hym yf man compelled borowe moneye vſure falſehede dettour wyl paye terme falſe dettour bounden make reſtytucyon det alſo vſure compelled paye falſehede el delyuer hym daūger yf yet paye extra liiijde fideiuſſori bus caꝑuenit et ca conſtitutus yf man woman lene x ſhellynges eeſter tyme reſceyue many buſſhelles whete myghelmaſſe whete better yt tyme moneye doubte reaſonably whether y• whete ſhall worthe leſſe tyme payment none vſure yf ſemely ſholde worthe tyme payment lent moneye hope y• lucre dyd vſure extra e ti nauigantiet ſū confliijtivij yf ſeller ſelle thynge pryce cauſe abydeth paye dooth vſure yf byer bye thynge leſſe worth payeth byfore thynge bought may taken hym doth vſure ibidem ſūma conf yf man lene ſyluer wyne haue ayen ſame quantyte certayn tyme hope yt ſame quantyte ſhall worth tyme paymēt doth vſure yf dettour wyl paye hym det byfore tyme flee owne harme wyll take hym tyme aſſygned payment ſo wynne lenynge dooth vſurye yf man lene moneye reſceyue certayn tyme corn wyne thynge • herfore ſhall take moche cometh therto tyme payment yf man lene moneye reſceyue maner moneye therfor certayn tyme wynne therby ſoo charge dettour doth vſurye yf man ſelle thynge certayn pryce market goth tyme y• ſellynge couenaūt y• yf better worth byfore ceſter ſhal paye ſo moche though leſſe worth ſhall paye leſſe doth vſurye yf byer bye horſe beſtis leſſe pryce worth tyme byenge reſceyue theym certayn tyme feyre vſure wene ſykerly ſholde ſo moche worth leſſe worth yf wene ſholde tyme worth vſurye caplm xxvi yf man let horſe oxe cowe hyre couenaūt • beſte dye appeyre hyreth ſhall ſtande loſſe halfe wynnynge yf amende doth vſurye ſemely ſholde haue moche profyte amendement beſte ſholde haue harme deth natheleſſe though letteth hyre make ſuche couenaūt hym y• hyreth hym beſy ſaue beſte doth ſynne yf purpoſe take though beſte peryſſhe without defaute yf gyle couetyſe doth vſurye therfor good flee ſuche couenauntes alle though entencyon good yet maner couenaunt ſemeth wycked ſclaunderous folke knowe entencyon natheleſſe hyreth thynge may lefully take hym peryll myſcheef thynge y• hyreth yf wyl yf man betake beeſt poore man hyre kepe couenaunt vtterly y• yf dye ſhall dye poore man lyue hym wyll haue good therfor wycked vſurye suche vſurers ben fendes charmours ſuche folke theyr ſhepe ne theyr beſtes ſhall neuer dye yf men tyme plente bye corne nedefull thynges pryncypally ſelle theym forth derer tyme derthe nede ſynne yf pryncypaly comon profyte ſaluacyon contree medefull ioſeph gouernour egypt dyde ſo ſaue people tyme hongre gen̄ xlvij alſo man maye ſo owne pſofyt flee myſcheef comyng waye prouydence though ſelle forth tyme nede helpe market goth doth ſynne yt yf witholde wyl ſelle forth tyme nede thyng y• hath paſſyng lyuyng kepeth ſtylle hope derth ſynneth greuouſly therfore salomon ſayth qui abſcondit frumentu maledicet populis bn̄dictio dnī ſuꝑ caput vendenciū prouerbio rum xi hydeth whete tyme hongre ſhall accurſed amonges people y• bleſſynge god vpon hede ſelle forth alſo may done comon ryght marchaundyſe wynne therby ther true lyuynge ſoo cauſe derthe ther byenge namely may bye ſo lefully y• haue wherby lyue ſuche marchaūdyſe yf auaryce compelle men bye men ther lykynge dere wyll ſynne greuouſly namely couetou se clerkes haue ynough el wherby lyue clerkes graunted ſuche marchaundyſe yf clerke bye beeſt thynge huſbondrye craft lefull hym amended put better degree byfore maye ſelle forthe lefully bought ſuche doynge called proprely crafte marchaundyſexxiiijq̄iij canonū gloſa et de condiv nunꝙ yf man lene olde corne haue therfore newe corne herueſt wyll take olde corne olde corne good good whan borower maye paye doth vſurye raymunde ſayth et ſūma confeſ vbi ſupra yf done pryncypally ſaue owne good el ſholde peryſſhe pryncypaly helpe neyghboure dooth none vſurye goddes lawe vſurye dampned emperours lawe mannes lawe ſome tyme ſuffreth good ne lefull flee y• euyll ofte men ſholde peryſſhe myght borowe vpon vſurye elles couetous ryche men wyl lene nedefull ſo lawe man ryghtfully ſuffereth good ende couetouſe man dooth vnryghtfully wycked ende therfor holy chirche dampneth y• lene vpon vſurye borowe nede good cauſe vpon vſurye whan may el borowe yf borowe wycked cauſe playe y• dyce ſpende glotonye lecherye pryde wycked vſe ſynne greuouſly though lefull borowe good ende vpon vſurye yet leful lene vpon vſurye ne counſeyll ony borowe vpon vſurye lefull cryſten man take hethen man ſwereth fals god yet lefull cryſten man axe hym y• othe ne ſtyre hym therto othe ſwerynge dyuyne worſhyp longeth verry god alſo notaryes make inſtrumentes vpon couenaūtes vſurye ben forſworne whan made notaryes make othe ſhall neuer make inſtrumentes vpon couenanutes vſurye ſoo yf make ony ſuche inſtrumentes ben forſworne may neuer bere wytneſſe ony cauſe ne make inſtrumentes ony cauſe ben made therby wycked name vnable euery fyce worſhypfull lawe euery dygnyte • ony prelate vnder wrytte ſuche couenaūt ſette ſeale therto wyttyngly gylty vſurye though haue wynnynge therby hec ſūma confeſ caplm xxvij diues payne ordeyned lawe vſurers ¶pauper vſurers lawe ben bounden reſtytucyon yf ben open vſurers ben accurſed lawe thre thynges ſholde houſeled ne holy chirche ſhall take ther ferynge ne reſceyue cryſten buryenge amende byfore theyr deth preeſt elles taketh offryng buryed ſhall make reſtytucōn y• taketh byſſhoppe helpe poore folke worthy ſuſpended offyce maſſe extra eti quia omni bus yf vſurer may make reſtytucyon muſte axe forgyueneſſe theym dettour yf wyll ſaued vſurer alſo heyre bounden reſtytucyon may compelled lawe reſtytucyon extra etitu no yf men boūden hym vſurye may reſtytucyon axe tyll haue made reſtytucyon bounde vſurye extra etiquia fruſtra ¶diues wherby ſholde men knowe open vſurer ¶auper kepe open ſtacyon open ſhoppe lene chaunge vſurye yf knowlege byfore iuge dome conuycte wytneſſe yf bere name vſurer dedes openly done accordynge name clerke vſurer heyre vſurer wyll make reſtytucōn ſhall ſuſpended wyll amende hym ſhall depoſed yf ſoo incorrygyble y• byſſhop may amende hym ſhall chaſtyſed ſeculer honde extraliijtide iudicijs cacū non ab homine clerke ſhall make reſtytucyon owne good yf haue wherof goodes holy chirche yf haue ought ſpent ſuche vſurye profyte holy chirche prelate reſceyue offerynge vſurer ſome clerkes ſaye ſhall take ayen vſurer repreef ſynne ſaye ſhall take byſſhoppe whiche ſhall take ayen vſurer yf vſurer may founden byſſhop ſhall gyue poore folke borower ſwere ſhall paye vſurer axe ayen muſ • e paye ſaue othe ſhall axe ayen may make denuncyacōn prelate holy chirche vſ • rye vſurer may compelled lawes holy chirche amende hym ſo make reſtytucyon yf ſwere y• ſhall neuer bewraye holy chirche vſurye boū den othe ayenſt ſaluacyon euen cryſten ayenſt cōmaundement god vſurer bye horſe londe without moneye vſurer gyue reſceyueth gyfte boūden make reſtytucyon yf wyſte ſoo bought gyuen extra ecū tu seruaūtes labourer ſerue vſurers honeſte thynges maye lefully take theyr hyre theym yf ſerue theym thynges nedefull ne lefull may take theyr hyre vſurer yf ſeruaunt borowe moneye vpon vſurye without byddynge mayſter though borowe nedes mayſter ony man borowe moneye vpon vſurye nedes without byddynge ſo boroweth bounden reſtytucyon yf vſurer wolde lene without vſure freely coūſeylleth hym lene vpon vſure boūde reſtytucōn letteth proufyte neyghbour yf iewe lene cryſten man vpon vſurye ſynneth may compelled prelate lordes make reſtytucōn extra e poſt miſerabilē lefull ony cryſten man woman take vſurye ony man cryſten hethen lorde college man ſholde ſuffre vſurers dwelle theyr lordſhyp ne lete theym hyre dwelle within thre monethes knowe theyr vſurye ſholde put theym neuer reſceyue ſuche vſurers yf byſſhop archebyſſhop doo contrarye ben ſuſpended ben leſſe degree ben accurſed yf doo contrarye college comontees falle interdyte yf ſtande ſtylle theyr malyce one moneth theyr londes ben interdyted lewde people ſuffre ſuche vſurers dwelle theyr lordſhyp theyr houſes ſholde compelled cenſure holy chirche put ſ • dm grego decimū et conſiliū lugdunenſe ti de vſuris ca vſura rum hec ſumma confe liijticodem alſo yf man ſelle thynge moche leſſe worthe couenaunt haue ayen tyme wyll paye pryce worthe vſurye byer getteth ayen payde moche therto yf man ſelle thynge x ſhellynges well worth xx ſhellynges ſhal haue ayen ſo byer wynneth vſure x ſhellynges ouer payed fyrſte caplm xxviij bvt ſuche reaſons many ben wryten falſe vſurers curſed god begyle robbe poore people ayenſt cōmaundement god ſayth thus yf thou lene poore people yu ſhalt therfore myſbede hym ne trauayll hym y• therfore ne ouerpreſſe hym vſurye exodixxij yf thy brod ſayth nedy poore feble take none vſure hym take noo thou gaue drede thy god thy poore brother may lyue thou ſhalt lene thy moneye vſurye ne axe hym ouer habondaūce take thou lenteſt thus ſayth god leuitici xxv non fenerabis fratri tuo • thou ſhalt lene thy brother vſurye neyther moneye ne corn ne ony thynge lene hym without vſurye thy lorde god may bleſſe euery werke yu haſte done deutxxiij ſo leneth euen cryſten without vſurye ſhall ſpede better lene vſurye ſhall ſpede worſe londe vſurye vſed openly londe ſhall myſfare therfore dauyd ſayth wyckedneſſe hath beſeged cyte y• comynte daye nyght aboue walles trauayle vnryght moche wronge y• cyte gyle vſure fayleth ſtre • e cyte die ac 〈◊〉 circūdabit eā ſuꝑ muros eiꝰ ini ••• 〈◊〉 ſuche vſurye gyle falſe othes byenge ſellynge prophete zacharye ſayth y• ſawe boke fleynge ayer yt • x cubytes longe x brede axed angell god myght y• angel ſayd hym curſe god y• gooth houſes theues mennes houſes yt forſwere theym name god zacharie v therfore salomon ſayth y• ſo gadreth treſours lyenge tonge vayne euyll herted ſhall ſtumble ſnares deth raueyners robberers wycked men ſhal drawe theym downe helle wolde ryghtfull dome prouer xxi ſuche god gyueth curſe w •• ſayth ioyne houſe houſe couple felde felde ſaye ryght wronge wronge y• ryght put lyght derkneſſe derkneſſe lyght bytter ſwete ſwete bytter yſayev theſe falſe men lawe ſlyght couetouſe folke mannes cauſe euer ſo good haue moneye ſtande hym ſhal ſaye wycked cauſe euer ſo clere ryght ſhal ſay full derke ſee none helpe therin neuer ſo derke y• man ſee ryght therin moneye ſhal ſay y• clere ynough euer ſo ſyker eaſy pnrſue ſwete ſelfe ſhal ſay bytter cauſe vnſauery dele wt haue moneye euer ſo peryloꝰ bytter moneye ſhal ſaye yt ſyker ynough robbeth euen cryſten ony good doth ayenſt iij lawes fyrſte ayetſt y• lawe kynde yt ſayth thus yu hateſt done yu alſo dooth ayenſt lawe wryten non furtū facies byddeth yu ſhalt theft alſo doth ayenſt lawe grace charyte y• pryncypall byheſt lawe grace byddeth y• men ſholde gyue theyr good take frō thē w • ongfully fynde holy wryt ioſue vietvijca achor ſtale golde ſyluer cloth ayenſt byheſt god wyfe childern beſtes ſtoned deth fyrſte afterwarde brente good yt xxxvi men ſlayne enemyes y• theft achor ſo ſtale ayenſt goddes byheſte god ſayd tyll whan thefte punyſſhed people ſholde neuer haue ſpede batayle ne iourneye ¶diues lytell wondre folke ſpede euyll theſe dayes warre vpon theyr enemyes go robbe pyle fyght ony ryght ¶pauper ſynne many ſpede full euyll ſo blent ſynne yt lyght grace whiche ſholde wyſſed ther dedes hyde awaye fro ſo wandre forth amonge theyr enemyes blynde beſtes ſene myſcheef tyll falle wyſe man ſayth obcecauit eos malicia eo rum sap̄ ij ther malyce hath made theym blynde grete clerke telleth solinus de mirabilibus mundi londe sardynye welle whiche welle yf true man drynke ſyght ſhall amende yf theef drynke therof though ſyght byfore neuer ſo clere ſhall wexe blynde welle vnderſtande plentee worldely goodes rycheſſes ye god ſendeth amonges mankynde whiche goodes rycheſſes comen erth newen yere yere water welle al true folke drynken welle ſaye comen truly theyr good rycheſſes worlde ſpenden well worſhyp god profyte theyr euen cryſten haue lyght grace ſee doo may pleaſe god falſely come goodes worlde theeft gyle vſure fals othes wexen blynde leſe lyght grace blent wt ther malyce therfore ſaynt ambroſe ſuꝑ lucā ſayth tyche sſes blame blame defaute theym wel vſe theyr rycheſſes rycheſſes ſayth lettynge vertue ſhrewes helpe vertue good folke y• ben wyll vſe well rycheſſes ¶diues drede nyghe nacyon hath ſoo dronken welle sardynye y• ben gooſtly blynde yf take hede theeft ſymonye regneth clergye theft vſure regneth pryncypaly amonge marchau te ryche folke theeft raueyne extorcyon regneth amonge lordes grete men mycherye robberye amonge poore comons alwaye enclyned ſlee robbe thynketh moche nacōn gylty theft ouerdone moche blent falſe couetyſe ¶pauper therfore god ſayth thus minimo vſ que ad maximū omnes ſequunt auariciā ppha vſ que ad ſacerdote cuncti faciunt mendaciū et ideo corruent fro leſte y• mooſt folowen auaryce falſe couetyſe prophete preeſt make leſynges gyle falſehede therfore ſhall falle ſhall gyue theyr wymen ſtraungers theyr londes theyr feldes heyres ieremie viij prophete yſaye god vndernameth gouernoures people bothe temporalyte ſpyrytualyte ſayth thus principe tui infideles ſocij furum et cetera thy prynces ben falſe felowes theues louen gyftes folowe medes yeldynge ayen demed ryght y• men myght paye yſa si videbas furem currebas cū eo et cū adulteris porcionen • yf thou ſee theef thou ranne hym helpe hym falſe iuges temporalte done theſe dayes lechoures auouteres thou puttedeſte thy parte iuges ſpyrytualte done theſe dayes ¶here endeth ſeuenth cōmaundement begynneth eyght capitulum primū diues full moche drede gyle falſehede ſhal vndo londe yu ſayeſt god mercy doo bote thanke myne herte thou haſte well enfourmed kepynge ſeuenth cōmaundement praye charyte yu wylt enfourme eyght commau dement ¶pauper eyght commaundement non loqueris contra proximū tuum falſum teſtimoniū ſaye thou ſhalt ſpeke noo falſe wytneſſe ayenſt thy neyghbour wordes ſayth ſaynt auſten ſaynt thomas de veritate theologie libro quinto god forbyddeth maner leſynges hydynge treuthe whan ſholde ſayd lawe ſayth qui tacet conſentire videtur ſtyll wyll ſaye treuthe whan ſholde ſaye ſemeth y• conſenteth falſeneſſe ſoo ſtylneſſe wytneſſeth falſeneſſe ayenſt treuthe ayenſt neyghbour ſynneth dedely tonge wyll vſe wytneſſe treuthe whan ſholde therfore ſayth ſaynt auſten bothe hydeth treuth y• lyeth ayenſt treuth ben gylty ayenſt cōmaūdement ſtylle wyll proufyte euen cryſten lyeth deſyreth harme euen cryſten epla ad caſulanū man woman boūden cōmaūdement harme neyghbour tonge therfore iohn cryſoſtome ſayth traytour treuthe lyeth ayenſt treuthe alſo ſayth frely treuthe y• ought ſaye frely defendeth y• treuth whiche ought mayntene defende ſo tho ſtylleneſſe enforce theym knowe treuthe yt knowe wyll aknowen due tyme lyers falſe wytneſſes natheleſſe leue frende ye ſhall vnderſtande ther thre maner ſtylne sſe one anentes god anentes euen cryſten thyrde anentes ſelfe fyrſte wycked whan ceſſe due prayſynge god thankynge benefyces ſeconde wycked whan ceſſe due maner techynge vndernemynge euen cryſten thyrde wycked ij maners fyrſte yf man woman drede ſhame pryde wyll ſaye thynge y• ſholde ſaye playne hym myſcheef ſeke helpe ſoule ſhryf • good coūſeyll bodye helpe good coūſeyll gnawynge fretynge hymſelfe inwarde wyll playne hym outwarde y• wolde conforte hym ſpeketh ſo moche inwarde without conforte tyl falleth wanehope ſhendeth hymſelfe angre inwarde ſorowe therfore ſayth ſaynt gregory li viij moraliū moche folke whan haue wronge ſuffren moche dyſeaſe inwarde wyll ſpeke outwarde ſayth yf ſayd peaſably theyr dyſeaſe outwarde theyr tonge ſorowe dyſea se ſholde paſſe theyr herte theyr conſcyence si illatas inquit moleſtias lingua tranquilie diceret conſciencia dolor • maneret somtyme men ſtylle deſceyte may bodely accuſe caplm ij diues many maner ben leſynges ¶ꝓauper saynt auſten li de mendacō putteth vij maner leſynges whiche ben comprehended thre quia ōne mendaciū vel ē ꝑnicioſū vel officio sū vel iocoſū euery leſynge ſuche y• doth harme called latyne ꝑnicioſū ſaye wycked englyſſhe ſuche doth good none harme called latyn officioſū profytable englyſſhe ſuche y• dooth neyther good ne harme called latyn • ocoſum bourdfull englyſſhe whan men make leſynges make folke mery fyrſte maner called ꝑnicioſū wycked alwaye dedely ſynne two maner leſynges ben venyall ſynne comon people men holy chirche relygyouſe ſholde folke perfeccōn ben dedely ſynne yf ben done auyſement cuſtome ſaynt auſten ſayth fyrſt maner leſynges done fyue maners fyrſte yf ony man ſaye preche teche ony thynge ayenſt ye fayth holy chirche ij whan leſynge harmeth ſome profyteth none leſynges bacbytynge fals wytne sſe ſynne y• comon lawe punyſſhed iij y• ſo profyteth one harmeth fals wytneſſe cauſe dette herytage ſuche iiij whan leſynge made without profyt without cauſe ſaue lykynge lye deſceyue cuſtome leſynges v whan leſynge made pleaſe flaterynge alle theſe maner leſynges ben forboden cōmaundement mener folke dedely ſynne leſynge flaterynge maye done thre maners prayſynge man thynge hath worthy prayſed prayſyng hym thynge y• hath prayſynge hym flaterynge hȳ ſynne ſhrewedneſſe folye maner flateryng yf done wyttyngly dedely ſynne ſecōde maner leſynge y• called officio ſū profytable done iij maners fyrſte ſaluacōn catel ſholde ellys loſte wyckedly theues yf wyſte alſo ſaluacōn man woman nocent ſought enemyes alſo ſaue man womā fro ſynne yf ſyngle woman ſaye y• ſhe wyfe kepe clene theym wolde defoule suche maner leſynges ſo auayle profyte alſo leſynges bourdfull ben venyal ſynnes ye comon people men perfeccōn ben dedly ſynne namely leſynges bourdfully whan ben cuſtomable vſe falleth men holy chirche relygyon iapers ne lyers falleth pryncypally flee ydell wordes cryſte ſayth goſpel men ſhall gyue anſwere y• euery ydell worde y• ſaye ſuche leſynges bourdful men perfeccōn tourne lyghtly leſynges ꝑnycyous wycked harme theym y• yt yt aſclaūdred theyr vanyte theyr leſynges thynketh ſoth men falſely lackynge hymſelf falſely ¶ꝓauper bothe ben foly caſe grete ſynne caton ſayth nō te collaudes necte culpaueris ip̄e prayſe yu thyſelf ne lacke yu thyſelf salomon ſayth laudet te alienꝰ et nō o tuū extraneꝰ et nō labium tua let man prayſe thyn owne mouth ſtraungers thy lyppes prou xxvij therfor comon opynyon clerkes ſynne man prayſe hȳſelf falſely auaū tement lacke hȳſelf falſely auaūtemēt cometh pryde yt worſt ſynnes lackyng hȳſelf may come lowneſſe medefully euery man hȳſelfe lacke prayſe therfore ſayth y• prophete omnis homo men dax euery man woman hȳſelf falſe lyer bere wytneſſe ben ſworne ſaye ſothe doo ayenſt theyr othe ſaynge falſe hydynge treuth thynge ſholde ſayd tranſpoſe thynges ſholde ſayd man ſaye thynge certayn ſyker though treuth yt ſayth alſo falſe vi diues may maner men bere wytneſſe ony dome ¶pauper nay bounde ſeruaūtes ſholde bere wytneſſe cauſes theyr lordes neyther ayenſt ne moche cauſe toucheth ſeruau te iiij q̄ iij criminali v item ſerui ne wymen ſholde bere wytneſſe preef cauſes felonye matrymonye cauſes purgacyon wymens euyll name may bere wytneſſe preef wymen may accuſe cauſes felonye alſo yonge folke within xiiij yere ne foles ne beggers ne ful poore folke ne hethen men ne cryſten men openly looſed falſehede one teynt falſe forſworen ne open wycked lyuers euyll name none theſe able bere wytneſſe dome byfore iuge v condicio ſexus eta diſcrecio fama et fortuna fides teſtibus iſta require falſe wytneſſes iewes ſlewe ſaynt steuen falſe wytneſſes ſlewe cryſte falſe wytneſſe true man naboth falſe wytneſſe wolde haue ſlayne holy woman suſanna god ſaued brought falſe wytneſſes ſame deth ſhe ſholde haue yf wytneſſe ben true lawe tyme yet many londes yf dyſheryte ony man woman doo hym leſe onythynge falſe wytneſſe ben bounden reſtytucyon alſo bacbyters forfet ayenſt cōmaūdement • hiche malyce bacbyten ben good leſynges dyffame •• ym alſo flaterers yt falſely prayſe y• wycked ſo fauour theyr ſynne ſo bacbyter bacbytynge good man flaterer prayſynge y• wycked man haue goddes curſe gyueth ſuche thus ſaynge qui dicunt bonū malū et malū bonū wo ſo ſaye good wycked wycked good yſaye v namely ben nyghe lordes grete men ben theyr gouernours ther counſeyllours confeſſours pleaſe flater theym neuer ſo falſe take none de god ne treuthe onely pleaſe ſaye nay ye treuth lorde wyll haue ſoo harden hym blynden hym folye suche flaterers lykeneth beeſt yt called cam • lyon whiche beeſt chaūgeth coloure thynges y• beſydes hym whyte blacke rede grene blewe yelowe ryght ſo ſuche flaterers chaūge theyr ſpeche yt hope beſt pleaſe ther lordes men ſpeke good man le lorde frende yf falle enemye hym anone ſpeke hym harme velonye ſo pleaſe lorde alſo ben y• mā ne enemyes preſence frendes ſpeke man good thoughe wyll hym good preſence enemyes ſpeke hym euyll fane ſteple torned wynde ſoo torne flaterers bacbyters theyr ſpeche companye ſpeketh ben moſell face camelyon lyke ſwyne ape eue • flaterer bacbyter ſwyne hath lykynge lye foule ſlough fayre grene wrotynge ſnoute defouleth place gooth ſo hath bacbyter lykynge ſpeke mennes defautes theyr vnhoneſtes ſynne ſpeke theyr goodneſſe honeſte wyſely ſpeche wrotynge vpon theyr defautes appere defoule theyr good name flaterer lyke ape ſeeth men wyll ſame flaterers rule theyr tonge treuth pleaſaunce ſpeche men beeſt camelyon though fayre whyle lyue yet ſoone deed ful foule ſayth mayſter kynde ryght ſo ſuche flaterers fayre ſpekers ye ſpeke well doo full euyll though ſeme fayre worſhypful worlde worlde theyr deth ſhall full foule fendes felowes helle payne amende y• ſpeke well therafter forfet ayenſt cōmaūdement denye theyr dedes treuth yt ſaye wt theyr mouth ſuche ſaynt poule ſayth y• theyr mouth knowlege themſelf knowe god ther dedes denye confitent ſe noſſe deū factis autē negant tite therfore god warneth folke ſuche falſe wytneſſes ſpeken treuth theyr mouth • nye dede ſayth thus omnia quecū que dicerint nobis facite ſcdm vero opera corde verba mendacij • haue conceyued ſtudye good enformacyon knowynge treuth owne herte contryuynge haue ſpoken wordes leſynge falſehede therfore ryghtfull dome tourned bacwarde ryghtfulneſſe ſtode ferre myght nyghe treuth felle downe y• ſtrete equyte myght entre treuth forgeten y• went awaye fro wycked thynge wolde haue lyued pea • treuth open pray falſe men qui receſſit malo prede patuit yſaye lix wolde god wolde amende theym ſaye wryten ſame chaptre lorde god ſynnes ben multeplyed fore ſynnes anſwere v grete ſynnes ben v accuſe v knowe wytneſſes haue ſynned lyed falſely ayenſt lorde god wyl preche ayenſt theyr vyces yf preche fallehede errour ſhewe theyr wyt curyouſt ſpeche preche hygh mater profytable people helpely mannes ſoule ſuche prechours ben called falſe wytneſſes alſo preche ſoo harde ayenſt mercy god brynge folke wanehope alſo preche ſo moche mercy god ſo lytell ryghtwyſneſſe make folke bolde ſynne ſuche prechoures ben falſe wytneſſes cryſte mercy medled ryghtwyſneſſe ryghtwyſneſſe medled mercy therfore dauyd ſayth vniuerſe vie dnī mia et veritas alle wayes dome lorde god ben mercy treuthe deus iuſtus et miſericors god ryghtfull mercyable wyll amende prechoures goddes worde ſholde wytneſſes cryſte ſouerayne treuthe therfore cryſte ſayth dyſcyples eritis michi teſtes ieruſalem • ye ſhall wytneſſes ieruſalem iurye samarye euery londe laſte ende erthe actuum therfore prechours ſholde auyſe theym well preched falſehede ne ſaye thynge certayne doubte hyde treuth y• ſholde ſayd theyr lyfe theyr techynge accorde techynge lyfe cryſte yf teche otherwyſe cryſte mynyſtres holy chirche namely men relygyon ſholde wytneſſes cryſte edyfycacyon people theyr neyghbours y• ben men wymen therfore men holy chirche ben betokened galaad ſaye hope wytneſſe al theyr lyuynge hert worde werke clothynge ſholde bere wytnes cryſte ¶diues ſholde men holy chirche bere wytneſſe clothynge cryſte ¶pauꝑ clothynge ſholde ſhewe ſadneſſe hone ste lowneſſe nygh folowers cryſte wytneſſes yt taught ſadneſſe ayenſt vanyte honeſte ayenſt glotony lecherye lowneſſe ayenſt pryde pouerte ayenſt couetyſe therfore outclothynge men holy chirche namely men relygyon ſholde ſtrayte ne ſhorte ſhewe ſhap theyr body pryde vanyte tempte wymen ne precyouſe ayenſt pouerte ne ouerdo ne feble ayenſt theyr degree honeſte holy chirche ne ſyde ne wyde ayenſt meaſure ¶diues mater thou ſpakeſt byfore coueyte therof yu ſothely ſaydeſt men holy chirche namely men relygyon paſſe grete arraye pompe temporall lordes ¶pauper alſo oft preeſt ſyngeth maſſe repreſenteth perſone cryſte yt dyed v vpon tree clothynge maſſe ſyngynge hereth wytne sſe cryſtus paſſyon ſheweth yt yt doth ſaynge maſſe doth mynde cryſtꝰ paſſyon yf haue mynde cryſtus paſlyon clothynge ſheweth ſholde falſe wytneſſe diſceyte neyghbour therfore ſaynt gregorye ſayth noo man doth harme holy chirche hath name ordre holyneſſe lyueth wyckedly nemo amplius nocet eccleſia ꝙ qui peruerſe agens nomen et ordinē ſanctitatis habet ¶diues betokeneth clothynge preſt maſſe ¶pauper amyt hede begynnynge betokeneth ye cloth yt cryſtus face hyled tyme paſſyon whan iewes hyled face bobbed hym badde hym arede ſmote hym longe aube betokeneth whyte cloth herode cladde cryſte ſcorne hadde ben fole fanon ſtole gyrdell betoken boūdes whiche cryſte boūden theef tyme paſſyon fanon betokneth boūdes hondes ſtole rope yt led wt deth gyrdell boūdes boū de pyler croſſe cheſyble betokeneth cloth purpure whiche knyghtes clothed hym ſcorne kneled hym ſayd ſcorne hayle thou kynge iewes byſſhop paſſynge preeſtes hath mytre croſſe mytre hede betokeneth ye crowne thornes ye cryſte bare hede mannes ſake therfore mytre hath two ſharpe horne token ij ſharpe thornes two tonges yt hange downe mytre betoken ſtremes blood yt ranne downe fro cryſtus hede pryckynge crowne thornes croſſe byſſhop bereth honde betokeneth rede ſpere yt knyghtes tourmentours put honde cryſte ſcorne ceptre archebyſſhoppes croſſe betokeneth croſſe cryſte dyed vpon v byſſhoppes gloues maſſe hondes betoken nayles cryſtes hondes ſandalyes foot maſſe betoken y• nayles cryſtes foot yf ſo yt men holy chirche hauyng theſe token cryſtes paſſyon theyr maſſe ſaynge haue deuocōn cryſtes paſſyon ne mynde paſſyon bere falſe wytneſſe inwarde token ſhewe outwdrde alſo amyt betokeneth ye baſynet helthe hope lyfe y• come forſakynge erthely thynges longe aube betokeneth chaſtyte bodye ſoule gyrdell fanon ſtole betoken cōmaundementes counſeyles cryſte goſpell whiche men relygyon holy chirche ben bounden paſſynge ſerue god • heſyble betokeneth holy cloth cryſte without ſeme wonne one whiche betokeneth parfyght charyte mytre byſſhopes hede wt y• horne betokeneth cōnynge two teſtamentes olde newe whiche connynge ought haue teche wt two tonges wt tonge dede tonge ſpeche ſhewe dede good example gyuynge ſpeche well techynge y• betokeneth two tonges hangyng behynde mytre ſame betoken two tonges hangyng behynde aube preſtes ſholder euery preeſt ſholde conne goddes lawe preche tonge dede good example wt tonge ſpeche theſe two tonges hange hygher byſſhop ſymple preeſt token y• byſſhop hyghly boū de y• tonges good example gode techynge ſymple preeſt ¶diues comon ſawe y• tho two tonges ye preſtes ſholdre betoken yt londe hath ben twyes renegate peruerted ¶pauper falſe ſyth londe toke fyrſte fayth y• people neuer renegat ye people londe ſlayne nygh vp fayth tyll ther cryſten man dwelle therin hethen people y• hath ſlayne cryſten people ye ſwerde kept londe y• wanne cryſten people therfor beda de officio diuino ſayh y• betokeneth two tonges y• men holy chirche ought haue haue ſayd therfor ben called tonges alſo y• preſtes crowne betokeneth crowne thornes cryſtes hede dygnyte preſthode ſha • ynge lawe ſayth betokeneth pouerte ſoule forſakynge worldely goodes caplm ix diues betokeneth byſſhoppes croſſe maner lyuynge ¶pauper ſayth grete clerke beda li de diu • officio byſſhops croſſe called ſhepherdes ſtaff ſtyre byſſhop lowneſſe thynke cure beſyneſſe charge taketh vpon hym whan made byſſhop bereth ceptre worldely dygnyte ſtyre hym pryde ne bereth ſwerde token cruelte bereth ſhepherdes ſtaff ſlee ne ſmyte ſaue ſheep y• ben ſuget • ſpyrytually whiche ſtaff aboue croked maner hoke drawe ayen yt wolde come ellys go awaye byſſhop ſholde pryncypaly trauayle drawe ſynful men wymen fayreneſſe good wordes good example mercy god fers • ne felle ſynfull therfore beda ſayth aboue hoke croſſe wryten thus cum iratus fueris miſericordie recordaberis whan thou ſhalt wroth thou ſhalt thynke mercy roūde knott byneth hoke wryten homo ſaye man byſſhoppe thynke y• man proude dygnyte byneth beſyde y• pyke yron wryten parce ſaye ſpare muſte ſpare ſugettes ſhewe grace wyll haue grace god token therof pyke croſſe ſholde ſharpe blunt deme y• byſſhop ſholde ſharpe alwaye medled mercy ſtaf croſſe ryght wronge token byſſhop ſholde deme ryghtfully gouerne ſugettes ryght equyte man wronge vnde verſus contrahe per primum medio regeparce per ymum theſe tokenes outwarde byſſhoppes pre • e wytneſſe themſelfe ſuche warde tokenes ſhewe yf ſuche falſe wytne sſes cryſte cryſtus lore dāmage theyr euen cryſten ypocrely deſceyue people ſothe leſynge ony man knowlege hymſelfe byſſhop preeſt clerke man relygyon werke contrarye thynges order ayenſt tokenes bereth holynes leſynge ony man woman ſaye hym cryſten ne lyue therafter cryſten man woman perauenture worſe iewe ſaraſyne panyme therfore ſayth ſaynt iohn epyſtle ſoo ſayth knoweth god kepeth cōmaūdementes lyer noo fayth hym prima iohis ij yt ſayth loueth god hate brother lyer io iiij ſo euery wycked lyuer lyer therfor ſaynt ambroſe ſayth maner bretheren flee ye leſynges louen leſynges ben childeren fende cryſte ſayth goſpell ſuche haue fende ther fader whiche hath euer lyer fader leſynges neuer ſtode treuth leſynge loſte mankynde cryſte hymſelf ſayth goſpell io viij yet daye vnnethes bryngeth ony man woman ſynne wt leſynges ſo wt leſynges ſleeth mannes ſoule woman euer hath cruel manſleer falſe lyer cryſte ſayth y• ſame goſpel ¶diues telle praye wytneſſes ſholde haue dome true wytneſſes ¶ꝓauper wytneſſes dome iuge alſo ſholde dyfferent partyes ſaye treuth partyes iuge may y• lawe take mede deme truly ne wytneſſe may lawe take mede bere true wytneſſe moche wytneſſe ought take mede bere fals wytneſſe ne iuge gyue vnryghtfull dome xiiij q̄ v non ſane netheleſſe wytneſſe may lefully take coſtes hym y• bryngeth hym wytneſſe yf man ſee y• neyghbour ſholde falle treuth leſe ryght defaut wytnes yf knowe treuth may bere wytneſſe cauſe bere wytneſſe ſaye treuth ſaluacōn neyghbour el ſynneth greuouſly though brought bere wytnes y• caſe men holy chirche may owen bere wytneſſe ſoo y• cauſe blood ne greuous ſynne yf man take mede wytneſſe boūde reſtytucōn caplm x diues whome ſhall make reſtytucōn ¶ꝓauper yf toke mede bere fals wytnes though bere true wytneſſe wytneſſe ſhall make reſtytuco n hym y• gaue worthy haue ayen ſyth gaf falſehede ſynne ſhall make reſtytucōn hym ayens toke hym wronge ſame maner ſhall make reſtytucōn yf toke mede bere wytneſſe ſtylle ſaye treuth yf wytneſſe take mede ſaye treuth ſhall make reſtytucōn hym y• gaue hym helpe right lefull hȳ ſo gyue lefull wytneſſe ſo take yf doubte ende gyfte gyuen ſhall make reſtytucōn gyue poore folke dome holy chirche hec raymundus li ij ti de teſti bus ¶diues many wytneſſes nedeful dome ¶pauper cauſe ſoo muſte nombre y• wytneſſes perſone perſones ben ayenſt whome wytneſſes ben brought ayenſt byſſhoppes preſtes ayenſt men holy chirche ayenſt perſones temporall dygnyte muſte brought wytneſſes worſhyppe ayenſt ſymple folke ¶diues ſo ¶pauꝑ ſholde man dygnyte neyther ſpirytual ne temporal true folke whoos treuth men ſholde gyue credence ſpeche ſymple folke whiche knowē wel treuth ne fals profytable comonte ne noyous ofte full lytyll dredynge god alſo perſones dygnyte ſoueraynes iuges gouernours people theyr ryghtfull dome ſomtyme vnryghtfull geten moche hate people without gylte ther good dede ſo haue many aduerſaryes power gouernour pleaſe nedes eyther muſte offende god ellys men dreden god therfore iuge ſhall lyghtly byleue fewe wytneſſes ayenſt ſuthe perſones alſo yf perſones dygnyte myght lyghtly dampned y• ſymple folke people ſholde holde ayenſt ther ſoueraynes lytyll let ſo dygnyte ſpyrytuall temporall ſholde deſpyte come nought therfor ſome tyme better ſuffre ſh • ewde prelate curate ſhrewde man regne lyghtly requeſte y• people depoſe hym ſynne well open well ſclaūderous noyous ¶diues ther ony caas whiche lefull ſtande one wytneſſe ¶pauper y• preiuoyce leful ſtande one wytneſſe yf doubte whether childe cryſtened chirche halowed aultre veſtymēt halowed alſo aſſent partyes men may ſtande wytneſſe one alſo men may ſtande y• wytne sſe preeſt ſeynge y• paryſſhen amended yf ſynne open vt dicit hoſtienſis ī ſūma li ij ru de teſti bus quotus eſt numerus alſo wytneſſe ſhall ſaye certaynte y• knoweth certayne ſaye doubte thynge hym doubte ¶diues ofce man weneth ſyker thynge deſceyued ¶pauper yf deuoure knowe treuth though deſceyued ſo ſaynge ayenſt treuth ſynneth dedely wyll bere falſe wytneſſe caplm xi diues man bounde kepe counſeyll thynge y• knoweth preuy tellynge ¶pauꝑ man knoweth ſhryft bounde kepe preuy noo wytneſſe therof knoweth goddes preuy mynyſter yf knewe onely ſhryfte waye tellynge ſhreuen hym therof yf ſuche grete harme comynte ony perſone boūde telle ſaluacyon euen cryſten ſauynge moche may perſone tolde hym ſoo beware harme tellynge yf ſuche harme comynte ne grete harme ony perſone yf haue boūde hym coūſeyll ſhal aknowe byddynge ſouerayne lawe kynde kepe counſeyll man knoweth coūſeyl yf kepynge coūſeyl ayenſt charyte ayenſt charyte may man bounden neyther byheſte ne othe dyſcouer counſeyll y• tolde theym counſeyll whan may lefully kepe counſeyll falſehede therfor wyſe man ſayth ſoo dyſcouereth preuytees frende leſeth fayth eccleſiaſtici viceſimo ſeptimo maner falſe frendes whan tourne enemytee telle preuytees theyr frendes ſhende ſayth wyſe man eccleſiaſtici ſexto wytneſſes muſte accorde thynge perſon place degree tyme yf one wytneſſe ſtande ayenſt many wytneſſes wytneſſe nought wryten ony inſtrument yf wytneſſes contrarye amonges themſelfe iuge ſhall deme partye leſſe partye paſſe partye worſhyp dygnyte good name ellys yf theyr wytneſſe ſemely treuth preue better theyr wordes partye y• muſt ſtande dyſcrecōn ye iuge y• ſhall atteynt wytneſſes muſte mo nombre worſhyp better name yf wytneſſes ben euen partyes nombre dygnyte iuge ſhall delyuer hym y• ſtandeth gylty mercy muſte pryncypall vertue iuge therfore ſayth ſaynt iames y• mercy enhaūſeth dome hec ſūconf li ij ti de teſti bus alſo ther wytneſſe dede dede withouten wytneſſe worde whan y• dede ſheweth ſelfe diſt xxviij priuſꝙ ther may man iuge wytneſſe accuſer togyder ſame cauſe caſe iuge may wytneſſe treuth excu se iiij q̄ iiij nullus vnꝙ euery dome muſte foure maner perſones iuge accuſer defendour wytneſſe ibidem cauſe felonye grete ſynne ſholde man wytneſſe ayenſt gylty borne wytneſſe ayenſt hym byfore ony dome token enemyte iiij q̄ iij teſtes item criminali wytneſſes ſholde worſhypful true ſadde ibidem suche folke ſholde wytneſſes dome knowe beſte treuthe xxxv q̄ vi wytneſſe one ſhall man ne woman dampned treſpaſſe ſo open dede ſheweth ſelfe iij q̄ iij teſtes et deutro xix et numeri xxxv man ſuffycyente wytneſſe owne cauſe xv queſtione tercia ſane fine item quarta queſtione tercia teſtes ſ item criminali poſt euery man may wytneſſe dome ayenſt hymſelfe hymſelfe quarta queſtione ſecunda defendour may forſake wytneſſes ben enemyes quarta queſtione terciateſtes noman may compelled lawe bere wytneſſe ayenſt owne kynneſman ne ayenſt ony nyghe alyaūce ibidem heretyke hethen man may bere wytneſſe ayenſt heretyke ayenſt hethen man helpe cryſten man ayenſt cryſten man ſholde bere wytneſſe xxiiij q̄ mirantur caplm xij vnable preſte ſholde bere wytneſſe ayenſt preeſt cauſe felonye grete ſynne ij q̄ vij ipſi apoſtoli bereth falſe wytneſſe forſaketh cryſte ſouerayne treuth xi qōe iij abijt yf preſtes dekenes taken falſe wytneſſe berynge ſholde thre yere ſuſpended theyr offyce harde penaūc v q̄ vi quis fine euery falſe wytneſſe ſholde vij yere penaunce xxijq̄vſi qi lawe vnable euery offyce laful dede ony worſhyp worthy leſe goodes beten harde chaſtyſed punyſſhed ſame payne worthy bryngeth men wyttyngly bere falſe wytneſſe xxijq̄vſi q ſe lawe ſayth ſholde faſte xl dayes brede water vij yere folowynge harde penaunce neuer without penaunce ſorowe contrycyon lynne aſſentynge falſe wytneſſe periurye ſholde ſame penaūce ibidē wordes wytneſſe ſholde taken beſte vnderſtandynge mooſte benygne extra liijti de teſtibus ca cū tu wytneſſe ayenſayth hymſelfe credence extra li ijtide ꝓbacionibs calicet men ſholde ſtande fyrſt ſpeche man woman ſayth cauſe yf varye tyme e ti per tuas yf wytneſſe dyſtraccōn ſaye amys leful hym anone amē de ſpeche yf abyde wt interuall though chaūge worde amende ſhall accept ne herde extra liijti de teſtibus cogendis ca preterea wytneſſe dome ſholde herde ayenſt hym abſent obſtynate wolde come extra de teſti bus caij ſayth fyrſte treuth muſte taken one wytneſſe eti omni yf man haue ſworne partye bere wytneſſe treuth partye othe vnlefull therfore withſtandynge othe may bere wytneſſe treuthe intumauit noo man ſhall bere wytneſſe cauſe yf haue ſame cauſe ony lyke ſpede hymſelfe ſuche perſone ſuſpecte wolde fauoure mannes cauſe haue hym fauorable hym cauſe eti perſonas noo mannes wytneſſe ſhall reſceyued dome preiudyce yf ſwere though wytneſſe man relygyon e ti nuꝓ honeſte worſhyp wytneſſes charge multytude e ti noſtra dyſcuſſe yrre gularyte bygamye lewde mā lewde woman maye taken wytneſſe e ti tam seke folke poore folke may compelled come byfore ye iuge bere wytnes iuge may ſende wyſe men wyt trenth e ti ſi • euery man woman ſholde hate falſe wytneſſe god hateth falſe wytneſſe salomon ſayth deus odit teſtem fallacem prouer vi aud euery lyer falſe wytneſſe full gyle ſodayne wytneſſe dyſpoſeth ordeyneth tonge lyenge y• redy bere wytneſſe byfore auyſed dyſpeſeth hȳ lye prouer xij salomon ſayth falſe wytneſſe ſhall vnpunyſſhed ſpeketh leſynges ſhall peryſſhe prouer xix ferthermore leue frende ye ſhall vnderſtande ther ben thre maner wytneſſes caplm xiij ther wytneſſe aboue v y• knoweth may dyſceyued god ſeeth ſhall daye dome v iuge wytneſſe ego ſum iuder et teſtis iuge wytneſſe ſayth lorde god ieremie xxix iob ſayth heuen wytneſſe knoweth coūſeyll aboue hyghe ther wytneſſe within v conſcyence ſaynt poule ſayth oure ioye wytneſſe conſcyence ther wytneſſe without v y• neyghbour creature y• ſhall bere wytneſſe ayenſt v dome byfore ye hyghe iuge amende v tyme deme wel ſelfe moyſes ſayd teſtem inuoco celū et terrā calle heuen erthe wytneſſe y• yf ye make ony lykeneſſe ymage worſhyp breke goddes lawe ye ſhall ſoone peryſſhe deutro iiij place ſayth thus calle heuen erthe wytneſſe haue ſette byfore lyfe dethe good euyll bleſſynge curſe therfore cheſe lyfe ye may lyue loue lorde god obeye voyce clyue hym fayth loue lyfe lengthe dayes herte tourned awaye hym ye wyll lawes worſhyppe falſe goddes ſaye byfore ye ſhall ſoone peryſſhe deutro xxx therfore leue frende yf wyll ſyker laſt dome come ſykerly byfore ſouerayne iuge knoweth muſte deme well ſelfe worlde ſaynt poule ſayth yf demed well ſelfe dyſcuſſed well lyfe ſholde dampned pri• ad co rum xi ¶diues ſholde deme ſelfe ¶pauper gloſe ſayth thou ſhalt thyne owne domeſman thy ſeete ſhall thyne herte ſet thy ſelfe gylty byfore thy ſelfe domeſman thy thought thy conſcyence ſhall thy two wytneſſes accuſe thy tourmentours ſholde drede ſorowe maner ſholde ſhe thy blood wepynge ſalt teeres whan wytneſſe thyne owne conſcyence thy thought thou haſte demed thy ſelfe gylty worthy come goddes borde ne heuens blyſſe ſayth gloſe ſekeneſſe febleneſſe ſodayne deth falle comonly eeſter amonges people men eeſter reſceyue vnworthely goddes fleſſe blood ideo multi infirmi et imbecilles et dormiunt multi ſ per mortē prima ad co rum xi euery man fauourable hymſelfe owne cauſe therfore thou ſhalt haue two aſſeſſours whoſe coūſeyll thou ſhalt deme thy ſelfe tho ſhall treuthe reaſone take treuthe thou make falſe excuſacyon thy ſynne ne lye thou excuſe thyſelfe ne excuſe thyſelfe falſely ne greuouſly thyne aſſeſſour reaſon wyll accorde yf tho two wytneſſes y• ſaye thy thought thy conſcyence ſuffyſe bere wytneſſe ne ful enfourme thy ſynfull lyf take thrydde wytneſſe thy fayth ſoo lete thy dome ſtande wytneſſe two thre fayth ſayth thus fides ſine operibus mortua eſt fayth without good werkes deed alle though byleue cryſten man thou lyue cryſtin man ellys thou art deed ſoule worthy dye without ende fayth fayleth worde thought deed helpeth blyſſe anone conſcyence mynde ſhall accorde hym ſaye thus vſeth amys free wyll dye reſon without remedye ſauynge goddes mercy take hede thy clergy may ſaue holy wryt clergye ſaye anima peccatoris mor • etur ſoule ſynner ſhall dye alſo thy clergy may ſaue yf thou dedely ſynne thou art bygamus twyus wedded fyrſte cryſte thy baptym fende aſſent ſynne ſo yu art wydowe fro cryſte wedded wydowe fende forſaken god pryde wedded begynnynge ye worlde ne truſte yu thy dome good contree yf queſt comyn x cōmaūdementes whiche thou haſt broken two cō maūdementes charyte ayenſt whiche yu haſte offended xij artycles fayth ayenſt whiche yu haſte erred vij dedes mercy whiche yu haſte fulfylled thy fyue wyttes whiche yu haſte myſpended foure cardynall vertues ayenſt whiche thou haſte treſpaſſed ſolempne queſte xl true wytneſſes ſhal dampne man queller thyne owne ſoule theef traytour thou haſte robbed thyne owne lorde good robberye called al maner myſtreatynge mannes good ayenſt wyll thou haſte robbed cryſte precyous ſoule bought dere blood myſuſed myſpente creature ayenſt wyll ſaynt gregorye ſayth omelye thynge take god vſe good lyuynge tourne vſe wycked lyuynge quicquid ad vſum recipimus vite vſu que conuert • mu culpe helthe bodye ſent v ſpende ſynne wyckedneſſe fayre weder vayne occupacyon pryde couetyſe pea vayne ſykerneſſe plentee vytayles glutonye lecherye ſo ſolempne queſte fourty wolde dampne gylty therfore ther none remedye truly deme thyſelf yelde gylty take ye mercy god punyſſhe thy ſelfe drede ſorowe herte put dome goddes iuge thy confeſſour make amendes dome aſſent god ayenſt yu haſte ſo hyghly offended wyll ſtande ryghtfull dome accepte ſuche ſatyſfaccōn aſſygneth y• lawe god yf thou good wyll caplm xiiij thus deme thou thyſelfe ſhalt thou ſyker dredefull dome whan cryſte brother verry god verry man ſhall come downe deme quycke deed ſaynt poule ſayth ſhall come downe voyce trumpe ſaye voyce angelles whiche crye reyſeth fro deth lyfe voyce cryſte daye dome ſhall arere v deth lyfe whiche voyce ſhall full dredefull y• lyue beſtely take none hede god ne lawe ſhall arreſt make ſtande ſtylle pryſoners erth abyde theyr iuge ſhall ſo charged ſynne ſhall wende vp ayenſt cryſte good ſhall wende vp mette cryſte y• ben goddes childern voyce ſhall full ſwete ful lykynge make ſoo lyght ſhall wende vp mete angellys ſo ſhall ſende ſory place ſory companye without ony remedye ther neuer thondblaſte ſo dredefull voyce ſhall theym y• ſhall dampned ther neuer ſonge ſo mery ne melodye ſo lykyng voyce ſhal ſhalbe ſaued therfore deme well thy ſelfe thou dampned stande ſawe grete queſte true wytneſſes whiche haue nempned deme thy ſelfe therafter true domeſman thyſelfe el yu ſhalt haue ſame queſte ayenſt hym wycked lyfte ſyde ſhewe theym croſſe ſpere nayles ſcourges garlonde thornes woūdes al freſſhe whiche ſuffered mankynde ſaye wycked wyſe ecce miſeri et ingrati quantum ꝓ vobis ſuſtinui propter vos homo factus ſum • see ye vnkynde curſed wretch ſuffered ſake whan god kynge kynges lorde lordes neuer wyſte woo ſake becam man ſake ſuffered beten bounde ſpateled deſpyſed nayled ye croſſe crowned thornes ſtongen herte ſpere ſlayne dyſpytous deth ye may ſee bye endeles deth raū ſom blood ſoules bought ſo dere ſeruyce ye ſholde haue done loue yt ye ſholde haue ſhewed loued aboue al creature loued dyde myne owne worſhyppe loue putte myſelfe ſorowe care ye loued lytyll mucke lytyl luſte • fleſſhe ye dyd ryghtfulneſſe lytyl nought wolde loue whan hongrye ye wolde fede whan thurſte ye gaue noo drynke whan naked ye hylde whan ſought myne harborowe ye reſceyued whan ſeke pryſon ye vyſyted therfore wende ye hen fyre helle without ende dwelle fende angelles ſayth ſaynt gregorye thou ſynfull wretche ſhalt thou flee may thou ne hyde may yu yf thou appere nedes thou muſt thou art ſhent thou ſhalt haue thynge ayenſt aboue thou ſhalt haue dredefull domeſman redy dampne y• ryght ſyde thou enforme ix cōmaundement ¶pauꝑ ix cōmaūdement nō ocupiſces domū ꝓximi tui exo xx thou ſhalt coueyte thy neyghbours good wt wronge houſe ne londe viij cōmaūdementes byfore god forbedeth wycked werkes theſe two laſte forbedeth wycked wylles conſente ſynne wycked wyll cometh euyll dede therfore cryſte ſayth ye goſpell yt herte cometh maner ſynne without wyll aſſente herte ſynne done de corde fleſſhe couetyſe worlde called couetyſe eye mennes good couetyſe fleſſhe called wylle lecherye glotonye ryght wycked wede clene clenſed londe whan rote drawen waye tylle whan rote drawen vp londe falſe couetyſe byddynge y• men ſholde put wycked couetyſe herte falſe couetyſe pryncypall letter kepynge goddes lawe rote al wyckedneſſe therfor cōmaūdement god forbedeth pryncypaly falſe worldely byheſte forbedeth maner wrongful deſyre mys couetyſe ony mannes good houſe londe golde ſyluer cloth corne ſuche thynges may ſtyre themſelfe cōmaūdement princypaly ayenſt falſe purchaſours yt falſe couety se ben beſy begyle wt falſehede robbe men houſe londe put theym theyr herytage ſuche falſe purchaſours god gyueth curſe ſayth thus qui cogitatis inutile et operamini malum cubilibus veſtris • woo thynke vnprouffytable thynge werke wyckēd thynge beddes morowe whan ye may ſlepe caſte gyle falſehede ayenſt theyr euen cryſten haue coueyted mennes f • ldes ſayth myght take awaye robbe theyr houſes falſly chalenge man houſe herytage often chalenge men boūde ſo entre theyr houſe londe haue theyr herytage goddes curſe michee ij alſo god gyueth curſe prophete yſaye ſayth thus qui coniungitis domum domui et agrum agro copulatis • woo falſely ioyne houſe houſe couple felde felde ende place yt ye may ſaye myne man hath ought within wene ye ſayth god ye allone ſhall dwelle vpon erthe falſe couetyſe ſayth ſowneth myne eeres therfor many fayre houſe grete ſhall forſaken man ne woman dwelle therin yſaye • nto thus wyſe man ſayth non attingas terminos paruulor rum • touche boūdes ſmall poore folke reue theym theyr ryght entre thou felde faderles childern put theyr herytage almyghty god ther nyghe frende ſhall make theyr full greuous full harde ayenſt prouer xxiij caplm ij fynde holy wrytte thyrde booke kynges xxi ca ther kyng iſraell hyght achab man dwellynge hym hyght naboth fayre vyneyerde yt laye nyghe kynges paleys therfore kyng deſyred gretly haue ſayd naboth gyue thy vyneyerde ſhall gyue better therfore ellys aſmoche moneye worth naboth ſayd god forbede ſholde chaū ge faders herytage wyll neuer chaunge ne ſelle kynge wroth malancoly layde hym bedde wolde lettres kynges name pryncypales cyte vnder kynges ſygnet badde gadre theyr courte gydre make ſolempne faſtynge ſo blynde people ypocreſye badde ordeyne two falſe wytneſſes whiche ſholde accuſe naboth ſaye yt ſpake euyl god kyng ſo dampne hym gylty ſtone hym deth ſoo dyd lawe yt ſo ſpake euyll god kyng curſed ſholde ſlayne whan ieſabell tydynges yt naboth ſlayne ſhe came kynge badde hym ryſe vp mery take vyneyerde hym naboth deed anone kyng roſe went vyneyerde toke hym yt byddynge god ely prophete met wt hym ſayd hym goddes name thou haſt ſlayne yu haſt yt yu coueyteſt telle forſoth ſame place yt hoūdes haue lycked vp blood naboth hoūdes ſhall lycke vp thy blood hoūdes ſhall ete thy wyfe ieſabell hoūdes bryddes ſhall ete thy bodye god ſhall deſtroye thyne houſholde ſlee thy kynrede thyn alyaunce ſoone fell ſo thus falſe couetyſe came periurye falſe wytneſſe murder manſlaughter deſtruccyon kyngdom rede alſo paſſyon ſaynt beatryce yt falſe couetouſe man who name lucre occupye ony thynge mys purchaced loke yt yu make reſtytucōn ſaluacyon thy ſelfe thyne here comon prouerbe de male queſitis vix gaudet tercius here euyl goten good thyrde heyre vnneth hath ioye caplm iij diues yf hadde ought purchaced mys ſelfe holde bounden reſtytucyon former faders purchace haue nought doo whether ryghtfull ryghtfull lefte wyll kepe good man naboth dyde thou ſpake full late ¶ꝓauper naboth wolde haue kepte uylle faders herytage longeth hym ryght dyſcente herytage yf thou kepe ony thynge wyttyngly thy former faders purcha sed falſely y• kepeſt thy faders herytage naboth dyde thou kepeſt mennes herytage whiche neyther y• ne thy fader ryght therfore thou make reſtytucyon yu ſhalt rewe thyne heyres achab dyd heyres whiche loſte onely y• myſgoten naboth murder gyle therto loſte theyr lyfe theyr worſhyp theyr herytage euer rede ther grete man whiche dyd moche almeſſe almeſſe god wolde haue hȳ ſaued byfell euenynge romed allone vnder wood ſyde place ther cam angel mā ne lykeneſſe bad hym go wt hym sodaynly togydre depe valey myddes valey depe pytt ful fyre ſmoderynge medled pytche brymſtone full foule ſtynkynge angell badde man loke pytt loked downe ſawe thre galowes ſtandynge fyre fertheſt henge man tonge ſeconde henge man hondes thyrde henge man angell axed hym ſawe tolde hym ſoth ſayd angell y• hangeth tonge y• thy faders fader whiche purchaſed place thou dwelleſt gyle tonge falſe othes leſynges periurye falſe wytneſſes dyd many men forſwere therfore pryncypally punyſſhed tonge hangeth tonge horryble fyre ſhall doo without ende wolde make reſtytucyon hangeth ſeconde galowes hondes thy fader whiche kepte ſtylle myghty honde fader amys purchaſed wolde make reſtytucyon thyrde galowe whiche hangeth man ben ordeyned yf thou amende make couetyſe nachor ſtoned deth ſtalle golde clothe ayenſt goddes forbode ioſue vij fynde lyfe ſaynt barlaam tyme archor toke nyghtyngale wolde haue ſlayne god gaue ſpeche nyghtyngale whiche ſayd archer ſhall profyte ſlee thou mayſt fylle thy wombe ſoo lytell saue lyfe lett flee ſhall teche thre wyſedomes whiche yf yu kepe well ſhall moche proufyte archer woūdred ſpeche behyght ſykerly let flee yf ſhe taught hym wyſedomes ſhe ſayd beſye take thynge yu myght take thynge loſt may recouered ne goten ayen make ſorowe thȳ ge ſemely ſoth byleue archer lete nyghtyngale flee whan nyghtyngale vp ayer ſhe ſayd archer feble coūſeyll haſte thou take yu haſte loſte grete treſour haue margery ſtone wombe oſtriches egge archer ſory prayed nyghtyngale come ayen hym hyght well ſayd nyghtyngale wote well thou art fole lore profyteth thou makeſt moche ſorowe thou haſte loſte yet yu myght gete ayen thou trauayleſte take thou myght take ne paſſe waye paſſe ouer yu byleueſt ſuche precyous ſtone body moche thy waye thy purpoſe yf thy waye purpoſe ayenſt pleaſaūce god waye balaam wende ayen ceſſe thyn euyll purpoſe yf de ayenſt pleaſaunce god dyſpoſe pacyence thanke god al take hede angell ſayd balaam yf ought contrarye god yf amendeth thrydde token y• aſſe fell downe vnder foot ſtrayt waye wolde ferther bere hym ſtrayt waye ſo narowe paas deth man may flee welth worlde lykened aſſe falleth downe grounde wyll lenger bere man vpon worlde paſſeth helth welth luſte fleſſhe therfore whan thou comeſt poynt take hede thy waye thy lyfe yf contrarye god amende y• euer thou wylt flee goddes ſwerde whele tourneth downewarde anone cometh age ſekeneſſe febleneſſe loſſe catell aduerſyte may ſaye regnaui haue reygned ſomtyme man whan lyeth deynge may ſaye sum ſine regno without kyngdome reygne kyngdome welth done alſo whele fortune y• one ſyde anone ſyde ben daye mānes frendes ſtande ſyde helpe hym next daye ſhall enemyes ſtande ayenſt hym wt aduerſarye whele ſpeketh dauyd circuitu impij ambulant wycked couetouſe folke go whele poſuiſti eos vt rotā et ſicut ſtipulā ante faciē venti lorde ſayth thou haſte put whele ſtoble byfore face wynde ſtoble whyle wynde bloweth wauereth fleeth aboue ayer hyghe lowe anone wynde paſſeth falleth adowne erth lyeth ſtylle ryght ſo proude couetouſe folke wauere worlde welth worſhyppe hygher lower ſtoble ſtrawe flyght kepeth certayne waye ſo kepe waye goddes lawe tyll laſte wynde paſſeth theyr bodye falle downe ther graue many pytte helle alſo worlde lykened ſhyp ſee ſaylynge ſhyp euer ſo grete hym ſelfe haue wynde hym wyll bere ſayle neuer ſoo hyghe go neuer ſoo yerne paſſed ther token went ryght ſo man neuer ſo grete worlde haue wynde mē ne mouth neuer ſo wel wt hym bere name prayſe flater hym though na • e ſprynge neuer ſo wyde bere hym neuer ſo hygh pryde ſo ſolempne ſo myghty y• man dare quycche ayenſt ne deed paſſed worlde ſoone foryeten men ſhal fynde token hym within fewe yeres vnnethes ſhall fynde one frende wyl ſynge maſſe ſoule goo chircheyerde yu ſhalt knowe bodyes ryche poore fayre foule wyſe foles free fro boūde torne erth aſſhes wormes mete ſtenche vnclenneſſe theſe grete kynges y• ſomtyme ſo grete name ben bycomen alexander iulius ceſar nabugodono ſor octauyan arthur kyng charles ſuche ben bycomen therfore may ſaye y• wryten boke wyſdom quid nobis ꝓfuit ſuꝑbia • profyted v grete pryde halpe v pompe grete rycheſſes paſſed awaye ſhadowe ſhyp yt paſſeth wawes ſee whiche paſſed men may fynde token sap v mannes lyf may well lykened ſhyp whiche ſtreyt narowe endes myddes wyde large ryght ſo mannes lyfe byrth begynnynge full ſtrayt ful narowe cometh worlde naked poore wepynge walynge vnmyghty vnwytty nought may ne helpe hymſelfe moche trauayle brought forth tyll lytell lytel cometh mānes age ſhyp lyf ſomdele wyde large myddell age hath mooſt myght wytte wyl anone ſhyp lyfe draweth ſtrayt ende anone cometh age febleneſſe ſekneſſe aduerſyte loſſe catell pouerte laſte deth maketh full ſtrayt ende whan dyeth wt bytter payne moche drede moche ſorowe gooth hen naked poore ryght cam bereth nought wt good dedes wycked theſe two ſtrayt endes ſayth iob thus nudus eg • eſſꝰ ſnm de vtero matris mee et nudus reuertar illuc naked cam moders wombe naked ſhall tourne ayen erthe moder yf man wyll ſtyre well ſhyp bote may ſtande y• myddes ſhyp ne former ende muſte ſtande y• laſte ende may ſtyre ſhyp wyl ryght ſo y• wyll ſtyre well y• ſhyp lyf worlde may ſtande y• myddes ſhyp ſet thought herte welth hath myddel age ne ſhal ſtonde y• former ende ſet herte ne thought byrthe ne begynnynge thynke moche kynrede ne alyaūce ſtyre pryde muſt ſtonde ye laſte ende ſhyp lyfe thynke deth laſte ende myſcheuouſly perylouſly ſhall wende hen wheder ne whan wote neuer maner ſhall beſte ſtyre ſhyp lyfe ſyker hauen heuen blyſſe therfore wyſe man ſayth memorare nouiſſimatua et eternū non peccabis thynke inwardly thy laſte thynges thyne ende thou ſhalt neuer ſynne ecclvij begynnynge euery dede thynke ende ende may haue may falle therof caplm ix alſo welthe worlde lykned floure ſoone fadeth falleth groū de roſo floure fayre ſyght ſwere ſmellynge ſofte handelynge ſo welth worlde fayre ſyght man lykynge hauynge ryght roſe wexeth alwaye amonges chornes gadreth roſes ware ſhal lyghtly hurte hym prycke hym ryght ſo welth rycheſſes worlde wexeth amonges thornes harde trauayle thonght b • yſyneſſe many peryls bodely gooſtely man hath moche trauayle getynge moche drede kepynge moche bytter ſorowe leſynge diues diuicias nō • gregat abſ que labore non tenet abſ que metu nee deſerit abſ que dolore whan man hath trauayled lyfe tyme gadre good haue welth worſhyppe worlde wyll ſoone welke tade falle awaye roſe sodaynly cometh moreyn beeſtes dye cometh aduerſyte loſſe catel laſte deth taketh awaye euery dele ſo wyll beſy gadre roſe worldely weth rycheſſes ryght ware ſhall hurte hym bodely gooſtly therfore ſaynt poule ſayth coueyte riche worlde falle fendes ſnare full harde temptacyons theſe cauſes ſaynt iames ſayth y• ryche man ſhall paſſe awaye y• floure graſſe heye whan ſonne ſhyneth hote heye welketh dryeth floure fadeth beaute paſſeth ryght ſo ſayth ryche man welketh fadeth wayes y• ſaye lyuynge iacobi alſo worldely welth lykened y• ſhadowe alwaye paſſyng lyuynge worlde paſſynge wantynge lyght heuen blyſſe myddes daye whan ſonne hygheſt y• ſhadowe ſhorteſt ryght ſo whan man weneth myddes lyfe hygheſt welthe pryde lyf ſhorteſt men dye ſooneſte theyr mooſt proſperyte y• nygher euen ende daye lenger mannes ſhadewe ryght ſoo theſe worldely couetouſe men lenger yt lyue whan ben theyr lyues ende thynke mooſt lyue lenger purchace houſe begyn plete tyll theyr lyfe paſſe ſodaynly awaye ſhadewe euen therfor mannes lyfe lykened ſlyder waye whan mar • goth ſlyder waye galeth ferther loketh fro hym ſooner harder ſhall falle bnt yf loke wel foot waye may kepe left though fall ſhall take grete harme ryght ſo fareth lyfe worlde ſo ſlyder yt ther myght neuer man ne woman paſſe wayt laſte ſlydeth ſekeneſſe myſcheef fell downe dyed ellys ſhall come y• ſame ende comonly whan men loke fertheſt fro ſelfe thynke lyue lengeſt begynne mooſt houſe purchas purpo se many ſhrewde tournes lyue mooſt welth delyces dye ſooneſt paſſe awaye ſodaynely ſhadowe euen example cryſte telleth goſpell lucexij ther ſayth cryſte ſome tyme ryche man hadde yere plenteuous crop londe ſo moche hadde houſes ynough laye thanked god gyft tourned hym proude couetou se thoughtes ſayd hymſelfe ſhall haue houſynge laye corn good ſhal deſtroye myn olde berne garnerys make newe lenger larger ſtuffe full good ſhall ſaye ſoule ſoule thou haſte good ynough many yeres take thy reſte ete drynke make feſte thought lyf worlde nought lyfe worlde anone god ſayd hym fole nyght fendes ſhall take thy ſoule ſhall goodes thou haſte arayed gadred gydre myght ſaye ſholde theyrs trauayled therfore caplm x clerkes treate kynde ſaye yt foxe wynter whan gooth ſeke pray yf come frollen water lyeth ere downe yce yf ony water rennynge vnderneth wyl paſſe ouer yce ſyker ſyketh hym ſyker waye thus wolde y• ſynful couetouſe men dyd whan go ſyke theyr pray fals couety se falſe purchace robbe begyle ony man good wolde layed theyr • eres yce thought freyle mannes lyfe yce cometh y• water tourneth ayen y• water ryght ſo came erthe ſhall tourne ayen erthe yf wolde thus laye theyr • ere yce ſholde water rēnyng ſholde ſay dyeth pope kyng prynce duke dyeth byſſhop knyght ſquyer ſholde ſoone dyeth ryche poore grete ſmalle yonge olde therfore holy wrytte ſayth omnes morimur et terram quali aqua dilabimur dye ſlyde erthe water ij regū xiiij therfor ſaynt bernarde medytacyon repreueth proude couetous folke worlde ſayth thus vbi ſunt amatores ſeculi qui nobiſcū ante pauca tempora fuerūt telle ſayth ben theſe lordes leders theſe proude gettours theſe falſe couetouſe men v within fewe yeres bycome ther thynge lefte aſſhes pouder wormes take hede ben men yu art ete dranke yu doſt led theyr dayes moche myrthe twynkelynge eye many ſanke downe pytte helle theyr fleſſhe gyuen vnto wormes theyr ſoule put endeles payne helpe theyr vayne glory ther pō pe theyr pryde theyr myrth theyr game glee theyr game many lytyll ſette welth worſhyp worlde well yt may haue helpe good deth fynde frendes true attorney ¶pauper moche better hath grace helpe hymſelfe byfore deth owne good one peny ſhal profyte byfore deth xx penys profyteth one candell byfore man xx behynd hȳ therfor ſaynt lucye taught moder almeſſe lyfe abyde tyll deth ſayd moder ye coūſeyll noo gyft full pleſaūt god whan man woman gyueth thynge y• may vſe hymſelfe therfor yf ye wyll yt god pleſed wt gyft gyue ye hȳ thynge y• ye may vſe ſelfe y• ye gyue dyenge therfore ye gyue ye may bere therfore moder whyle ye lyue haue helth bodye gyue god ye haue caplm xi whan man wyll hȳſelf whyle may though executours attorney nought hym grete woūdre eche man woman mooſt holden hymſelfe fareth ofte hem dyed theyr executours dyd one two fooles y• dwelled lordes courte one foole ſage naturell foole byfell daye came gydre kabehouſe whan folke ouen ouen glowynge hote ſayde foole ſage natural foole whether ouen hote ſemeth wyll aſſaye ſayd ye ſayd foole ſage whiche v ſhall go ouen fyrſte aſſaye ſayd naturell foole ſhall goo thou ſhalte haue bolle full water ſtande ouens mouth yf fele hete crye caſte caſte anone caſte water quenche fyre ſhall done ſayd foole naturell foole toke foole ſage bolle full water honde wente crepte ouen anone beganne brenne anone cryed caſte caſte whan foole ſawe foly laughed ſo enterely foly vnnethes myght ſtonde fete foole ouen cryed caſte man caſte brenne deth foole anſwered brēne yu yf brenne wylt dye yf thou dye wylt laugh ſo may caſte ſo foole brent deth ye ouen tho two fooles vnderſtaude men y• dye theyr falſe executours ben fooles executours ben grete fooles bynde theym helle payne theyr falſehede dye ben fooles truſte men themſelf whan ſhall crepe purgatorye hoter ony ouen take theyr executours bolle full water theyr honde ſaye golde ſyluer rycheſſes almeſſe almeſdede maſſes ſyngynge holy prayer refreſſhe theyr paynes kele fyre theym comonly whan haue bolle water theyr honde haue goodes theyr wyll laugh ſo make ſo mery fare ſo well goodes deed may thynge caſt full loth forgo ony goodes therwhyles y• ſynfull ſoule lyeth purgatory ſuffreth ful moche wo cryeth helpe nyght daye ſayenge maner miſeremini mei miſeremini mei ſaltē vos amici mei qr manꝰ dnī tetigit iob xix haue ye mercy haue ye mercy namely ye frendes y• honde god full harde hath touched whan fynde helpe y• ſholde helpe axe vengeaūce nyght daye grete clerke turpinꝰ de geſt • karoli telleth yt kyng charles wt hym knyght ooſt man good conſcyence whan ſholde dye called hȳ neuewe praynge hym yt whan deed ſhold ſelle horſe harneys almeſſe ſynge thrytty maſſes loue behyght hym well laſted hym full euyll kept ſtylle owne vſe dyd badde hym doo whan thrytty dayes paſſed y• nyght folowynge knyght apperyd ſlepe neuewe axed hym done bad hym excuſed dyuer se beſyneſſes y• fayned hadde axed eme fared anſwered ſayd ſhall telle fare thou ſhalt fare alle theſe thrytty dayes haue ben purgatorye ſuffred ful moche woo payne defaute helpe thanke god paſſed purgatorye goo vp heuens blyſſe without ende thou woldeſt helpe badde therfore daye mydmorowe thou ſhalt dye goo helle without ende next daye folowynge rode y• ooſt y• ſame horſe tolde theſe dremes felowes iape mydmorowe came ſodaynly blake ſkye thondre lyghtnynge grete nombre fendes lykeneſſe rauens rokes hent hym vp fro horſe myddes fyndeth fewe frendes caplm xij pauper rede vita barla y• ther ryche man whiche iij frendes fyrſte frende ſeconde loued herte thyrde frende loued lytell nought man felle ſuche daunger ayenſt kyng yt • good forfetted eſchetyd ye kyng hymſelfe wened haue ben ſlayn wente fyrſte frende yt loued ſoo moche praynge hym helpe yt wolde go kyng ſpeke hȳ ſaue lyfe yf myght anſwerd ſayd fare well faue knowe haue felowes frendes ynough haue myrtes ſolace natheleſſe yf thou ſlayne ſhall gyue ſhete burye went ſeconde frende loued ſoo moche praynge hym alſo helpe excuſed hym ſayd praye haue excuſed ſo beſye may atende yet olde felauſhyp ſhall go waye yate went thyrde frende loued ſo lytel prayed hym helpe ſayd leue frende aſhamed ſpeke haue ben ful vnkynde lytell loue ſhewed praye haue reuth goddes ſake fareth theſe dayes longe man welth ſo longe ſhall haue frendes ynough take may flater hym pleaſe hym yf begynne go donewarde fyndeth fewe frendes many enemyes therfore ſayth wyſe man tempore felici vnderſtande euery man yt hath rycheſſes goodes worlde fyrſte frende y• loued ſoo moche whiche gaaf hym ſhete buryed vnderſtā de worlde whiche worldely men loue ſo moche y• loue therof trauayle nyght daye put peryl bodye ſoule oft leſe ſelfe bodye ſoule yet ye laſt ende vnnethes gyueth ſhete buryed many whan dye haue leſſe nought yf haue ought yet theyr executours wyll ſaye y• haue nought yt owe haue ſeconde frende went hym yate vnderſtande mannes wyfe childern bodely frendes womannes huſbonde childern bodely frendes whiche whan ben deed ſhall go waye yate brynge theyr graue per auenture ſtande wepe man woman deed doluen vnder claye ſoone forgeten mynde paſſed awaye belle ronge maſſes ſonge ſoone forgeten vnnethes ſhall fynde one frende wyll ſynge hym one maſſe vnnethes yere thrydde frende whiche loued ſoo lytell whiche halpe hym nede vnderſtande almeſdede whiche worldely couetouſe men loue full lytyll yet dredeful dome whan ſhall ſtande barre byfore ſouerayne iuge cryſte iheſn almeſſe dede ſhall beſte frende ſhall haue ſhall ſpeke theym praye theym ſaue theym yf ſhall ſaued therfore salomon ſayth conclude elemoſmam ſinu pauperis et ipſa pro te exorabit ab omni malo eccleſiaſtici xxix therfore leue frende doo ye tobye taught ſone ex ſubſtancia tua fac elemoſinam doo almeſſe thy good thy catell nyll thou tourne awaye thy face ony poore man yu myght thou mercyable yf thou haue moche gyue thou moche yf thou haue lytell ſtudye thou gyue lytell good wyll thou treſoureſt grete gyft daye nede almeſſe delyuered ſoules euery ſynne deth ſuffered ſoule go derkeneſſe thobie iiij caplm xiij diues ſhal myn almeſſe ¶pauper doo cryſte byddeth goſpell omni petenti te tribue gyue euery nedy axeth yf yu myght luce vi ¶diues contra cryſte y• goſpell luce xiiij ſayth thus whan yu makeſt feeſt nyll yu calle therto thy frendes thy neyghbours thy coſyns ryche men calle yu poore men feble blynde halt whiche wordes ſemeth y• ſholde none almeſſe poore y• ben feble blynde lame ¶pauꝑ cryſte fordydeth men byd ther frendes ther neyghbours ryche men ye feeſt bad hē y• ſholde byd theyr frendes y• ryche alſo poore folke nedy teble alſo bad yt men ſholde byd ye ryche folke theyr frendes feeſt wt wycked emencōn hope falſe wynnynge pompe glotonye lecherye gete grete worldely name pryncypaly nouryſſhe pea charyte token yt feeſt made wt good entencōn ryche poore ben pleſaūt god cryſte called v al ryche poore y• endeleſſe feeſt cryſte hymſelf though poore manhede feble blynde ne halt whan y• phariſe ſayd tho wordes bad mete ne whan brydales mod chane galyle ne whan mary magdaleyn ſyſter martha zacheus made grete feſtes yet prayſed cryſte ther dedes fedde cryſte apoſtles dyſcyples whan went worlde prechynge techynge ben prayſed yet apoſtles dyſcyples ſtronge men neyther blynde ne lame cryſte hymſelfe fedde dyſcyples neyther blynde ne lame ſomtyme • ed foure thouſande men ſomtyme fyue thouſande folowed hym fro contre contre prechyng ſee woūdres dyd yet blynde ne lam • goſpell ſayth made hole theyr bodely ſekneſſe yt fedde luce ix et math xiiij alſo tho two dyſcyples yt toke cryſte herborowe ye lykeneſſe pylgryme • eſter daye euen ben prayſed yet neuer blynde ne lame alſo abraham loth many holy men reſceyued angel lykeneſſe worſhypfull men neyther blynde ne lame mete herborowe ſaynt peter reſceyued knyghtes worſhypfull men mete herborowe whiche came hym meſſage ye grete lorde cornely rede holy wrytt actuū x theſe ben prayſed god moche thanke god theyr almeſdede therfore ſayd fyrſt cryſte bad men ſholde almeſſe al nede frende foo apoſtle byddeth yf thyne enemye haue hongre fede hym yf haue thurſte gyue drynke charyte cryſten fayth outaketh perſone man ne woman ne ſtate ne degree ne ſecte hethen ne cryſten frō almeſdede whā nede muſt haue pyte helpe power natheleſſe muſte kepe ordre gyuynge takynge hede cauſe maner nede theym gyue almeſſe ſome poore theyr wylle ſome ayenſt theyr wyll ben poore theyr wyll ſome ben poore loue god ſome loue worlde ben poore loue god muſte holpen paſſyng theyr pouerte medefull parfyght vertuous ben poore wylfully god ye worlde romaynes theſe dayes moche folke dyſmytte theyr owne good take ther childeren make grete worlde moche folke take ſo moche hede mennes proufyte take none hede ſelfe ſo falle pouerte nede ſuche poore folke muſte pryncypaly holpen theyr goodes profyted rather helpe y• ben poore ayenſt theyr wyll ſhall put byfore poore loue god nede caplm xiiij ben poore ayenſt theyr wyll ſome ben poore fortune myſauentures fortune ſerueth theyr wyll ne god multeplyeth theyr good wolde haue leſe myſauentures dome god ſome ben poore onely ſynne loue ſynne waſte theyr good lecherye glotonye pryde pletynge myſuſe dyce ryot vanyte suche poore folke ben laſte ordre almeſſe doynge theyr nede natheleſſe yf haue pacyence theyr pouerte ſhall haue mede theyr pacyence yf repente theyr myſdedes y• ſame maner ſome ben feble blynde lame goddes cauſe goddes loue ayenſt theyr wyll courſe kynde ayenſt theyr wyl loue ſynne theues fyghters baratours whiche fyght barett leſe theyr eyen theyr foot theyr hō de ofte ben punyſſhed lawe god forbede y• ſuche poore folke poore goddes ſake ſaynt auſten ſheweth ſo y• god ſhal accept almeſſe done ben poore goddes ſake y• ben poore ayenſt theyr wyll ſynne ſake whiche concluſyon al though ſoth yet thynketh yt cryſte ſhall ſaye tho wordes almeſſe yt hath done maner poore men bothe parfyght vnparfyght ſhall yelde mede euery good dede wycked doer ſynful poore men ben called leſte goddes menye leſte ſett courte heuen therfore ſayth goſpell ſo breketh one leſt cō mau demētes techeth worde euyll example ſo breke cōmaūdementes ſhall called leſt kyngdom heuen god ſhal ſhewe dome grete pyte moche mercy thynge yt done ſake enemyes leſte ſeruaūtes mooſt vnworthy ſhal accept rewarde done owne perſone ſaye thanke ye dyde leſte myne ye dyd ¶diues ſhall calle brethern y• leſte worthye many theym almeſſe done ſhall dampned ¶pauper er ſhall gyue ſentence dampnacōn ſhall calle al men brethern lykeneſſe kynde y• man brother v lykeneſſe kynde grace ne blyſſe y• ben grace meke iuge ſhall calle al men brethern confort ſhall ſaued grete dyſconfort y• ſhall dampned whan ſhall ſee meke iuge forgete brotherhede ne lykeneſſe kynde whiche hath yet catched maner cō pelled ryghtfulneſſe dampne theym grete mater ſhall haue ſyghe ſorowe whan ſhall knowe theyr ſynnes ſo greuous ſo grete theyr vnkyndeneſſe ſoo moche ther owne brother ſo meke iuge muſte dampne ¶diues opynyon pleaſaūt ryche men ſynfull wretch y• hope holpen almeſdede many countrees ben fewe poore folke ſpyryte ne theyr wyll fewe y• forſaken worlde goddes ſake many ther worlde hath forſaken many y• ſynne ſake ben full poore many theyr myſdedes lye bounde pryſon grete pouerte hongre colde bytter paynes ſuche folke many contrees men doo mooſt comonly theyr almeſſe hope thā ked rewarded therfore att laſte dome ¶pauper ſhal thanked meded therfore ſayd fyrſte ſythen cryſte ryghtful iuge ſhal thanke men theyr almeſſe y• dyd loue enemyes wycked doer many ſuche ben moche ſhal thanke theyr almeſſe yt dyd frendes true ſeruaūt • ſythen ſhal dampned wolde gyue enemyes nede ſake moche ſooner ſhall dāpned ye wolde helpe frendes true ſeruaūtes nede ſake put themſelfe loue pouerte moche trauayle helpe mannes ſoule yf ſo pleſaūt medefull gyue almeſſe ſuche poore folke forſakynge worlde whiche many neyther ſhall reſceyued endleſſe tabnacles blyſſe neyther ſhall reſceyue blyſſe moche pleſaūt god rytorye helpe yt ben poore ſpyryte wyll loue god cryſte ſayth goſpell kyngdom heuen theyrs graunted theym reſceyue folke haue holpen endeleſſe tabernacle caplm xv therfore leue frende wytt ye wel yt yf man woman haue wyl gyue thē ben poore ayenſt theyr wyl loue ſynne gyue yt ben poore goddes ſake goddes cauſe ſynne greuouſly leſe mede theyr almeſſe put goddes enemyes byfore frendes vyce byfore vertue therfore ye ſhall releue poore nedy ye maye pryncypally y• ben nedy poore goddes ſake waye vertue yf ye leue falſe opynyon almeſſe leſſe whan ye may good maner ye leſe mede leſſe therfore ſaynt auſten ſayth thus thou ſhalt y• poore prechour goddes worde yu doſt begger paſſynge waye begger yu gyueſt cryſte byddeth yu gyue eche axeth poore prechour yu oughteſt gyue though axe therfor loke poore prechour goddes knyght nede axe yf nede axe thy defaute thy defaute thy laccheſſe ſheweth dampnable axe ryght ſayd begger ſeketh gyue yu euery man axeth ſo ſayd hym y• yu oughteſt ſeke let thyne almeſſe ſwete thyne honde tylle y• fynde hym whome yu muſte gyue gyue yu euery man y• axeth moche rather gyue goddes ſeruaūt • y• knyght cryſte though axe hec auguſtinꝰ et ponit gloſa ſuꝑ illud p̄i producens fenū iumentis therfore ſayth lawe ſo wyll gyue almeſſe men yt folowe lyfe apoſtles pouerte poore prechoures theyr nedefull vſe dampneth hymſelfe xvi q̄ aplicis apoſtle ſayth due dette y• poore prechour goddes worde lyue prechynge therfor raymūdde hoſpitalitate ordinand ſayth ſome axe almeſſe dette ſome nede ſuſteyne bodye axe almeſſe dette eyther knowen ſuche knowen ſuche yf knowen ſuche muſte nedes holpen yf knowen ſhall examyned wyſely whether ſaye grete peryll lette yf ſo gyue gooſtely thynges bodely thynges due dett ſaynt poul ſayth lawe xlij diſt quieſcamus yf axe ſuſtenaunce bodye eyther yu myght gyue ſtede tyme eyther yu myght gyue yf yu mayſt gyue yu oweſt gyue nede pretende theyr aſtate well ruled take exſample abraham loth whiche reſceyued folke indyfferently hoſpytalyte ſo reſceyued angel yf put ſome awaye peraduenture ſholde haue put awaye angeles men ſayth cryſoſtom ſuꝑ eplam ad hebre therfore ſayth god ſhal yelde thy mede good lyfe whiche yu reſceyueſt thy good wyll worſhyp y• yu doſt goddes ſake thy mercy thy goodneſſe therfore lawe ſayth yt men ought gyue theyr almeſſe curſed folke ſynfull folke neuer ſo wycked xi q̄ iij qm̄ multos et di lxxxvi paſce • nō ſatis fine worſe yt ben ſyker theyr lyuelode ſaynt auſten ſayth yf ſynner y• worſe mennes almeſſe better withdrawe gyue hym v q̄ v nō • ni natheleſſe yf vtter nede muſte holpen di lxxxvi paſce caplm xvi caſe whan yu mygh helpe thou muſte take hede ten thynges fayth cauſe place tyme maner nede nygheneſſe bloode affynyte age febleneſſe nobley fyr c take hede fayth caas thou ſhalt put cryſten man byfore hethen man alſo take hede cauſe nede whether come nede goddes cauſe cauſe ſynne take hede alſo y• place whan y• ryght full man tourmented pryſon dette helpe hym yf thou may ſythen boūde helpe yf may moche boūden helpe ryghtfull man woman alſo take hede tyme yf gete thynge tyme trybulacyon tyme peryll whan led deth vnryghtfully yu ſetteſt thy moneye thou dooſt lyfe lyght ſynne alſo take hede maner gyuynge yu gyue ſoo one daye thou may gyue daye ſo one yu may gyue thou wylt forſake worlde one goddes ſake perfeccōn alſo take hede nede gyue haue nede alſo take hede nygheneſſe bloode affynyte waye kynde muſte holpen rather ſtraungers yf nede euen alſo take hede age olde folke muſte put byfore yonge folke alſo take hede febleneſſe blynde lame feble folke muſt holpen rather hole folke euen nede alſo take hede ye nobley perſone namely yt wt ſynne ben fallen pouerte myſcheef comonly ſuche ben ſhamefaſte axe diſt lxxxvi non latis et eadem dicit ambro li de officijs vnde vſus cauſa fidem tempus ſanguis holyneſſe profytableneſſe nyghenes perſone y• nedeth helpe holyer man hym y• hath ben profytable comonte yf nede thou ſhalt gyue rather better perſone nyghe kynne affynyte ſo holy ne ſo profytable yu whan ſholde entre y• londe byheſte moyſes forbad fyrſte couety se fleſſhe putteth byfore rede deut• v cauſe dyuerſyte ¶pauꝑ whan god gaf y• lawe moūt synay deſert grete myſcheef therfore enclyned begynnynge vnto endynge token yt man woman youth begynnynge ſooner tempted couetyſe eye worldely good couetyſe fleſſhe endynge age latter tempted couetyſe eye worldely good couetyſe fleſſhe olde folke cloſed herſelf houſe wolde neuer ſee man ne come yt houſe toke lyuynge ſmalle wyked men axed ſhe dyde ſo ſhe ſaye ſhe hadde leuer ſhytte herſelfe quyck graue harme ony ſoule god made lykeneſſe bought ſoo dere precyous blood rede alſo lyfe ſaynt bryde yt man wolde haue wedded beaute ſhe prayed god wolde ſen ſome blemyſſhynge face wherby mannes temptacyon myght ceſe anone one eye braſte hede knyght dooth horſe yf y• horſe proude euyl tached may lyghtly leſe mayſter becau se deth yf tame mayſter well tached ſhall hym worſhyp helpe nede caſe ſaue lyfe thre thynges ben nedeful knyght rule wel horſe muſte haue brydel ſadel two ſpores brydel vnder stande abſtynence trauayle whiche fleſſhe muſte refrayned fro luſtes euyll tacches whan begynneth wexe proude wynſynge kykyng ayenſt mayſter poſſidebi •• aīas vrās ye ſhall kepe ſoules pacyence ſadell maketh horſe ſemely pleſaūt ſyght ſo pacyence maketh man pleſaūt ſyght god men maketh haue loue euery cō pany ben wrath inpacyence haſtynes maketh mā vnpleſaūt without loue ſadel god ſpake caym whan wroth wt brother abel ſayd god art yu wroth thy face thy ſo fallen fallen ſadell pacyence yf yu well yu ſhalt reſceyue good mede yf yu euyll anone thy ſynne cometh y• yate punyſſhed deſyre ſynne ſhal vnder thy power horſe vnder knyght thou ſhalt lorde therof yf thou wylt gen̄ iiij caym myſgouernaūce hors felle ſadel pacyence frendes none aduerſyte trybula cyon ſekeneſſe vnſadel pacyence ſytte ye faſt iob dyd ſaye ye ſayd whan hadde loſte good childern ſlayne hymſelfe ſmyten harde ſekeneſſe horryble foule ſayd thus yf haue dartes y• wycked fende take ye y• baſyn̄et helth ſwerde holy gooſt goddes worde whiche ſayth another place ſharper ony two egged ſwerde ad hebre iiij almaner prayer beſechynge praye ye euery tyme alwaye ſpiryte wake ye alwaye maner beſyneſſe thus ſaynt poule lykeneſſe bodely armure techeth v gooſtly armure techeth v well arme lendes vertue chaſtyte whan byddeth v gyrde well lendes byddeth v habergeon ryghtfulneſſe defence bodye ſoule y• ryght yelde god euery creature yt longeth hym ſoueraynes felowes ſugettes theym ben byfore v paſte worlde almeſſe gyuynge yeldynge dettes ben deed theym ben behynde v come ſauynge theyr ryght theyr due herytage thus arme v behynde byfore euery ſyde habergeon ryghtfulneſſe ryght habergeon euery rynge accordeth wt knytt ſholde ryghtfulnes accorde gydre ſo knytt gydre yt ryght ſoo yt man ne woman wronge yf ſo moche ryght fauour one hyndrynge others ryght y• rynges haberge • ryghtfulnes accorde ne well knytt gydre ther hole wherby fende may hurte euery cryſten man woman ought haue goſtly pouerte whiche cryſt taught goſpell forther goſpell cryſte goſpell pea wyll dede power teche yf yf helpe forther yt techynge goſpell goddes lawe helpe thē good theyr nedefull ſuſtenaunce yf may haue nede alſo byddeth v take v ſhelde fayth ſhelde tryangle hath thre corner whiche tryangle yf fro y• myddes drawen thre lynes thre corner ther ſholde thre tryangles whiche thre one tryangle yet none therfore ſayth fayth holy trynyte lykened ſhelde ther ben thre perſones y• holy trynyte fader ſone holy gooſt eche god none theym ether though ben al thre wylt kepe lawes amende ſhall lede thy kynge y• yu ſhalt make vpon pryſoners ferre contree yu neuer knewe ne thy faders byfore theſe curſes many mo therto whiche wryten ſame place ſhall take purſue
